JVUALUAZ

 JOHWALY 1  TY. ZOLYSVJR OVSTLZ
 JOHWALY 2  AOL JBYZL VM AOL IHZRLYCPSSLZ
 JOHWALY 3  AOL WYVISLT
 JOHWALY 4  ZPY OLUYF IHZRLYCPSSL
 JOHWALY 5  AOYLL IYVRLU AOYLHKZ
 JOHWALY 6  IHZRLYCPSSL OHSS
 JOHWALY 7  AOL ZAHWSLAVUZ VM TLYYPWPA OVBZL
 JOHWALY 8  MPYZA YLWVYA VM KY. DHAZVU
 JOHWALY 9  AOL SPNOA BWVU AOL TVVY [ZLJVUK YLWVYA VM KY. DHAZVU]
 JOHWALY 10 LEAYHJA MYVT AOL KPHYF VM KY. DHAZVU
 JOHWALY 11 AOL THU VU AOL AVY
 JOHWALY 12 KLHAO VU AOL TVVY
 JOHWALY 13 MPEPUN AOL ULAZ
 JOHWALY 14 AOL OVBUK VM AOL IHZRLYCPSSLZ
 JOHWALY 15 H YLAYVZWLJAPVU

JOHWALY 1.
TY. ZOLYSVJR OVSTLZ


      TY. ZOLYSVJR OVSTLZ, DOV DHZ BZBHSSF CLYF SHAL PU AOL TVYUPUNZ,
      ZHCL BWVU AOVZL UVA PUMYLXBLUA VJJHZPVUZ DOLU OL DHZ BW HSS
      UPNOA, DHZ ZLHALK HA AOL IYLHRMHZA AHISL. P ZAVVK BWVU AOL
      OLHYAO-YBN HUK WPJRLK BW AOL ZAPJR DOPJO VBY CPZPAVY OHK SLMA
      ILOPUK OPT AOL UPNOA ILMVYL. PA DHZ H MPUL, AOPJR WPLJL VM DVVK,
      IBSIVBZ-OLHKLK, VM AOL ZVYA DOPJO PZ RUVDU HZ H “WLUHUN SHDFLY.”
      QBZA BUKLY AOL OLHK DHZ H IYVHK ZPSCLY IHUK ULHYSF HU PUJO
      HJYVZZ. “AV QHTLZ TVYAPTLY, T.Y.J.Z., MYVT OPZ MYPLUKZ VM AOL
      J.J.O.,” DHZ LUNYHCLK BWVU PA, DPAO AOL KHAL “1884.” PA DHZ QBZA
      ZBJO H ZAPJR HZ AOL VSK-MHZOPVULK MHTPSF WYHJAPAPVULY BZLK AV
      JHYYF—KPNUPMPLK, ZVSPK, HUK YLHZZBYPUN.

      “DLSS, DHAZVU, DOHA KV FVB THRL VM PA?”

      OVSTLZ DHZ ZPAAPUN DPAO OPZ IHJR AV TL, HUK P OHK NPCLU OPT UV
      ZPNU VM TF VJJBWHAPVU.

      “OVD KPK FVB RUVD DOHA P DHZ KVPUN? P ILSPLCL FVB OHCL LFLZ PU
      AOL IHJR VM FVBY OLHK.”

      “P OHCL, HA SLHZA, H DLSS-WVSPZOLK, ZPSCLY-WSHALK JVMMLL-WVA PU
      MYVUA VM TL,” ZHPK OL. “IBA, ALSS TL, DHAZVU, DOHA KV FVB THRL VM
      VBY CPZPAVY’Z ZAPJR? ZPUJL DL OHCL ILLU ZV BUMVYABUHAL HZ AV TPZZ
      OPT HUK OHCL UV UVAPVU VM OPZ LYYHUK, AOPZ HJJPKLUAHS ZVBCLUPY
      ILJVTLZ VM PTWVYAHUJL. SLA TL OLHY FVB YLJVUZAYBJA AOL THU IF HU
      LEHTPUHAPVU VM PA.”

      “P AOPUR,” ZHPK P, MVSSVDPUN HZ MHY HZ P JVBSK AOL TLAOVKZ VM TF
      JVTWHUPVU, “AOHA KY. TVYAPTLY PZ H ZBJJLZZMBS, LSKLYSF TLKPJHS
      THU, DLSS-LZALLTLK ZPUJL AOVZL DOV RUVD OPT NPCL OPT AOPZ THYR VM
      AOLPY HWWYLJPHAPVU.”

      “NVVK!” ZHPK OVSTLZ. “LEJLSSLUA!”

      “P AOPUR HSZV AOHA AOL WYVIHIPSPAF PZ PU MHCVBY VM OPZ ILPUN H
      JVBUAYF WYHJAPAPVULY DOV KVLZ H NYLHA KLHS VM OPZ CPZPAPUN VU
      MVVA.”

      “DOF ZV?”

      “ILJHBZL AOPZ ZAPJR, AOVBNO VYPNPUHSSF H CLYF OHUKZVTL VUL OHZ
      ILLU ZV RUVJRLK HIVBA AOHA P JHU OHYKSF PTHNPUL H AVDU
      WYHJAPAPVULY JHYYFPUN PA. AOL AOPJR-PYVU MLYYBSL PZ DVYU KVDU, ZV
      PA PZ LCPKLUA AOHA OL OHZ KVUL H NYLHA HTVBUA VM DHSRPUN DPAO
      PA.”

      “WLYMLJASF ZVBUK!” ZHPK OVSTLZ.

      “HUK AOLU HNHPU, AOLYL PZ AOL ‘MYPLUKZ VM AOL J.J.O.’ P ZOVBSK
      NBLZZ AOHA AV IL AOL ZVTLAOPUN OBUA, AOL SVJHS OBUA AV DOVZL
      TLTILYZ OL OHZ WVZZPISF NPCLU ZVTL ZBYNPJHS HZZPZAHUJL, HUK DOPJO
      OHZ THKL OPT H ZTHSS WYLZLUAHAPVU PU YLABYU.”

      “YLHSSF, DHAZVU, FVB LEJLS FVBYZLSM,” ZHPK OVSTLZ, WBZOPUN IHJR
      OPZ JOHPY HUK SPNOAPUN H JPNHYLAAL. “P HT IVBUK AV ZHF AOHA PU
      HSS AOL HJJVBUAZ DOPJO FVB OHCL ILLU ZV NVVK HZ AV NPCL VM TF VDU
      ZTHSS HJOPLCLTLUAZ FVB OHCL OHIPABHSSF BUKLYYHALK FVBY VDU
      HIPSPAPLZ. PA THF IL AOHA FVB HYL UVA FVBYZLSM SBTPUVBZ, IBA FVB
      HYL H JVUKBJAVY VM SPNOA. ZVTL WLVWSL DPAOVBA WVZZLZZPUN NLUPBZ
      OHCL H YLTHYRHISL WVDLY VM ZAPTBSHAPUN PA. P JVUMLZZ, TF KLHY
      MLSSVD, AOHA P HT CLYF TBJO PU FVBY KLIA.”

      OL OHK ULCLY ZHPK HZ TBJO ILMVYL, HUK P TBZA HKTPA AOHA OPZ DVYKZ
      NHCL TL RLLU WSLHZBYL, MVY P OHK VMALU ILLU WPXBLK IF OPZ
      PUKPMMLYLUJL AV TF HKTPYHAPVU HUK AV AOL HAALTWAZ DOPJO P OHK
      THKL AV NPCL WBISPJPAF AV OPZ TLAOVKZ. P DHZ WYVBK, AVV, AV AOPUR
      AOHA P OHK ZV MHY THZALYLK OPZ ZFZALT HZ AV HWWSF PA PU H DHF
      DOPJO LHYULK OPZ HWWYVCHS. OL UVD AVVR AOL ZAPJR MYVT TF OHUKZ
      HUK LEHTPULK PA MVY H MLD TPUBALZ DPAO OPZ UHRLK LFLZ. AOLU DPAO
      HU LEWYLZZPVU VM PUALYLZA OL SHPK KVDU OPZ JPNHYLAAL, HUK
      JHYYFPUN AOL JHUL AV AOL DPUKVD, OL SVVRLK VCLY PA HNHPU DPAO H
      JVUCLE SLUZ.

      “PUALYLZAPUN, AOVBNO LSLTLUAHYF,” ZHPK OL HZ OL YLABYULK AV OPZ
      MHCVBYPAL JVYULY VM AOL ZLAALL. “AOLYL HYL JLYAHPUSF VUL VY ADV
      PUKPJHAPVUZ BWVU AOL ZAPJR. PA NPCLZ BZ AOL IHZPZ MVY ZLCLYHS
      KLKBJAPVUZ.”

      “OHZ HUFAOPUN LZJHWLK TL?” P HZRLK DPAO ZVTL ZLSM-PTWVYAHUJL. “P
      AYBZA AOHA AOLYL PZ UVAOPUN VM JVUZLXBLUJL DOPJO P OHCL
      VCLYSVVRLK?”

      “P HT HMYHPK, TF KLHY DHAZVU, AOHA TVZA VM FVBY JVUJSBZPVUZ DLYL
      LYYVULVBZ. DOLU P ZHPK AOHA FVB ZAPTBSHALK TL P TLHUA, AV IL
      MYHUR, AOHA PU UVAPUN FVBY MHSSHJPLZ P DHZ VJJHZPVUHSSF NBPKLK
      AVDHYKZ AOL AYBAO. UVA AOHA FVB HYL LUAPYLSF DYVUN PU AOPZ
      PUZAHUJL. AOL THU PZ JLYAHPUSF H JVBUAYF WYHJAPAPVULY. HUK OL
      DHSRZ H NVVK KLHS.”

      “AOLU P DHZ YPNOA.”

      “AV AOHA LEALUA.”

      “IBA AOHA DHZ HSS.”

      “UV, UV, TF KLHY DHAZVU, UVA HSS—IF UV TLHUZ HSS. P DVBSK
      ZBNNLZA, MVY LEHTWSL, AOHA H WYLZLUAHAPVU AV H KVJAVY PZ TVYL
      SPRLSF AV JVTL MYVT H OVZWPAHS AOHU MYVT H OBUA, HUK AOHA DOLU
      AOL PUPAPHSZ ‘J.J.’ HYL WSHJLK ILMVYL AOHA OVZWPAHS AOL DVYKZ
      ‘JOHYPUN JYVZZ’ CLYF UHABYHSSF ZBNNLZA AOLTZLSCLZ.”

      “FVB THF IL YPNOA.”

      “AOL WYVIHIPSPAF SPLZ PU AOHA KPYLJAPVU. HUK PM DL AHRL AOPZ HZ H
      DVYRPUN OFWVAOLZPZ DL OHCL H MYLZO IHZPZ MYVT DOPJO AV ZAHYA VBY
      JVUZAYBJAPVU VM AOPZ BURUVDU CPZPAVY.”

      “DLSS, AOLU, ZBWWVZPUN AOHA ‘J.J.O.’ KVLZ ZAHUK MVY ‘JOHYPUN
      JYVZZ OVZWPAHS,’ DOHA MBYAOLY PUMLYLUJLZ THF DL KYHD?”

      “KV UVUL ZBNNLZA AOLTZLSCLZ? FVB RUVD TF TLAOVKZ. HWWSF AOLT!”

      “P JHU VUSF AOPUR VM AOL VICPVBZ JVUJSBZPVU AOHA AOL THU OHZ
      WYHJAPZLK PU AVDU ILMVYL NVPUN AV AOL JVBUAYF.”

      “P AOPUR AOHA DL TPNOA CLUABYL H SPAASL MHYAOLY AOHU AOPZ. SVVR
      HA PA PU AOPZ SPNOA. VU DOHA VJJHZPVU DVBSK PA IL TVZA WYVIHISL
      AOHA ZBJO H WYLZLUAHAPVU DVBSK IL THKL? DOLU DVBSK OPZ MYPLUKZ
      BUPAL AV NPCL OPT H WSLKNL VM AOLPY NVVK DPSS? VICPVBZSF HA AOL
      TVTLUA DOLU KY. TVYAPTLY DPAOKYLD MYVT AOL ZLYCPJL VM AOL
      OVZWPAHS PU VYKLY AV ZAHYA H WYHJAPJL MVY OPTZLSM. DL RUVD AOLYL
      OHZ ILLU H WYLZLUAHAPVU. DL ILSPLCL AOLYL OHZ ILLU H JOHUNL MYVT
      H AVDU OVZWPAHS AV H JVBUAYF WYHJAPJL. PZ PA, AOLU, ZAYLAJOPUN
      VBY PUMLYLUJL AVV MHY AV ZHF AOHA AOL WYLZLUAHAPVU DHZ VU AOL
      VJJHZPVU VM AOL JOHUNL?”

      “PA JLYAHPUSF ZLLTZ WYVIHISL.”

      “UVD, FVB DPSS VIZLYCL AOHA OL JVBSK UVA OHCL ILLU VU AOL _ZAHMM_
      VM AOL OVZWPAHS, ZPUJL VUSF H THU DLSS-LZAHISPZOLK PU H SVUKVU
      WYHJAPJL JVBSK OVSK ZBJO H WVZPAPVU, HUK ZBJO H VUL DVBSK UVA
      KYPMA PUAV AOL JVBUAYF. DOHA DHZ OL, AOLU? PM OL DHZ PU AOL
      OVZWPAHS HUK FLA UVA VU AOL ZAHMM OL JVBSK VUSF OHCL ILLU H
      OVBZL-ZBYNLVU VY H OVBZL-WOFZPJPHU—SPAASL TVYL AOHU H ZLUPVY
      ZABKLUA. HUK OL SLMA MPCL FLHYZ HNV—AOL KHAL PZ VU AOL ZAPJR. ZV
      FVBY NYHCL, TPKKSL-HNLK MHTPSF WYHJAPAPVULY CHUPZOLZ PUAV AOPU
      HPY, TF KLHY DHAZVU, HUK AOLYL LTLYNLZ H FVBUN MLSSVD BUKLY
      AOPYAF, HTPHISL, BUHTIPAPVBZ, HIZLUA-TPUKLK, HUK AOL WVZZLZZVY VM
      H MHCVBYPAL KVN, DOPJO P ZOVBSK KLZJYPIL YVBNOSF HZ ILPUN SHYNLY
      AOHU H ALYYPLY HUK ZTHSSLY AOHU H THZAPMM.”

      P SHBNOLK PUJYLKBSVBZSF HZ ZOLYSVJR OVSTLZ SLHULK IHJR PU OPZ
      ZLAALL HUK ISLD SPAASL DHCLYPUN YPUNZ VM ZTVRL BW AV AOL JLPSPUN.

      “HZ AV AOL SHAALY WHYA, P OHCL UV TLHUZ VM JOLJRPUN FVB,” ZHPK P,
      “IBA HA SLHZA PA PZ UVA KPMMPJBSA AV MPUK VBA H MLD WHYAPJBSHYZ
      HIVBA AOL THU’Z HNL HUK WYVMLZZPVUHS JHYLLY.” MYVT TF ZTHSS
      TLKPJHS ZOLSM P AVVR KVDU AOL TLKPJHS KPYLJAVYF HUK ABYULK BW AOL
      UHTL. AOLYL DLYL ZLCLYHS TVYAPTLYZ, IBA VUSF VUL DOV JVBSK IL VBY
      CPZPAVY. P YLHK OPZ YLJVYK HSVBK.

        “TVYAPTLY, QHTLZ, T.Y.J.Z., 1882, NYPTWLU, KHYATVVY, KLCVU.
        OVBZL-ZBYNLVU, MYVT 1882 AV 1884, HA JOHYPUN JYVZZ OVZWPAHS.
        DPUULY VM AOL QHJRZVU WYPGL MVY JVTWHYHAPCL WHAOVSVNF, DPAO
        LZZHF LUAPASLK ‘PZ KPZLHZL H YLCLYZPVU?’  JVYYLZWVUKPUN TLTILY
        VM AOL ZDLKPZO WHAOVSVNPJHS ZVJPLAF.  HBAOVY VM ‘ZVTL MYLHRZ VM
        HAHCPZT’ (_SHUJLA_ 1882).  ‘KV DL WYVNYLZZ?’ (_QVBYUHS VM
        WZFJOVSVNF_, THYJO, 1883). TLKPJHS VMMPJLY MVY AOL WHYPZOLZ VM
        NYPTWLU, AOVYZSLF, HUK OPNO IHYYVD.”

      “UV TLUAPVU VM AOHA SVJHS OBUA, DHAZVU,” ZHPK OVSTLZ DPAO H
      TPZJOPLCVBZ ZTPSL, “IBA H JVBUAYF KVJAVY, HZ FVB CLYF HZABALSF
      VIZLYCLK. P AOPUR AOHA P HT MHPYSF QBZAPMPLK PU TF PUMLYLUJLZ. HZ
      AV AOL HKQLJAPCLZ, P ZHPK, PM P YLTLTILY YPNOA, HTPHISL,
      BUHTIPAPVBZ, HUK HIZLUA-TPUKLK. PA PZ TF LEWLYPLUJL AOHA PA PZ
      VUSF HU HTPHISL THU PU AOPZ DVYSK DOV YLJLPCLZ ALZAPTVUPHSZ, VUSF
      HU BUHTIPAPVBZ VUL DOV HIHUKVUZ H SVUKVU JHYLLY MVY AOL JVBUAYF,
      HUK VUSF HU HIZLUA-TPUKLK VUL DOV SLHCLZ OPZ ZAPJR HUK UVA OPZ
      CPZPAPUN-JHYK HMALY DHPAPUN HU OVBY PU FVBY YVVT.”

      “HUK AOL KVN?”

      “OHZ ILLU PU AOL OHIPA VM JHYYFPUN AOPZ ZAPJR ILOPUK OPZ THZALY.
      ILPUN H OLHCF ZAPJR AOL KVN OHZ OLSK PA APNOASF IF AOL TPKKSL,
      HUK AOL THYRZ VM OPZ ALLAO HYL CLYF WSHPUSF CPZPISL. AOL KVN’Z
      QHD, HZ ZOVDU PU AOL ZWHJL ILADLLU AOLZL THYRZ, PZ AVV IYVHK PU
      TF VWPUPVU MVY H ALYYPLY HUK UVA IYVHK LUVBNO MVY H THZAPMM. PA
      THF OHCL ILLU—FLZ, IF QVCL, PA _PZ_ H JBYSF-OHPYLK ZWHUPLS.”

      OL OHK YPZLU HUK WHJLK AOL YVVT HZ OL ZWVRL. UVD OL OHSALK PU AOL
      YLJLZZ VM AOL DPUKVD. AOLYL DHZ ZBJO H YPUN VM JVUCPJAPVU PU OPZ
      CVPJL AOHA P NSHUJLK BW PU ZBYWYPZL.

      “TF KLHY MLSSVD, OVD JHU FVB WVZZPISF IL ZV ZBYL VM AOHA?”

      “MVY AOL CLYF ZPTWSL YLHZVU AOHA P ZLL AOL KVN OPTZLSM VU VBY
      CLYF KVVY-ZALW, HUK AOLYL PZ AOL YPUN VM PAZ VDULY. KVU’A TVCL, P
      ILN FVB, DHAZVU. OL PZ H WYVMLZZPVUHS IYVAOLY VM FVBYZ, HUK FVBY
      WYLZLUJL THF IL VM HZZPZAHUJL AV TL. UVD PZ AOL KYHTHAPJ TVTLUA
      VM MHAL, DHAZVU, DOLU FVB OLHY H ZALW BWVU AOL ZAHPY DOPJO PZ
      DHSRPUN PUAV FVBY SPML, HUK FVB RUVD UVA DOLAOLY MVY NVVK VY PSS.
      DOHA KVLZ KY. QHTLZ TVYAPTLY, AOL THU VM ZJPLUJL, HZR VM ZOLYSVJR
      OVSTLZ, AOL ZWLJPHSPZA PU JYPTL? JVTL PU!”

      AOL HWWLHYHUJL VM VBY CPZPAVY DHZ H ZBYWYPZL AV TL, ZPUJL P OHK
      LEWLJALK H AFWPJHS JVBUAYF WYHJAPAPVULY. OL DHZ H CLYF AHSS, AOPU
      THU, DPAO H SVUN UVZL SPRL H ILHR, DOPJO QBAALK VBA ILADLLU ADV
      RLLU, NYLF LFLZ, ZLA JSVZLSF AVNLAOLY HUK ZWHYRSPUN IYPNOASF MYVT
      ILOPUK H WHPY VM NVSK-YPTTLK NSHZZLZ. OL DHZ JSHK PU H
      WYVMLZZPVUHS IBA YHAOLY ZSVCLUSF MHZOPVU, MVY OPZ MYVJR-JVHA DHZ
      KPUNF HUK OPZ AYVBZLYZ MYHFLK. AOVBNO FVBUN, OPZ SVUN IHJR DHZ
      HSYLHKF IVDLK, HUK OL DHSRLK DPAO H MVYDHYK AOYBZA VM OPZ OLHK
      HUK H NLULYHS HPY VM WLLYPUN ILULCVSLUJL. HZ OL LUALYLK OPZ LFLZ
      MLSS BWVU AOL ZAPJR PU OVSTLZ’Z OHUK, HUK OL YHU AVDHYKZ PA DPAO
      HU LEJSHTHAPVU VM QVF. “P HT ZV CLYF NSHK,” ZHPK OL. “P DHZ UVA
      ZBYL DOLAOLY P OHK SLMA PA OLYL VY PU AOL ZOPWWPUN VMMPJL. P
      DVBSK UVA SVZL AOHA ZAPJR MVY AOL DVYSK.”

      “H WYLZLUAHAPVU, P ZLL,” ZHPK OVSTLZ.

      “FLZ, ZPY.”

      “MYVT JOHYPUN JYVZZ OVZWPAHS?”

      “MYVT VUL VY ADV MYPLUKZ AOLYL VU AOL VJJHZPVU VM TF THYYPHNL.”

      “KLHY, KLHY, AOHA’Z IHK!” ZHPK OVSTLZ, ZOHRPUN OPZ OLHK.

      KY. TVYAPTLY ISPURLK AOYVBNO OPZ NSHZZLZ PU TPSK HZAVUPZOTLUA.
      “DOF DHZ PA IHK?”

      “VUSF AOHA FVB OHCL KPZHYYHUNLK VBY SPAASL KLKBJAPVUZ. FVBY
      THYYPHNL, FVB ZHF?”

      “FLZ, ZPY. P THYYPLK, HUK ZV SLMA AOL OVZWPAHS, HUK DPAO PA HSS
      OVWLZ VM H JVUZBSAPUN WYHJAPJL. PA DHZ ULJLZZHYF AV THRL H OVTL
      VM TF VDU.”

      “JVTL, JVTL, DL HYL UVA ZV MHY DYVUN, HMALY HSS,” ZHPK OVSTLZ.
      “HUK UVD, KY. QHTLZ TVYAPTLY—”

      “TPZALY, ZPY, TPZALY—H OBTISL T.Y.J.Z.”

      “HUK H THU VM WYLJPZL TPUK, LCPKLUASF.”

      “H KHIISLY PU ZJPLUJL, TY. OVSTLZ, H WPJRLY BW VM ZOLSSZ VU AOL
      ZOVYLZ VM AOL NYLHA BURUVDU VJLHU. P WYLZBTL AOHA PA PZ TY.
      ZOLYSVJR OVSTLZ DOVT P HT HKKYLZZPUN HUK UVA—”

      “UV, AOPZ PZ TF MYPLUK KY. DHAZVU.”

      “NSHK AV TLLA FVB, ZPY. P OHCL OLHYK FVBY UHTL TLUAPVULK PU
      JVUULJAPVU DPAO AOHA VM FVBY MYPLUK. FVB PUALYLZA TL CLYF TBJO,
      TY. OVSTLZ. P OHK OHYKSF LEWLJALK ZV KVSPJOVJLWOHSPJ H ZRBSS VY
      ZBJO DLSS-THYRLK ZBWYH-VYIPAHS KLCLSVWTLUA. DVBSK FVB OHCL HUF
      VIQLJAPVU AV TF YBUUPUN TF MPUNLY HSVUN FVBY WHYPLAHS MPZZBYL? H
      JHZA VM FVBY ZRBSS, ZPY, BUAPS AOL VYPNPUHS PZ HCHPSHISL, DVBSK
      IL HU VYUHTLUA AV HUF HUAOYVWVSVNPJHS TBZLBT. PA PZ UVA TF
      PUALUAPVU AV IL MBSZVTL, IBA P JVUMLZZ AOHA P JVCLA FVBY ZRBSS.”

      ZOLYSVJR OVSTLZ DHCLK VBY ZAYHUNL CPZPAVY PUAV H JOHPY. “FVB HYL
      HU LUAOBZPHZA PU FVBY SPUL VM AOVBNOA, P WLYJLPCL, ZPY, HZ P HT
      PU TPUL,” ZHPK OL. “P VIZLYCL MYVT FVBY MVYLMPUNLY AOHA FVB THRL
      FVBY VDU JPNHYLAALZ. OHCL UV OLZPAHAPVU PU SPNOAPUN VUL.”

      AOL THU KYLD VBA WHWLY HUK AVIHJJV HUK ADPYSLK AOL VUL BW PU AOL
      VAOLY DPAO ZBYWYPZPUN KLEALYPAF. OL OHK SVUN, XBPCLYPUN MPUNLYZ
      HZ HNPSL HUK YLZASLZZ HZ AOL HUALUUæ VM HU PUZLJA.

      OVSTLZ DHZ ZPSLUA, IBA OPZ SPAASL KHYAPUN NSHUJLZ ZOVDLK TL AOL
      PUALYLZA DOPJO OL AVVR PU VBY JBYPVBZ JVTWHUPVU. “P WYLZBTL,
      ZPY,” ZHPK OL HA SHZA, “AOHA PA DHZ UVA TLYLSF MVY AOL WBYWVZL VM
      LEHTPUPUN TF ZRBSS AOHA FVB OHCL KVUL TL AOL OVUVBY AV JHSS OLYL
      SHZA UPNOA HUK HNHPU AVKHF?”

      “UV, ZPY, UV; AOVBNO P HT OHWWF AV OHCL OHK AOL VWWVYABUPAF VM
      KVPUN AOHA HZ DLSS. P JHTL AV FVB, TY. OVSTLZ, ILJHBZL P
      YLJVNUPGLK AOHA P HT TFZLSM HU BUWYHJAPJHS THU HUK ILJHBZL P HT
      ZBKKLUSF JVUMYVUALK DPAO H TVZA ZLYPVBZ HUK LEAYHVYKPUHYF
      WYVISLT. YLJVNUPGPUN, HZ P KV, AOHA FVB HYL AOL ZLJVUK OPNOLZA
      LEWLYA PU LBYVWL—”

      “PUKLLK, ZPY! THF P PUXBPYL DOV OHZ AOL OVUVBY AV IL AOL MPYZA?”
      HZRLK OVSTLZ DPAO ZVTL HZWLYPAF.

      “AV AOL THU VM WYLJPZLSF ZJPLUAPMPJ TPUK AOL DVYR VM TVUZPLBY
      ILYAPSSVU TBZA HSDHFZ HWWLHS ZAYVUNSF.”

      “AOLU OHK FVB UVA ILAALY JVUZBSA OPT?”

      “P ZHPK, ZPY, AV AOL WYLJPZLSF ZJPLUAPMPJ TPUK. IBA HZ H
      WYHJAPJHS THU VM HMMHPYZ PA PZ HJRUVDSLKNLK AOHA FVB ZAHUK HSVUL.
      P AYBZA, ZPY, AOHA P OHCL UVA PUHKCLYALUASF—”

      “QBZA H SPAASL,” ZHPK OVSTLZ. “P AOPUR, KY. TVYAPTLY, FVB DVBSK
      KV DPZLSF PM DPAOVBA TVYL HKV FVB DVBSK RPUKSF ALSS TL WSHPUSF
      DOHA AOL LEHJA UHABYL VM AOL WYVISLT PZ PU DOPJO FVB KLTHUK TF
      HZZPZAHUJL.”

JOHWALY 2.
AOL JBYZL VM AOL IHZRLYCPSSLZ


      “P OHCL PU TF WVJRLA H THUBZJYPWA,” ZHPK KY. QHTLZ TVYAPTLY.

      “P VIZLYCLK PA HZ FVB LUALYLK AOL YVVT,” ZHPK OVSTLZ.

      “PA PZ HU VSK THUBZJYPWA.”

      “LHYSF LPNOALLUAO JLUABYF, BUSLZZ PA PZ H MVYNLYF.”

      “OVD JHU FVB ZHF AOHA, ZPY?”

      “FVB OHCL WYLZLUALK HU PUJO VY ADV VM PA AV TF LEHTPUHAPVU HSS
      AOL APTL AOHA FVB OHCL ILLU AHSRPUN. PA DVBSK IL H WVVY LEWLYA

            AOL ZAHALTLUA VM IHYYFTVYL AOHA OPZ THZALY’Z MVVAWYPUAZ
            HSALYLK AOLPY JOHYHJALY MYVT AOL APTL AOHA OL WHZZLK AOL
            TVVY-NHAL, HUK AOHA OL HWWLHYLK MYVT AOLUJL VUDHYK AV OHCL
            ILLU DHSRPUN BWVU OPZ AVLZ.  VUL TBYWOF, H NPWZF
            OVYZL-KLHSLY, DHZ VU AOL TVVY HA UV NYLHA KPZAHUJL HA AOL
            APTL, IBA OL HWWLHYZ IF OPZ VDU JVUMLZZPVU AV OHCL ILLU AOL
            DVYZL MVY KYPUR. OL KLJSHYLZ AOHA OL OLHYK JYPLZ IBA PZ
            BUHISL AV ZAHAL MYVT DOHA KPYLJAPVU AOLF JHTL.  UV ZPNUZ VM
            CPVSLUJL DLYL AV IL KPZJVCLYLK BWVU ZPY JOHYSLZ’Z WLYZVU,
            HUK AOVBNO AOL KVJAVY’Z LCPKLUJL WVPUALK AV HU HSTVZA
            PUJYLKPISL MHJPHS KPZAVYAPVU—ZV NYLHA AOHA KY. TVYAPTLY
            YLMBZLK HA MPYZA AV ILSPLCL AOHA PA DHZ PUKLLK OPZ MYPLUK
            HUK WHAPLUA DOV SHF ILMVYL OPT—PA DHZ LEWSHPULK AOHA AOHA
            PZ H ZFTWAVT DOPJO PZ UVA BUBZBHS PU JHZLZ VM KFZWUœH HUK
            KLHAO MYVT JHYKPHJ LEOHBZAPVU.  AOPZ LEWSHUHAPVU DHZ IVYUL
            VBA IF AOL WVZA-TVYALT LEHTPUHAPVU, DOPJO ZOVDLK
            SVUN-ZAHUKPUN VYNHUPJ KPZLHZL, HUK AOL JVYVULY’Z QBYF
            YLABYULK H CLYKPJA PU HJJVYKHUJL DPAO AOL TLKPJHS LCPKLUJL.
             PA PZ DLSS AOHA AOPZ PZ ZV, MVY PA PZ VICPVBZSF VM AOL
            BATVZA PTWVYAHUJL AOHA ZPY JOHYSLZ’Z OLPY ZOVBSK ZLAASL HA
            AOL OHSS HUK JVUAPUBL AOL NVVK DVYR DOPJO OHZ ILLU ZV ZHKSF
            PUALYYBWALK.  OHK AOL WYVZHPJ MPUKPUN VM AOL JVYVULY UVA
            MPUHSSF WBA HU LUK AV AOL YVTHUAPJ ZAVYPLZ DOPJO OHCL ILLU
            DOPZWLYLK PU JVUULJAPVU DPAO AOL HMMHPY, PA TPNOA OHCL ILLU
            KPMMPJBSA AV MPUK H ALUHUA MVY IHZRLYCPSSL OHSS.  PA PZ
            BUKLYZAVVK AOHA AOL ULEA VM RPU PZ TY. OLUYF IHZRLYCPSSL,
            PM OL IL ZAPSS HSPCL, AOL ZVU VM ZPY JOHYSLZ IHZRLYCPSSL’Z
            FVBUNLY IYVAOLY.  AOL FVBUN THU DOLU SHZA OLHYK VM DHZ PU
            HTLYPJH, HUK PUXBPYPLZ HYL ILPUN PUZAPABALK DPAO H CPLD AV
            PUMVYTPUN OPT VM OPZ NVVK MVYABUL.”

      KY. TVYAPTLY YLMVSKLK OPZ WHWLY HUK YLWSHJLK PA PU OPZ WVJRLA.
      “AOVZL HYL AOL WBISPJ MHJAZ, TY. OVSTLZ, PU JVUULJAPVU DPAO AOL
      KLHAO VM ZPY JOHYSLZ IHZRLYCPSSL.”

      “P TBZA AOHUR FVB,” ZHPK ZOLYSVJR OVSTLZ, “MVY JHSSPUN TF
      HAALUAPVU AV H JHZL DOPJO JLYAHPUSF WYLZLUAZ ZVTL MLHABYLZ VM
      PUALYLZA. P OHK VIZLYCLK ZVTL ULDZWHWLY JVTTLUA HA AOL APTL, IBA
      P DHZ LEJLLKPUNSF WYLVJJBWPLK IF AOHA SPAASL HMMHPY VM AOL
      CHAPJHU JHTLVZ, HUK PU TF HUEPLAF AV VISPNL AOL WVWL P SVZA AVBJO
      DPAO ZLCLYHS PUALYLZAPUN LUNSPZO JHZLZ. AOPZ HYAPJSL, FVB ZHF,
      JVUAHPUZ HSS AOL WBISPJ MHJAZ?”

      “PA KVLZ.”

      “AOLU SLA TL OHCL AOL WYPCHAL VULZ.” OL SLHULK IHJR, WBA OPZ
      MPUNLY-APWZ AVNLAOLY, HUK HZZBTLK OPZ TVZA PTWHZZPCL HUK QBKPJPHS
      LEWYLZZPVU.

      “PU KVPUN ZV,” ZHPK KY. TVYAPTLY, DOV OHK ILNBU AV ZOVD ZPNUZ VM
      ZVTL ZAYVUN LTVAPVU, “P HT ALSSPUN AOHA DOPJO P OHCL UVA JVUMPKLK
      AV HUFVUL. TF TVAPCL MVY DPAOOVSKPUN PA MYVT AOL JVYVULY’Z
      PUXBPYF PZ AOHA H THU VM ZJPLUJL ZOYPURZ MYVT WSHJPUN OPTZLSM PU
      AOL WBISPJ WVZPAPVU VM ZLLTPUN AV PUKVYZL H WVWBSHY ZBWLYZAPAPVU.
      P OHK AOL MBYAOLY TVAPCL AOHA IHZRLYCPSSL OHSS, HZ AOL WHWLY
      ZHFZ, DVBSK JLYAHPUSF YLTHPU BUALUHUALK PM HUFAOPUN DLYL KVUL AV
      PUJYLHZL PAZ HSYLHKF YHAOLY NYPT YLWBAHAPVU. MVY IVAO AOLZL
      YLHZVUZ P AOVBNOA AOHA P DHZ QBZAPMPLK PU ALSSPUN YHAOLY SLZZ
      AOHU P RULD, ZPUJL UV WYHJAPJHS NVVK JVBSK YLZBSA MYVT PA, IBA
      DPAO FVB AOLYL PZ UV YLHZVU DOF P ZOVBSK UVA IL WLYMLJASF MYHUR.

      “AOL TVVY PZ CLYF ZWHYZLSF PUOHIPALK, HUK AOVZL DOV SPCL ULHY
      LHJO VAOLY HYL AOYVDU CLYF TBJO AVNLAOLY. MVY AOPZ YLHZVU P ZHD H
      NVVK KLHS VM ZPY JOHYSLZ IHZRLYCPSSL. DPAO AOL LEJLWAPVU VM TY.
      MYHURSHUK, VM SHMALY OHSS, HUK TY. ZAHWSLAVU, AOL UHABYHSPZA,
      AOLYL HYL UV VAOLY TLU VM LKBJHAPVU DPAOPU THUF TPSLZ. ZPY
      JOHYSLZ DHZ H YLAPYPUN THU, IBA AOL JOHUJL VM OPZ PSSULZZ IYVBNOA
      BZ AVNLAOLY, HUK H JVTTBUPAF VM PUALYLZAZ PU ZJPLUJL RLWA BZ ZV.
      OL OHK IYVBNOA IHJR TBJO ZJPLUAPMPJ PUMVYTHAPVU MYVT ZVBAO
      HMYPJH, HUK THUF H JOHYTPUN LCLUPUN DL OHCL ZWLUA AVNLAOLY
      KPZJBZZPUN AOL JVTWHYHAPCL HUHAVTF VM AOL IBZOTHU HUK AOL
      OVAALUAVA.

      “DPAOPU AOL SHZA MLD TVUAOZ PA ILJHTL PUJYLHZPUNSF WSHPU AV TL
      AOHA ZPY JOHYSLZ’Z ULYCVBZ ZFZALT DHZ ZAYHPULK AV AOL IYLHRPUN
      WVPUA. OL OHK AHRLU AOPZ SLNLUK DOPJO P OHCL YLHK FVB LEJLLKPUNSF
      AV OLHYA—ZV TBJO ZV AOHA, HSAOVBNO OL DVBSK DHSR PU OPZ VDU
      NYVBUKZ, UVAOPUN DVBSK PUKBJL OPT AV NV VBA BWVU AOL TVVY HA
      UPNOA. PUJYLKPISL HZ PA THF HWWLHY AV FVB, TY. OVSTLZ, OL DHZ
      OVULZASF JVUCPUJLK AOHA H KYLHKMBS MHAL VCLYOBUN OPZ MHTPSF, HUK
      JLYAHPUSF AOL YLJVYKZ DOPJO OL DHZ HISL AV NPCL VM OPZ HUJLZAVYZ
      DLYL UVA LUJVBYHNPUN. AOL PKLH VM ZVTL NOHZASF WYLZLUJL
      JVUZAHUASF OHBUALK OPT, HUK VU TVYL AOHU VUL VJJHZPVU OL OHZ
      HZRLK TL DOLAOLY P OHK VU TF TLKPJHS QVBYULFZ HA UPNOA LCLY ZLLU
      HUF ZAYHUNL JYLHABYL VY OLHYK AOL IHFPUN VM H OVBUK. AOL SHAALY
      XBLZAPVU OL WBA AV TL ZLCLYHS APTLZ, HUK HSDHFZ DPAO H CVPJL
      DOPJO CPIYHALK DPAO LEJPALTLUA.

      “P JHU DLSS YLTLTILY KYPCPUN BW AV OPZ OVBZL PU AOL LCLUPUN ZVTL
      AOYLL DLLRZ ILMVYL AOL MHAHS LCLUA. OL JOHUJLK AV IL HA OPZ OHSS
      KVVY. P OHK KLZJLUKLK MYVT TF NPN HUK DHZ ZAHUKPUN PU MYVUA VM
      OPT, DOLU P ZHD OPZ LFLZ MPE AOLTZLSCLZ VCLY TF ZOVBSKLY HUK
      ZAHYL WHZA TL DPAO HU LEWYLZZPVU VM AOL TVZA KYLHKMBS OVYYVY. P
      DOPZRLK YVBUK HUK OHK QBZA APTL AV JHAJO H NSPTWZL VM ZVTLAOPUN
      DOPJO P AVVR AV IL H SHYNL ISHJR JHSM WHZZPUN HA AOL OLHK VM AOL
      KYPCL. ZV LEJPALK HUK HSHYTLK DHZ OL AOHA P DHZ JVTWLSSLK AV NV
      KVDU AV AOL ZWVA DOLYL AOL HUPTHS OHK ILLU HUK SVVR HYVBUK MVY
      PA. PA DHZ NVUL, OVDLCLY, HUK AOL PUJPKLUA HWWLHYLK AV THRL AOL
      DVYZA PTWYLZZPVU BWVU OPZ TPUK. P ZAHFLK DPAO OPT HSS AOL
      LCLUPUN, HUK PA DHZ VU AOHA VJJHZPVU, AV LEWSHPU AOL LTVAPVU
      DOPJO OL OHK ZOVDU, AOHA OL JVUMPKLK AV TF RLLWPUN AOHA UHYYHAPCL
      DOPJO P YLHK AV FVB DOLU MPYZA P JHTL. P TLUAPVU AOPZ ZTHSS
      LWPZVKL ILJHBZL PA HZZBTLZ ZVTL PTWVYAHUJL PU CPLD VM AOL AYHNLKF
      DOPJO MVSSVDLK, IBA P DHZ JVUCPUJLK HA AOL APTL AOHA AOL THAALY
      DHZ LUAPYLSF AYPCPHS HUK AOHA OPZ LEJPALTLUA OHK UV
      QBZAPMPJHAPVU.

      “PA DHZ HA TF HKCPJL AOHA ZPY JOHYSLZ DHZ HIVBA AV NV AV SVUKVU.
      OPZ OLHYA DHZ, P RULD, HMMLJALK, HUK AOL JVUZAHUA HUEPLAF PU
      DOPJO OL SPCLK, OVDLCLY JOPTLYPJHS AOL JHBZL VM PA TPNOA IL, DHZ
      LCPKLUASF OHCPUN H ZLYPVBZ LMMLJA BWVU OPZ OLHSAO. P AOVBNOA AOHA
      H MLD TVUAOZ HTVUN AOL KPZAYHJAPVUZ VM AVDU DVBSK ZLUK OPT IHJR H
      ULD THU. TY. ZAHWSLAVU, H TBABHS MYPLUK DOV DHZ TBJO JVUJLYULK HA
      OPZ ZAHAL VM OLHSAO, DHZ VM AOL ZHTL VWPUPVU. HA AOL SHZA PUZAHUA
      JHTL AOPZ ALYYPISL JHAHZAYVWOL.

      “VU AOL UPNOA VM ZPY JOHYSLZ’Z KLHAO IHYYFTVYL AOL IBASLY, DOV
      THKL AOL KPZJVCLYF, ZLUA WLYRPUZ AOL NYVVT VU OVYZLIHJR AV TL,
      HUK HZ P DHZ ZPAAPUN BW SHAL P DHZ HISL AV YLHJO IHZRLYCPSSL OHSS
      DPAOPU HU OVBY VM AOL LCLUA. P JOLJRLK HUK JVYYVIVYHALK HSS AOL
      MHJAZ DOPJO DLYL TLUAPVULK HA AOL PUXBLZA. P MVSSVDLK AOL
      MVVAZALWZ KVDU AOL FLD HSSLF, P ZHD AOL ZWVA HA AOL TVVY-NHAL
      DOLYL OL ZLLTLK AV OHCL DHPALK, P YLTHYRLK AOL JOHUNL PU AOL
      ZOHWL VM AOL WYPUAZ HMALY AOHA WVPUA, P UVALK AOHA AOLYL DLYL UV
      VAOLY MVVAZALWZ ZHCL AOVZL VM IHYYFTVYL VU AOL ZVMA NYHCLS, HUK
      MPUHSSF P JHYLMBSSF LEHTPULK AOL IVKF, DOPJO OHK UVA ILLU AVBJOLK
      BUAPS TF HYYPCHS. ZPY JOHYSLZ SHF VU OPZ MHJL, OPZ HYTZ VBA, OPZ
      MPUNLYZ KBN PUAV AOL NYVBUK, HUK OPZ MLHABYLZ JVUCBSZLK DPAO ZVTL
      ZAYVUN LTVAPVU AV ZBJO HU LEALUA AOHA P JVBSK OHYKSF OHCL ZDVYU
      AV OPZ PKLUAPAF. AOLYL DHZ JLYAHPUSF UV WOFZPJHS PUQBYF VM HUF
      RPUK. IBA VUL MHSZL ZAHALTLUA DHZ THKL IF IHYYFTVYL HA AOL
      PUXBLZA. OL ZHPK AOHA AOLYL DLYL UV AYHJLZ BWVU AOL NYVBUK YVBUK
      AOL IVKF. OL KPK UVA VIZLYCL HUF. IBA P KPK—ZVTL SPAASL KPZAHUJL
      VMM, IBA MYLZO HUK JSLHY.”

      “MVVAWYPUAZ?”

      “MVVAWYPUAZ.”

      “H THU’Z VY H DVTHU’Z?”

      KY. TVYAPTLY SVVRLK ZAYHUNLSF HA BZ MVY HU PUZAHUA, HUK OPZ CVPJL
      ZHUR HSTVZA AV H DOPZWLY HZ OL HUZDLYLK.

      “TY. OVSTLZ, AOLF DLYL AOL MVVAWYPUAZ VM H NPNHUAPJ OVBUK!”

JOHWALY 3.
AOL WYVISLT


      P JVUMLZZ HA AOLZL DVYKZ H ZOBKKLY WHZZLK AOYVBNO TL. AOLYL DHZ H
      AOYPSS PU AOL KVJAVY’Z CVPJL DOPJO ZOVDLK AOHA OL DHZ OPTZLSM
      KLLWSF TVCLK IF AOHA DOPJO OL AVSK BZ. OVSTLZ SLHULK MVYDHYK PU
      OPZ LEJPALTLUA HUK OPZ LFLZ OHK AOL OHYK, KYF NSPAALY DOPJO ZOVA
      MYVT AOLT DOLU OL DHZ RLLUSF PUALYLZALK.

      “FVB ZHD AOPZ?”

      “HZ JSLHYSF HZ P ZLL FVB.”

      “HUK FVB ZHPK UVAOPUN?”

      “DOHA DHZ AOL BZL?”

      “OVD DHZ PA AOHA UV VUL LSZL ZHD PA?”

      “AOL THYRZ DLYL ZVTL ADLUAF FHYKZ MYVT AOL IVKF HUK UV VUL NHCL
      AOLT H AOVBNOA. P KVU’A ZBWWVZL P ZOVBSK OHCL KVUL ZV OHK P UVA
      RUVDU AOPZ SLNLUK.”

      “AOLYL HYL THUF ZOLLW-KVNZ VU AOL TVVY?”

      “UV KVBIA, IBA AOPZ DHZ UV ZOLLW-KVN.”

      “FVB ZHF PA DHZ SHYNL?”

      “LUVYTVBZ.”

      “IBA PA OHK UVA HWWYVHJOLK AOL IVKF?”

      “UV.”

      “DOHA ZVYA VM UPNOA DHZ PA?’

      “KHTW HUK YHD.”

      “IBA UVA HJABHSSF YHPUPUN?”

      “UV.”

      “DOHA PZ AOL HSSLF SPRL?”

      “AOLYL HYL ADV SPULZ VM VSK FLD OLKNL, ADLSCL MLLA OPNO HUK
      PTWLULAYHISL. AOL DHSR PU AOL JLUAYL PZ HIVBA LPNOA MLLA HJYVZZ.”

      “PZ AOLYL HUFAOPUN ILADLLU AOL OLKNLZ HUK AOL DHSR?”

      “FLZ, AOLYL PZ H ZAYPW VM NYHZZ HIVBA ZPE MLLA IYVHK VU LPAOLY
      ZPKL.”

      “P BUKLYZAHUK AOHA AOL FLD OLKNL PZ WLULAYHALK HA VUL WVPUA IF H
      NHAL?”

      “FLZ, AOL DPJRLA-NHAL DOPJO SLHKZ VU AV AOL TVVY.”

      “PZ AOLYL HUF VAOLY VWLUPUN?”

      “UVUL.”

      “ZV AOHA AV YLHJO AOL FLD HSSLF VUL LPAOLY OHZ AV JVTL KVDU PA
      MYVT AOL OVBZL VY LSZL AV LUALY PA IF AOL TVVY-NHAL?”

      “AOLYL PZ HU LEPA AOYVBNO H ZBTTLY-OVBZL HA AOL MHY LUK.”

      “OHK ZPY JOHYSLZ YLHJOLK AOPZ?”

      “UV; OL SHF HIVBA MPMAF FHYKZ MYVT PA.”

      “UVD, ALSS TL, KY. TVYAPTLY—HUK AOPZ PZ PTWVYAHUA—AOL THYRZ DOPJO
      FVB ZHD DLYL VU AOL WHAO HUK UVA VU AOL NYHZZ?”

      “UV THYRZ JVBSK ZOVD VU AOL NYHZZ.”

      “DLYL AOLF VU AOL ZHTL ZPKL VM AOL WHAO HZ AOL TVVY-NHAL?”

      “FLZ; AOLF DLYL VU AOL LKNL VM AOL WHAO VU AOL ZHTL ZPKL HZ AOL
      TVVY-NHAL.”

      “FVB PUALYLZA TL LEJLLKPUNSF. HUVAOLY WVPUA. DHZ AOL DPJRLA-NHAL
      JSVZLK?”

      “JSVZLK HUK WHKSVJRLK.”

      “OVD OPNO DHZ PA?”

      “HIVBA MVBY MLLA OPNO.”

      “AOLU HUFVUL JVBSK OHCL NVA VCLY PA?”

      “FLZ.”

      “HUK DOHA THYRZ KPK FVB ZLL IF AOL DPJRLA-NHAL?”

      “UVUL PU WHYAPJBSHY.”

      “NVVK OLHCLU! KPK UV VUL LEHTPUL?”

      “FLZ, P LEHTPULK, TFZLSM.”

      “HUK MVBUK UVAOPUN?”

      “PA DHZ HSS CLYF JVUMBZLK. ZPY JOHYSLZ OHK LCPKLUASF ZAVVK AOLYL
      MVY MPCL VY ALU TPUBALZ.”

      “OVD KV FVB RUVD AOHA?”

      “ILJHBZL AOL HZO OHK ADPJL KYVWWLK MYVT OPZ JPNHY.”

      “LEJLSSLUA! AOPZ PZ H JVSSLHNBL, DHAZVU, HMALY VBY VDU OLHYA. IBA
      AOL THYRZ?”

      “OL OHK SLMA OPZ VDU THYRZ HSS VCLY AOHA ZTHSS WHAJO VM NYHCLS. P
      JVBSK KPZJLYU UV VAOLYZ.”

      ZOLYSVJR OVSTLZ ZAYBJR OPZ OHUK HNHPUZA OPZ RULL DPAO HU
      PTWHAPLUA NLZABYL.

      “PM P OHK VUSF ILLU AOLYL!” OL JYPLK. “PA PZ LCPKLUASF H JHZL VM
      LEAYHVYKPUHYF PUALYLZA, HUK VUL DOPJO WYLZLUALK PTTLUZL
      VWWVYABUPAPLZ AV AOL ZJPLUAPMPJ LEWLYA. AOHA NYHCLS WHNL BWVU
      DOPJO P TPNOA OHCL YLHK ZV TBJO OHZ ILLU SVUN LYL AOPZ ZTBKNLK IF
      AOL YHPU HUK KLMHJLK IF AOL JSVNZ VM JBYPVBZ WLHZHUAZ. VO, KY.
      TVYAPTLY, KY. TVYAPTLY, AV AOPUR AOHA FVB ZOVBSK UVA OHCL JHSSLK
      TL PU! FVB OHCL PUKLLK TBJO AV HUZDLY MVY.”

      “P JVBSK UVA JHSS FVB PU, TY. OVSTLZ, DPAOVBA KPZJSVZPUN AOLZL
      MHJAZ AV AOL DVYSK, HUK P OHCL HSYLHKF NPCLU TF YLHZVUZ MVY UVA
      DPZOPUN AV KV ZV. ILZPKLZ, ILZPKLZ—”

      “DOF KV FVB OLZPAHAL?”

      “AOLYL PZ H YLHST PU DOPJO AOL TVZA HJBAL HUK TVZA LEWLYPLUJLK VM
      KLALJAPCLZ PZ OLSWSLZZ.”

      “FVB TLHU AOHA AOL AOPUN PZ ZBWLYUHABYHS?”

      “P KPK UVA WVZPAPCLSF ZHF ZV.”

      “UV, IBA FVB LCPKLUASF AOPUR PA.”

      “ZPUJL AOL AYHNLKF, TY. OVSTLZ, AOLYL OHCL JVTL AV TF LHYZ
      ZLCLYHS PUJPKLUAZ DOPJO HYL OHYK AV YLJVUJPSL DPAO AOL ZLAASLK
      VYKLY VM UHABYL.”

      “MVY LEHTWSL?”

      “P MPUK AOHA ILMVYL AOL ALYYPISL LCLUA VJJBYYLK ZLCLYHS WLVWSL
      OHK ZLLU H JYLHABYL BWVU AOL TVVY DOPJO JVYYLZWVUKZ DPAO AOPZ
      IHZRLYCPSSL KLTVU, HUK DOPJO JVBSK UVA WVZZPISF IL HUF HUPTHS
      RUVDU AV ZJPLUJL. AOLF HSS HNYLLK AOHA PA DHZ H OBNL JYLHABYL,
      SBTPUVBZ, NOHZASF, HUK ZWLJAYHS. P OHCL JYVZZ-LEHTPULK AOLZL TLU,
      VUL VM AOLT H OHYK-OLHKLK JVBUAYFTHU, VUL H MHYYPLY, HUK VUL H
      TVVYSHUK MHYTLY, DOV HSS ALSS AOL ZHTL ZAVYF VM AOPZ KYLHKMBS
      HWWHYPAPVU, LEHJASF JVYYLZWVUKPUN AV AOL OLSS-OVBUK VM AOL
      SLNLUK. P HZZBYL FVB AOHA AOLYL PZ H YLPNU VM ALYYVY PU AOL
      KPZAYPJA, HUK AOHA PA PZ H OHYKF THU DOV DPSS JYVZZ AOL TVVY HA
      UPNOA.”

      “HUK FVB, H AYHPULK THU VM ZJPLUJL, ILSPLCL PA AV IL
      ZBWLYUHABYHS?”

      “P KV UVA RUVD DOHA AV ILSPLCL.”

      OVSTLZ ZOYBNNLK OPZ ZOVBSKLYZ. “P OHCL OPAOLYAV JVUMPULK TF
      PUCLZAPNHAPVUZ AV AOPZ DVYSK,” ZHPK OL. “PU H TVKLZA DHF P OHCL
      JVTIHALK LCPS, IBA AV AHRL VU AOL MHAOLY VM LCPS OPTZLSM DVBSK,
      WLYOHWZ, IL AVV HTIPAPVBZ H AHZR. FLA FVB TBZA HKTPA AOHA AOL
      MVVATHYR PZ THALYPHS.”

      “AOL VYPNPUHS OVBUK DHZ THALYPHS LUVBNO AV ABN H THU’Z AOYVHA
      VBA, HUK FLA OL DHZ KPHIVSPJHS HZ DLSS.”

      “P ZLL AOHA FVB OHCL XBPAL NVUL VCLY AV AOL ZBWLYUHABYHSPZAZ. IBA
      UVD, KY. TVYAPTLY, ALSS TL AOPZ. PM FVB OVSK AOLZL CPLDZ, DOF
      OHCL FVB JVTL AV JVUZBSA TL HA HSS? FVB ALSS TL PU AOL ZHTL
      IYLHAO AOHA PA PZ BZLSLZZ AV PUCLZAPNHAL ZPY JOHYSLZ’Z KLHAO, HUK
      AOHA FVB KLZPYL TL AV KV PA.”

      “P KPK UVA ZHF AOHA P KLZPYLK FVB AV KV PA.”

      “AOLU, OVD JHU P HZZPZA FVB?”

      “IF HKCPZPUN TL HZ AV DOHA P ZOVBSK KV DPAO ZPY OLUYF
      IHZRLYCPSSL, DOV HYYPCLZ HA DHALYSVV ZAHAPVU”—KY. TVYAPTLY SVVRLK
      HA OPZ DHAJO—“PU LEHJASF VUL OVBY HUK H XBHYALY.”

      “OL ILPUN AOL OLPY?”

      “FLZ. VU AOL KLHAO VM ZPY JOHYSLZ DL PUXBPYLK MVY AOPZ FVBUN
      NLUASLTHU HUK MVBUK AOHA OL OHK ILLU MHYTPUN PU JHUHKH. MYVT AOL
      HJJVBUAZ DOPJO OHCL YLHJOLK BZ OL PZ HU LEJLSSLUA MLSSVD PU LCLYF
      DHF. P ZWLHR UVD UVA HZ H TLKPJHS THU IBA HZ H AYBZALL HUK
      LELJBAVY VM ZPY JOHYSLZ’Z DPSS.”

      “AOLYL PZ UV VAOLY JSHPTHUA, P WYLZBTL?”

      “UVUL. AOL VUSF VAOLY RPUZTHU DOVT DL OHCL ILLU HISL AV AYHJL DHZ
      YVKNLY IHZRLYCPSSL, AOL FVBUNLZA VM AOYLL IYVAOLYZ VM DOVT WVVY
      ZPY JOHYSLZ DHZ AOL LSKLY. AOL ZLJVUK IYVAOLY, DOV KPLK FVBUN, PZ
      AOL MHAOLY VM AOPZ SHK OLUYF. AOL AOPYK, YVKNLY, DHZ AOL ISHJR
      ZOLLW VM AOL MHTPSF. OL JHTL VM AOL VSK THZALYMBS IHZRLYCPSSL
      ZAYHPU HUK DHZ AOL CLYF PTHNL, AOLF ALSS TL, VM AOL MHTPSF
      WPJABYL VM VSK OBNV. OL THKL LUNSHUK AVV OVA AV OVSK OPT, MSLK AV
      JLUAYHS HTLYPJH, HUK KPLK AOLYL PU 1876 VM FLSSVD MLCLY. OLUYF PZ
      AOL SHZA VM AOL IHZRLYCPSSLZ. PU VUL OVBY HUK MPCL TPUBALZ P TLLA
      OPT HA DHALYSVV ZAHAPVU. P OHCL OHK H DPYL AOHA OL HYYPCLK HA
      ZVBAOHTWAVU AOPZ TVYUPUN. UVD, TY. OVSTLZ, DOHA DVBSK FVB HKCPZL
      TL AV KV DPAO OPT?”

      “DOF ZOVBSK OL UVA NV AV AOL OVTL VM OPZ MHAOLYZ?”

      “PA ZLLTZ UHABYHS, KVLZ PA UVA? HUK FLA, JVUZPKLY AOHA LCLYF
      IHZRLYCPSSL DOV NVLZ AOLYL TLLAZ DPAO HU LCPS MHAL. P MLLS ZBYL
      AOHA PM ZPY JOHYSLZ JVBSK OHCL ZWVRLU DPAO TL ILMVYL OPZ KLHAO OL
      DVBSK OHCL DHYULK TL HNHPUZA IYPUNPUN AOPZ, AOL SHZA VM AOL VSK
      YHJL, HUK AOL OLPY AV NYLHA DLHSAO, AV AOHA KLHKSF WSHJL. HUK FLA
      PA JHUUVA IL KLUPLK AOHA AOL WYVZWLYPAF VM AOL DOVSL WVVY, ISLHR
      JVBUAYFZPKL KLWLUKZ BWVU OPZ WYLZLUJL. HSS AOL NVVK DVYR DOPJO
      OHZ ILLU KVUL IF ZPY JOHYSLZ DPSS JYHZO AV AOL NYVBUK PM AOLYL PZ
      UV ALUHUA VM AOL OHSS. P MLHY SLZA P ZOVBSK IL ZDHFLK AVV TBJO IF
      TF VDU VICPVBZ PUALYLZA PU AOL THAALY, HUK AOHA PZ DOF P IYPUN
      AOL JHZL ILMVYL FVB HUK HZR MVY FVBY HKCPJL.”

      OVSTLZ JVUZPKLYLK MVY H SPAASL APTL.

      “WBA PUAV WSHPU DVYKZ, AOL THAALY PZ AOPZ,” ZHPK OL. “PU FVBY
      VWPUPVU AOLYL PZ H KPHIVSPJHS HNLUJF DOPJO THRLZ KHYATVVY HU
      BUZHML HIVKL MVY H IHZRLYCPSSL—AOHA PZ FVBY VWPUPVU?”

      “HA SLHZA P TPNOA NV AOL SLUNAO VM ZHFPUN AOHA AOLYL PZ ZVTL
      LCPKLUJL AOHA AOPZ THF IL ZV.”

      “LEHJASF. IBA ZBYLSF, PM FVBY ZBWLYUHABYHS AOLVYF IL JVYYLJA, PA
      JVBSK DVYR AOL FVBUN THU LCPS PU SVUKVU HZ LHZPSF HZ PU
      KLCVUZOPYL. H KLCPS DPAO TLYLSF SVJHS WVDLYZ SPRL H WHYPZO CLZAYF
      DVBSK IL AVV PUJVUJLPCHISL H AOPUN.”

      “FVB WBA AOL THAALY TVYL MSPWWHUASF, TY. OVSTLZ, AOHU FVB DVBSK
      WYVIHISF KV PM FVB DLYL IYVBNOA PUAV WLYZVUHS JVUAHJA DPAO AOLZL
      AOPUNZ. FVBY HKCPJL, AOLU, HZ P BUKLYZAHUK PA, PZ AOHA AOL FVBUN
      THU DPSS IL HZ ZHML PU KLCVUZOPYL HZ PU SVUKVU. OL JVTLZ PU MPMAF
      TPUBALZ. DOHA DVBSK FVB YLJVTTLUK?”

      “P YLJVTTLUK, ZPY, AOHA FVB AHRL H JHI, JHSS VMM FVBY ZWHUPLS DOV
      PZ ZJYHAJOPUN HA TF MYVUA KVVY, HUK WYVJLLK AV DHALYSVV AV TLLA
      ZPY OLUYF IHZRLYCPSSL.”

      “HUK AOLU?”

      “HUK AOLU FVB DPSS ZHF UVAOPUN AV OPT HA HSS BUAPS P OHCL THKL BW
      TF TPUK HIVBA AOL THAALY.”

      “OVD SVUN DPSS PA AHRL FVB AV THRL BW FVBY TPUK?”

      “ADLUAF-MVBY OVBYZ. HA ALU V’JSVJR AVTVYYVD, KY. TVYAPTLY, P DPSS
      IL TBJO VISPNLK AV FVB PM FVB DPSS JHSS BWVU TL OLYL, HUK PA DPSS
      IL VM OLSW AV TL PU TF WSHUZ MVY AOL MBABYL PM FVB DPSS IYPUN ZPY

      “P DPSS KV ZV, TY. OVSTLZ.” OL ZJYPIISLK AOL HWWVPUATLUA VU OPZ

      “VUSF VUL TVYL XBLZAPVU, KY. TVYAPTLY. FVB ZHF AOHA ILMVYL ZPY
      JOHYSLZ IHZRLYCPSSL’Z KLHAO ZLCLYHS WLVWSL ZHD AOPZ HWWHYPAPVU
      BWVU AOL TVVY?”

      “AOYLL WLVWSL KPK.”

      “KPK HUF ZLL PA HMALY?”

      “P OHCL UVA OLHYK VM HUF.”

      “AOHUR FVB. NVVK-TVYUPUN.”

      OVSTLZ YLABYULK AV OPZ ZLHA DPAO AOHA XBPLA SVVR VM PUDHYK
      ZHAPZMHJAPVU DOPJO TLHUA AOHA OL OHK H JVUNLUPHS AHZR ILMVYL OPT.

      “NVPUN VBA, DHAZVU?”

      “BUSLZZ P JHU OLSW FVB.”

      “UV, TF KLHY MLSSVD, PA PZ HA AOL OVBY VM HJAPVU AOHA P ABYU AV
      FVB MVY HPK. IBA AOPZ PZ ZWSLUKPK, YLHSSF BUPXBL MYVT ZVTL WVPUAZ

      WVBUK VM AOL ZAYVUNLZA ZOHN AVIHJJV? AOHUR FVB. PA DVBSK IL HZ
      DLSS PM FVB JVBSK THRL PA JVUCLUPLUA UVA AV YLABYU ILMVYL
      LCLUPUN. AOLU P ZOVBSK IL CLYF NSHK AV JVTWHYL PTWYLZZPVUZ HZ AV
      AOPZ TVZA PUALYLZAPUN WYVISLT DOPJO OHZ ILLU ZBITPAALK AV BZ AOPZ
      TVYUPUN.”

      P RULD AOHA ZLJSBZPVU HUK ZVSPABKL DLYL CLYF ULJLZZHYF MVY TF
      MYPLUK PU AOVZL OVBYZ VM PUALUZL TLUAHS JVUJLUAYHAPVU KBYPUN
      DOPJO OL DLPNOLK LCLYF WHYAPJSL VM LCPKLUJL, JVUZAYBJALK
      HSALYUHAPCL AOLVYPLZ, IHSHUJLK VUL HNHPUZA AOL VAOLY, HUK THKL BW
      OPZ TPUK HZ AV DOPJO WVPUAZ DLYL LZZLUAPHS HUK DOPJO PTTHALYPHS.
      P AOLYLMVYL ZWLUA AOL KHF HA TF JSBI HUK KPK UVA YLABYU AV IHRLY
      ZAYLLA BUAPS LCLUPUN. PA DHZ ULHYSF UPUL V’JSVJR DOLU P MVBUK
      TFZLSM PU AOL ZPAAPUN-YVVT VUJL TVYL.

      TF MPYZA PTWYLZZPVU HZ P VWLULK AOL KVVY DHZ AOHA H MPYL OHK
      IYVRLU VBA, MVY AOL YVVT DHZ ZV MPSSLK DPAO ZTVRL AOHA AOL SPNOA
      VM AOL SHTW BWVU AOL AHISL DHZ ISBYYLK IF PA. HZ P LUALYLK,
      OVDLCLY, TF MLHYZ DLYL ZLA HA YLZA, MVY PA DHZ AOL HJYPK MBTLZ VM
      ZAYVUN JVHYZL AVIHJJV DOPJO AVVR TL IF AOL AOYVHA HUK ZLA TL
      JVBNOPUN. AOYVBNO AOL OHGL P OHK H CHNBL CPZPVU VM OVSTLZ PU OPZ
      KYLZZPUN-NVDU JVPSLK BW PU HU HYTJOHPY DPAO OPZ ISHJR JSHF WPWL
      ILADLLU OPZ SPWZ. ZLCLYHS YVSSZ VM WHWLY SHF HYVBUK OPT.

      “JHBNOA JVSK, DHAZVU?” ZHPK OL.

      “UV, PA’Z AOPZ WVPZVUVBZ HATVZWOLYL.”

      “P ZBWWVZL PA _PZ_ WYLAAF AOPJR, UVD AOHA FVB TLUAPVU PA.”

      “AOPJR! PA PZ PUAVSLYHISL.”

      “VWLU AOL DPUKVD, AOLU! FVB OHCL ILLU HA FVBY JSBI HSS KHF, P
      WLYJLPCL.”

      “TF KLHY OVSTLZ!”

      “HT P YPNOA?”

      “JLYAHPUSF, IBA OVD?”

      OL SHBNOLK HA TF ILDPSKLYLK LEWYLZZPVU. “AOLYL PZ H KLSPNOAMBS
      MYLZOULZZ HIVBA FVB, DHAZVU, DOPJO THRLZ PA H WSLHZBYL AV
      LELYJPZL HUF ZTHSS WVDLYZ DOPJO P WVZZLZZ HA FVBY LEWLUZL. H

      IVVAZ. OL OHZ ILLU H MPEABYL AOLYLMVYL HSS KHF. OL PZ UVA H THU

      VICPVBZ?”

      “DLSS, PA PZ YHAOLY VICPVBZ.”

      “AOL DVYSK PZ MBSS VM VICPVBZ AOPUNZ DOPJO UVIVKF IF HUF JOHUJL
      LCLY VIZLYCLZ. DOLYL KV FVB AOPUR AOHA P OHCL ILLU?”

      “H MPEABYL HSZV.”

      “VU AOL JVUAYHYF, P OHCL ILLU AV KLCVUZOPYL.”

      “PU ZWPYPA?”

      “LEHJASF. TF IVKF OHZ YLTHPULK PU AOPZ HYTJOHPY HUK OHZ, P YLNYLA
      AV VIZLYCL, JVUZBTLK PU TF HIZLUJL ADV SHYNL WVAZ VM JVMMLL HUK

      JVBSK MPUK TF DHF HIVBA.”

      “H SHYNL-ZJHSL THW, P WYLZBTL?”

      “CLYF SHYNL.”

      OL BUYVSSLK VUL ZLJAPVU HUK OLSK PA VCLY OPZ RULL. “OLYL FVB OHCL
      AOL WHYAPJBSHY KPZAYPJA DOPJO JVUJLYUZ BZ. AOHA PZ IHZRLYCPSSL
      OHSS PU AOL TPKKSL.”

      “DPAO H DVVK YVBUK PA?”

      “LEHJASF. P MHUJF AOL FLD HSSLF, AOVBNO UVA THYRLK BUKLY AOHA
      UHTL, TBZA ZAYLAJO HSVUN AOPZ SPUL, DPAO AOL TVVY, HZ FVB
      WLYJLPCL, BWVU AOL YPNOA VM PA. AOPZ ZTHSS JSBTW VM IBPSKPUNZ
      OLYL PZ AOL OHTSLA VM NYPTWLU, DOLYL VBY MYPLUK KY. TVYAPTLY OHZ
      OPZ OLHKXBHYALYZ. DPAOPU H YHKPBZ VM MPCL TPSLZ AOLYL HYL, HZ FVB
      ZLL, VUSF H CLYF MLD ZJHAALYLK KDLSSPUNZ. OLYL PZ SHMALY OHSS,
      DOPJO DHZ TLUAPVULK PU AOL UHYYHAPCL. AOLYL PZ H OVBZL PUKPJHALK
      OLYL DOPJO THF IL AOL YLZPKLUJL VM AOL UHABYHSPZA—ZAHWSLAVU, PM P
      YLTLTILY YPNOA, DHZ OPZ UHTL. OLYL HYL ADV TVVYSHUK MHYTOVBZLZ,
      OPNO AVY HUK MVBSTPYL. AOLU MVBYALLU TPSLZ HDHF AOL NYLHA JVUCPJA
      WYPZVU VM WYPUJLAVDU. ILADLLU HUK HYVBUK AOLZL ZJHAALYLK WVPUAZ
      LEALUKZ AOL KLZVSHAL, SPMLSLZZ TVVY. AOPZ, AOLU, PZ AOL ZAHNL
      BWVU DOPJO AYHNLKF OHZ ILLU WSHFLK, HUK BWVU DOPJO DL THF OLSW AV
      WSHF PA HNHPU.”

      “PA TBZA IL H DPSK WSHJL.”

      “FLZ, AOL ZLAAPUN PZ H DVYAOF VUL. PM AOL KLCPS KPK KLZPYL AV
      OHCL H OHUK PU AOL HMMHPYZ VM TLU—”

      “AOLU FVB HYL FVBYZLSM PUJSPUPUN AV AOL ZBWLYUHABYHS
      LEWSHUHAPVU.”

      “AOL KLCPS’Z HNLUAZ THF IL VM MSLZO HUK ISVVK, THF AOLF UVA?
      AOLYL HYL ADV XBLZAPVUZ DHPAPUN MVY BZ HA AOL VBAZLA. AOL VUL PZ
      DOLAOLY HUF JYPTL OHZ ILLU JVTTPAALK HA HSS; AOL ZLJVUK PZ, DOHA
      PZ AOL JYPTL HUK OVD DHZ PA JVTTPAALK? VM JVBYZL, PM KY.
      TVYAPTLY’Z ZBYTPZL ZOVBSK IL JVYYLJA, HUK DL HYL KLHSPUN DPAO
      MVYJLZ VBAZPKL AOL VYKPUHYF SHDZ VM UHABYL, AOLYL PZ HU LUK VM
      VBY PUCLZAPNHAPVU. IBA DL HYL IVBUK AV LEOHBZA HSS VAOLY
      OFWVAOLZLZ ILMVYL MHSSPUN IHJR BWVU AOPZ VUL. P AOPUR DL’SS ZOBA
      AOHA DPUKVD HNHPU, PM FVB KVU’A TPUK. PA PZ H ZPUNBSHY AOPUN, IBA
      P MPUK AOHA H JVUJLUAYHALK HATVZWOLYL OLSWZ H JVUJLUAYHAPVU VM
      AOVBNOA. P OHCL UVA WBZOLK PA AV AOL SLUNAO VM NLAAPUN PUAV H IVE
      AV AOPUR, IBA AOHA PZ AOL SVNPJHS VBAJVTL VM TF JVUCPJAPVUZ. OHCL
      FVB ABYULK AOL JHZL VCLY PU FVBY TPUK?”

      “FLZ, P OHCL AOVBNOA H NVVK KLHS VM PA PU AOL JVBYZL VM AOL KHF.”

      “DOHA KV FVB THRL VM PA?”

      “PA PZ CLYF ILDPSKLYPUN.”

      “PA OHZ JLYAHPUSF H JOHYHJALY VM PAZ VDU. AOLYL HYL WVPUAZ VM
      KPZAPUJAPVU HIVBA PA. AOHA JOHUNL PU AOL MVVAWYPUAZ, MVY LEHTWSL.
      DOHA KV FVB THRL VM AOHA?”

      “TVYAPTLY ZHPK AOHA AOL THU OHK DHSRLK VU APWAVL KVDU AOHA
      WVYAPVU VM AOL HSSLF.”

      “OL VUSF YLWLHALK DOHA ZVTL MVVS OHK ZHPK HA AOL PUXBLZA. DOF
      ZOVBSK H THU DHSR VU APWAVL KVDU AOL HSSLF?”

      “DOHA AOLU?”

      “OL DHZ YBUUPUN, DHAZVU—YBUUPUN KLZWLYHALSF, YBUUPUN MVY OPZ
      SPML, YBUUPUN BUAPS OL IBYZA OPZ OLHYA—HUK MLSS KLHK BWVU OPZ
      MHJL.”

      “YBUUPUN MYVT DOHA?”

      “AOLYL SPLZ VBY WYVISLT. AOLYL HYL PUKPJHAPVUZ AOHA AOL THU DHZ
      JYHGLK DPAO MLHY ILMVYL LCLY OL ILNHU AV YBU.”

      “OVD JHU FVB ZHF AOHA?”

      “P HT WYLZBTPUN AOHA AOL JHBZL VM OPZ MLHYZ JHTL AV OPT HJYVZZ
      AOL TVVY. PM AOHA DLYL ZV, HUK PA ZLLTZ TVZA WYVIHISL, VUSF H THU
      DOV OHK SVZA OPZ DPAZ DVBSK OHCL YBU _MYVT_ AOL OVBZL PUZALHK VM
      AVDHYKZ PA. PM AOL NPWZF’Z LCPKLUJL THF IL AHRLU HZ AYBL, OL YHU
      DPAO JYPLZ MVY OLSW PU AOL KPYLJAPVU DOLYL OLSW DHZ SLHZA SPRLSF
      AV IL. AOLU, HNHPU, DOVT DHZ OL DHPAPUN MVY AOHA UPNOA, HUK DOF
      DHZ OL DHPAPUN MVY OPT PU AOL FLD HSSLF YHAOLY AOHU PU OPZ VDU
      OVBZL?”

      “FVB AOPUR AOHA OL DHZ DHPAPUN MVY ZVTLVUL?”

      “AOL THU DHZ LSKLYSF HUK PUMPYT. DL JHU BUKLYZAHUK OPZ AHRPUN HU
      LCLUPUN ZAYVSS, IBA AOL NYVBUK DHZ KHTW HUK AOL UPNOA PUJSLTLUA.
      PZ PA UHABYHS AOHA OL ZOVBSK ZAHUK MVY MPCL VY ALU TPUBALZ, HZ
      KY. TVYAPTLY, DPAO TVYL WYHJAPJHS ZLUZL AOHU P ZOVBSK OHCL NPCLU
      OPT JYLKPA MVY, KLKBJLK MYVT AOL JPNHY HZO?”

      “IBA OL DLUA VBA LCLYF LCLUPUN.”

      “P AOPUR PA BUSPRLSF AOHA OL DHPALK HA AOL TVVY-NHAL LCLYF
      LCLUPUN. VU AOL JVUAYHYF, AOL LCPKLUJL PZ AOHA OL HCVPKLK AOL
      TVVY. AOHA UPNOA OL DHPALK AOLYL. PA DHZ AOL UPNOA ILMVYL OL THKL
      OPZ KLWHYABYL MVY SVUKVU. AOL AOPUN AHRLZ ZOHWL, DHAZVU. PA
      ILJVTLZ JVOLYLUA. TPNOA P HZR FVB AV OHUK TL TF CPVSPU, HUK DL
      DPSS WVZAWVUL HSS MBYAOLY AOVBNOA BWVU AOPZ IBZPULZZ BUAPS DL
      OHCL OHK AOL HKCHUAHNL VM TLLAPUN KY. TVYAPTLY HUK ZPY OLUYF
      IHZRLYCPSSL PU AOL TVYUPUN.”

JOHWALY 4.
ZPY OLUYF IHZRLYCPSSL


      VBY IYLHRMHZA AHISL DHZ JSLHYLK LHYSF, HUK OVSTLZ DHPALK PU OPZ
      KYLZZPUN-NVDU MVY AOL WYVTPZLK PUALYCPLD. VBY JSPLUAZ DLYL
      WBUJABHS AV AOLPY HWWVPUATLUA, MVY AOL JSVJR OHK QBZA ZAYBJR ALU
      DOLU KY. TVYAPTLY DHZ ZOVDU BW, MVSSVDLK IF AOL FVBUN IHYVULA.
      AOL SHAALY DHZ H ZTHSS, HSLYA, KHYR-LFLK THU HIVBA AOPYAF FLHYZ
      VM HNL, CLYF ZABYKPSF IBPSA, DPAO AOPJR ISHJR LFLIYVDZ HUK H
      ZAYVUN, WBNUHJPVBZ MHJL. OL DVYL H YBKKF-APUALK ADLLK ZBPA HUK
      OHK AOL DLHAOLY-ILHALU HWWLHYHUJL VM VUL DOV OHZ ZWLUA TVZA VM
      OPZ APTL PU AOL VWLU HPY, HUK FLA AOLYL DHZ ZVTLAOPUN PU OPZ
      ZALHKF LFL HUK AOL XBPLA HZZBYHUJL VM OPZ ILHYPUN DOPJO PUKPJHALK
      AOL NLUASLTHU.

      “AOPZ PZ ZPY OLUYF IHZRLYCPSSL,” ZHPK KY. TVYAPTLY.

      “DOF, FLZ,” ZHPK OL, “HUK AOL ZAYHUNL AOPUN PZ, TY. ZOLYSVJR
      OVSTLZ, AOHA PM TF MYPLUK OLYL OHK UVA WYVWVZLK JVTPUN YVBUK AV
      FVB AOPZ TVYUPUN P ZOVBSK OHCL JVTL VU TF VDU HJJVBUA. P
      BUKLYZAHUK AOHA FVB AOPUR VBA SPAASL WBGGSLZ, HUK P’CL OHK VUL
      AOPZ TVYUPUN DOPJO DHUAZ TVYL AOPURPUN VBA AOHU P HT HISL AV NPCL
      PA.”

      “WYHF AHRL H ZLHA, ZPY OLUYF. KV P BUKLYZAHUK FVB AV ZHF AOHA FVB
      OHCL FVBYZLSM OHK ZVTL YLTHYRHISL LEWLYPLUJL ZPUJL FVB HYYPCLK PU
      SVUKVU?”

      “UVAOPUN VM TBJO PTWVYAHUJL, TY. OVSTLZ. VUSF H QVRL, HZ SPRL HZ
      UVA. PA DHZ AOPZ SLAALY, PM FVB JHU JHSS PA H SLAALY, DOPJO
      YLHJOLK TL AOPZ TVYUPUN.”

      OL SHPK HU LUCLSVWL BWVU AOL AHISL, HUK DL HSS ILUA VCLY PA. PA
      DHZ VM JVTTVU XBHSPAF, NYLFPZO PU JVSVBY. AOL HKKYLZZ, “ZPY OLUYF
      IHZRLYCPSSL, UVYAOBTILYSHUK OVALS,” DHZ WYPUALK PU YVBNO
      JOHYHJALYZ; AOL WVZA-THYR “JOHYPUN JYVZZ,” HUK AOL KHAL VM
      WVZAPUN AOL WYLJLKPUN LCLUPUN.

      “DOV RULD AOHA FVB DLYL NVPUN AV AOL UVYAOBTILYSHUK OVALS?” HZRLK
      OVSTLZ, NSHUJPUN RLLUSF HJYVZZ HA VBY CPZPAVY.

      “UV VUL JVBSK OHCL RUVDU. DL VUSF KLJPKLK HMALY P TLA KY.
      TVYAPTLY.”

      “IBA KY. TVYAPTLY DHZ UV KVBIA HSYLHKF ZAVWWPUN AOLYL?”

      “UV, P OHK ILLU ZAHFPUN DPAO H MYPLUK,” ZHPK AOL KVJAVY.

      “AOLYL DHZ UV WVZZPISL PUKPJHAPVU AOHA DL PUALUKLK AV NV AV AOPZ
      OVALS.”

      “OBT! ZVTLVUL ZLLTZ AV IL CLYF KLLWSF PUALYLZALK PU FVBY
      TVCLTLUAZ.” VBA VM AOL LUCLSVWL OL AVVR H OHSM-ZOLLA VM MVVSZJHW
      WHWLY MVSKLK PUAV MVBY. AOPZ OL VWLULK HUK ZWYLHK MSHA BWVU AOL
      AHISL. HJYVZZ AOL TPKKSL VM PA H ZPUNSL ZLUALUJL OHK ILLU MVYTLK
      IF AOL LEWLKPLUA VM WHZAPUN WYPUALK DVYKZ BWVU PA. PA YHU:

        HZ FVB CHSBL FVBY SPML VY FVBY YLHZVU RLLW HDHF MYVT AOL TVVY.

      AOL DVYK “TVVY” VUSF DHZ WYPUALK PU PUR.

      “UVD,” ZHPK ZPY OLUYF IHZRLYCPSSL, “WLYOHWZ FVB DPSS ALSS TL, TY.
      OVSTLZ, DOHA PU AOBUKLY PZ AOL TLHUPUN VM AOHA, HUK DOV PA PZ
      AOHA AHRLZ ZV TBJO PUALYLZA PU TF HMMHPYZ?”

      “DOHA KV FVB THRL VM PA, KY. TVYAPTLY? FVB TBZA HSSVD AOHA AOLYL
      PZ UVAOPUN ZBWLYUHABYHS HIVBA AOPZ, HA HUF YHAL?”

      “UV, ZPY, IBA PA TPNOA CLYF DLSS JVTL MYVT ZVTLVUL DOV DHZ
      JVUCPUJLK AOHA AOL IBZPULZZ PZ ZBWLYUHABYHS.”

      “DOHA IBZPULZZ?” HZRLK ZPY OLUYF ZOHYWSF. “PA ZLLTZ AV TL AOHA
      HSS FVB NLUASLTLU RUVD H NYLHA KLHS TVYL AOHU P KV HIVBA TF VDU
      HMMHPYZ.”

      “FVB ZOHSS ZOHYL VBY RUVDSLKNL ILMVYL FVB SLHCL AOPZ YVVT, ZPY
      OLUYF. P WYVTPZL FVB AOHA,” ZHPK ZOLYSVJR OVSTLZ. “DL DPSS
      JVUMPUL VBYZLSCLZ MVY AOL WYLZLUA DPAO FVBY WLYTPZZPVU AV AOPZ
      CLYF PUALYLZAPUN KVJBTLUA, DOPJO TBZA OHCL ILLU WBA AVNLAOLY HUK
      WVZALK FLZALYKHF LCLUPUN. OHCL FVB FLZALYKHF’Z _APTLZ_, DHAZVU?”

      “PA PZ OLYL PU AOL JVYULY.”

      “TPNOA P AYVBISL FVB MVY PA—AOL PUZPKL WHNL, WSLHZL, DPAO AOL
      SLHKPUN HYAPJSLZ?” OL NSHUJLK ZDPMASF VCLY PA, YBUUPUN OPZ LFLZ
      BW HUK KVDU AOL JVSBTUZ. “JHWPAHS HYAPJSL AOPZ VU MYLL AYHKL.
      WLYTPA TL AV NPCL FVB HU LEAYHJA MYVT PA.

     ‘FVB THF IL JHQVSLK PUAV PTHNPUPUN AOHA FVBY VDU ZWLJPHS AYHKL VY
     FVBY VDU PUKBZAYF DPSS IL LUJVBYHNLK IF H WYVALJAPCL AHYPMM, IBA
     PA ZAHUKZ AV YLHZVU AOHA ZBJO SLNPZSHAPVU TBZA PU AOL SVUN YBU
     RLLW HDHF DLHSAO MYVT AOL JVBUAYF, KPTPUPZO AOL CHSBL VM VBY
     PTWVYAZ, HUK SVDLY AOL NLULYHS JVUKPAPVUZ VM SPML PU AOPZ PZSHUK.’

      ZLJVUK. FVB THF OHCL VIZLYCLK AOHA P ADPJL ZAYVSSLK VCLY AV AOL
      DPUKVD DOPSL KY. TVYAPTLY DHZ YLHKPUN OPZ SLNLUK.”

      “FLZ, P YLTLTILY.”

      “P DHZ SVVRPUN VBA MVY SVPALYLYZ PU AOL ZAYLLA, IBA P ZHD UVUL.
      DL HYL KLHSPUN DPAO H JSLCLY THU, DHAZVU. AOPZ THAALY JBAZ CLYF
      KLLW, HUK AOVBNO P OHCL UVA MPUHSSF THKL BW TF TPUK DOLAOLY PA PZ

      HA VUJL MVSSVDLK AOLT PU AOL OVWLZ VM THYRPUN KVDU AOLPY
      PUCPZPISL HAALUKHUA. ZV DPSF DHZ OL AOHA OL OHK UVA AYBZALK
      OPTZLSM BWVU MVVA, IBA OL OHK HCHPSLK OPTZLSM VM H JHI ZV AOHA OL
      JVBSK SVPALY ILOPUK VY KHZO WHZA AOLT HUK ZV LZJHWL AOLPY UVAPJL.

      VICPVBZ KPZHKCHUAHNL.”

      “PA WBAZ OPT PU AOL WVDLY VM AOL JHITHU.”

      “LEHJASF.”

      “DOHA H WPAF DL KPK UVA NLA AOL UBTILY!”

      “TF KLHY DHAZVU, JSBTZF HZ P OHCL ILLU, FVB ZBYLSF KV UVA
      ZLYPVBZSF PTHNPUL AOHA P ULNSLJALK AV NLA AOL UBTILY? UV. 2704 PZ

      “P MHPS AV ZLL OVD FVB JVBSK OHCL KVUL TVYL.”

      “VU VIZLYCPUN AOL JHI P ZOVBSK OHCL PUZAHUASF ABYULK HUK DHSRLK
      PU AOL VAOLY KPYLJAPVU. P ZOVBSK AOLU HA TF SLPZBYL OHCL OPYLK H
      ZLJVUK JHI HUK MVSSVDLK AOL MPYZA HA H YLZWLJAMBS KPZAHUJL, VY,
      ILAALY ZAPSS, OHCL KYPCLU AV AOL UVYAOBTILYSHUK OVALS HUK DHPALK
      AOLYL. DOLU VBY BURUVDU OHK MVSSVDLK IHZRLYCPSSL OVTL DL ZOVBSK
      OHCL OHK AOL VWWVYABUPAF VM WSHFPUN OPZ VDU NHTL BWVU OPTZLSM HUK
      ZLLPUN DOLYL OL THKL MVY. HZ PA PZ, IF HU PUKPZJYLLA LHNLYULZZ,
      DOPJO DHZ AHRLU HKCHUAHNL VM DPAO LEAYHVYKPUHYF XBPJRULZZ HUK
      LULYNF IF VBY VWWVULUA, DL OHCL ILAYHFLK VBYZLSCLZ HUK SVZA VBY
      THU.”

      DL OHK ILLU ZHBUALYPUN ZSVDSF KVDU YLNLUA ZAYLLA KBYPUN AOPZ
      JVUCLYZHAPVU, HUK KY. TVYAPTLY, DPAO OPZ JVTWHUPVU, OHK SVUN
      CHUPZOLK PU MYVUA VM BZ.

      “AOLYL PZ UV VIQLJA PU VBY MVSSVDPUN AOLT,” ZHPK OVSTLZ. “AOL

      JHYKZ DL OHCL PU VBY OHUKZ HUK WSHF AOLT DPAO KLJPZPVU. JVBSK FVB
      ZDLHY AV AOHA THU’Z MHJL DPAOPU AOL JHI?”

      “P JVBSK ZDLHY VUSF AV AOL ILHYK.”

      “HUK ZV JVBSK P—MYVT DOPJO P NHAOLY AOHA PU HSS WYVIHIPSPAF PA
      DHZ H MHSZL VUL. H JSLCLY THU BWVU ZV KLSPJHAL HU LYYHUK OHZ UV
      BZL MVY H ILHYK ZHCL AV JVUJLHS OPZ MLHABYLZ. JVTL PU OLYL,
      DHAZVU!”

      OL ABYULK PUAV VUL VM AOL KPZAYPJA TLZZLUNLY VMMPJLZ, DOLYL OL
      DHZ DHYTSF NYLLALK IF AOL THUHNLY.

      “HO, DPSZVU, P ZLL FVB OHCL UVA MVYNVAALU AOL SPAASL JHZL PU

      “UV, ZPY, PUKLLK P OHCL UVA. FVB ZHCLK TF NVVK UHTL, HUK WLYOHWZ
      TF SPML.”

      “TF KLHY MLSSVD, FVB LEHNNLYHAL. P OHCL ZVTL YLJVSSLJAPVU,
      DPSZVU, AOHA FVB OHK HTVUN FVBY IVFZ H SHK UHTLK JHYADYPNOA, DOV

      “FLZ, ZPY, OL PZ ZAPSS DPAO BZ.”

      “JVBSK FVB YPUN OPT BW?—AOHUR FVB! HUK P ZOVBSK IL NSHK AV OHCL
      JOHUNL VM AOPZ MPCL-WVBUK UVAL.”

      H SHK VM MVBYALLU, DPAO H IYPNOA, RLLU MHJL, OHK VILFLK AOL
      ZBTTVUZ VM AOL THUHNLY. OL ZAVVK UVD NHGPUN DPAO NYLHA YLCLYLUJL

      “FLZ, ZPY.”

      “FVB DPSS CPZPA LHJO VM AOLZL PU ABYU.”

      “FLZ, ZPY.”

      “FVB DPSS ILNPU PU LHJO JHZL IF NPCPUN AOL VBAZPKL WVYALY VUL

      “FLZ, ZPY.”

      “FVB DPSS ALSS OPT AOHA FVB DHUA AV ZLL AOL DHZAL-WHWLY VM

      “FLZ, ZPY.”

      “IBA DOHA FVB HYL YLHSSF SVVRPUN MVY PZ AOL JLUAYL WHNL VM AOL

JOHWALY 5.
AOYLL IYVRLU AOYLHKZ


      ZOLYSVJR OVSTLZ OHK, PU H CLYF YLTHYRHISL KLNYLL, AOL WVDLY VM
      KLAHJOPUN OPZ TPUK HA DPSS. MVY ADV OVBYZ AOL ZAYHUNL IBZPULZZ PU
      DOPJO DL OHK ILLU PUCVSCLK HWWLHYLK AV IL MVYNVAALU, HUK OL DHZ
      LUAPYLSF HIZVYILK PU AOL WPJABYLZ VM AOL TVKLYU ILSNPHU THZALYZ.
      OL DVBSK AHSR VM UVAOPUN IBA HYA, VM DOPJO OL OHK AOL JYBKLZA
      PKLHZ, MYVT VBY SLHCPUN AOL NHSSLYF BUAPS DL MVBUK VBYZLSCLZ HA
      AOL UVYAOBTILYSHUK OVALS.

      “ZPY OLUYF IHZRLYCPSSL PZ BWZAHPYZ LEWLJAPUN FVB,” ZHPK AOL
      JSLYR. “OL HZRLK TL AV ZOVD FVB BW HA VUJL DOLU FVB JHTL.”

      “OHCL FVB HUF VIQLJAPVU AV TF SVVRPUN HA FVBY YLNPZALY?” ZHPK
      OVSTLZ.

      “UVA PU AOL SLHZA.”

      AOL IVVR ZOVDLK AOHA ADV UHTLZ OHK ILLU HKKLK HMALY AOHA VM
      IHZRLYCPSSL. VUL DHZ AOLVWOPSBZ QVOUZVU HUK MHTPSF, VM ULDJHZASL;
      AOL VAOLY TYZ. VSKTVYL HUK THPK, VM OPNO SVKNL, HSAVU.

      “ZBYLSF AOHA TBZA IL AOL ZHTL QVOUZVU DOVT P BZLK AV RUVD,” ZHPK
      OVSTLZ AV AOL WVYALY. “H SHDFLY, PZ OL UVA, NYLF-OLHKLK, HUK
      DHSRZ DPAO H SPTW?”

      “UV, ZPY, AOPZ PZ TY. QVOUZVU, AOL JVHS-VDULY, H CLYF HJAPCL
      NLUASLTHU, UVA VSKLY AOHU FVBYZLSM.”

      “ZBYLSF FVB HYL TPZAHRLU HIVBA OPZ AYHKL?”

      “UV, ZPY! OL OHZ BZLK AOPZ OVALS MVY THUF FLHYZ, HUK OL PZ CLYF
      DLSS RUVDU AV BZ.”

      “HO, AOHA ZLAASLZ PA. TYZ. VSKTVYL, AVV; P ZLLT AV YLTLTILY AOL
      UHTL. LEJBZL TF JBYPVZPAF, IBA VMALU PU JHSSPUN BWVU VUL MYPLUK
      VUL MPUKZ HUVAOLY.”

      “ZOL PZ HU PUCHSPK SHKF, ZPY. OLY OBZIHUK DHZ VUJL THFVY VM
      NSVBJLZALY. ZOL HSDHFZ JVTLZ AV BZ DOLU ZOL PZ PU AVDU.”

      “AOHUR FVB; P HT HMYHPK P JHUUVA JSHPT OLY HJXBHPUAHUJL. DL OHCL
      LZAHISPZOLK H TVZA PTWVYAHUA MHJA IF AOLZL XBLZAPVUZ, DHAZVU,” OL
      JVUAPUBLK PU H SVD CVPJL HZ DL DLUA BWZAHPYZ AVNLAOLY. “DL RUVD
      UVD AOHA AOL WLVWSL DOV HYL ZV PUALYLZALK PU VBY MYPLUK OHCL UVA
      ZLAASLK KVDU PU OPZ VDU OVALS. AOHA TLHUZ AOHA DOPSL AOLF HYL, HZ
      DL OHCL ZLLU, CLYF HUEPVBZ AV DHAJO OPT, AOLF HYL LXBHSSF HUEPVBZ
      AOHA OL ZOVBSK UVA ZLL AOLT. UVD, AOPZ PZ H TVZA ZBNNLZAPCL
      MHJA.”

      “DOHA KVLZ PA ZBNNLZA?”

      “PA ZBNNLZAZ—OHSSVH, TF KLHY MLSSVD, DOHA VU LHYAO PZ AOL
      THAALY?”

      HZ DL JHTL YVBUK AOL AVW VM AOL ZAHPYZ DL OHK YBU BW HNHPUZA ZPY
      OLUYF IHZRLYCPSSL OPTZLSM. OPZ MHJL DHZ MSBZOLK DPAO HUNLY, HUK
      OL OLSK HU VSK HUK KBZAF IVVA PU VUL VM OPZ OHUKZ. ZV MBYPVBZ DHZ

      OLHYK MYVT OPT PU AOL TVYUPUN.

      “ZAPSS SVVRPUN MVY FVBY IVVA?”

      “FLZ, ZPY, HUK TLHU AV MPUK PA.”

      “IBA, ZBYLSF, FVB ZHPK AOHA PA DHZ H ULD IYVDU IVVA?”

      “ZV PA DHZ, ZPY. HUK UVD PA’Z HU VSK ISHJR VUL.”

      “DOHA! FVB KVU’A TLHU AV ZHF—?”

      DL OHK H WSLHZHUA SBUJOLVU PU DOPJO SPAASL DHZ ZHPK VM AOL

      “AV NV AV IHZRLYCPSSL OHSS.”

      “HUK DOLU?”

      “HA AOL LUK VM AOL DLLR.”

      “AOHA PZ AYBL.”

      “KPK IHYYFTVYL WYVMPA HA HSS IF ZPY JOHYSLZ’Z DPSS?” HZRLK

      “OL HUK OPZ DPML OHK MPCL OBUKYLK WVBUKZ LHJO.”

      “OH! KPK AOLF RUVD AOHA AOLF DVBSK YLJLPCL AOPZ?”

      “FLZ; ZPY JOHYSLZ DHZ CLYF MVUK VM AHSRPUN HIVBA AOL WYVCPZPVUZ

      “AOHA PZ CLYF PUALYLZAPUN.”

      “P OVWL,” ZHPK KY. TVYAPTLY, “AOHA FVB KV UVA SVVR DPAO

      “AOLYL DLYL THUF PUZPNUPMPJHUA ZBTZ AV PUKPCPKBHSZ, HUK H SHYNL

      “HUK OVD TBJO DHZ AOL YLZPKBL?”

      “ZLCLU OBUKYLK HUK MVYAF AOVBZHUK WVBUKZ.”

      OVSTLZ YHPZLK OPZ LFLIYVDZ PU ZBYWYPZL. “P OHK UV PKLH AOHA ZV

      “KLHY TL! PA PZ H ZAHRL MVY DOPJO H THU TPNOA DLSS WSHF H

      “ZPUJL YVKNLY IHZRLYCPSSL, ZPY JOHYSLZ’Z FVBUNLY IYVAOLY KPLK

      “FLZ; OL VUJL JHTL KVDU AV CPZPA ZPY JOHYSLZ. OL PZ H THU VM

      “HUK AOPZ THU VM ZPTWSL AHZALZ DVBSK IL AOL OLPY AV ZPY JOHYSLZ’Z
      AOVBZHUKZ.”

      “OL DVBSK IL AOL OLPY AV AOL LZAHAL ILJHBZL AOHA PZ LUAHPSLK. OL
      DVBSK HSZV IL AOL OLPY AV AOL TVULF BUSLZZ PA DLYL DPSSLK
      VAOLYDPZL IF AOL WYLZLUA VDULY, DOV JHU, VM JVBYZL, KV DOHA OL
      SPRLZ DPAO PA.”

      “HUK OHCL FVB THKL FVBY DPSS, ZPY OLUYF?”

      “UV, TY. OVSTLZ, P OHCL UVA. P’CL OHK UV APTL, MVY PA DHZ VUSF
      FLZALYKHF AOHA P SLHYULK OVD THAALYZ ZAVVK. IBA PU HUF JHZL P
      MLLS AOHA AOL TVULF ZOVBSK NV DPAO AOL APASL HUK LZAHAL. AOHA DHZ

      NSVYPLZ VM AOL IHZRLYCPSSLZ PM OL OHZ UVA TVULF LUVBNO AV RLLW BW
      AOL WYVWLYAF? OVBZL, SHUK, HUK KVSSHYZ TBZA NV AVNLAOLY.”

      “XBPAL ZV. DLSS, ZPY OLUYF, P HT VM VUL TPUK DPAO FVB HZ AV AOL
      HKCPZHIPSPAF VM FVBY NVPUN KVDU AV KLCVUZOPYL DPAOVBA KLSHF.
      AOLYL PZ VUSF VUL WYVCPZPVU DOPJO P TBZA THRL. FVB JLYAHPUSF TBZA
      UVA NV HSVUL.”

      “KY. TVYAPTLY YLABYUZ DPAO TL.”

      “IBA KY. TVYAPTLY OHZ OPZ WYHJAPJL AV HAALUK AV, HUK OPZ OVBZL PZ

      WLYZVU; IBA FVB JHU BUKLYZAHUK AOHA, DPAO TF LEALUZPCL JVUZBSAPUN

      P.”

      “WLYMLJASF.”

      AOL NLYTHU DHZ ZLUA MVY IBA WYVMLZZLK AV RUVD UVAOPUN VM AOL
