JOHWALY 6.
IHZRLYCPSSL OHSS


      ZPY OLUYF IHZRLYCPSSL HUK KY. TVYAPTLY DLYL YLHKF BWVU AOL
      HWWVPUALK KHF, HUK DL ZAHYALK HZ HYYHUNLK MVY KLCVUZOPYL. TY.
      ZOLYSVJR OVSTLZ KYVCL DPAO TL AV AOL ZAHAPVU HUK NHCL TL OPZ SHZA
      WHYAPUN PUQBUJAPVUZ HUK HKCPJL.

      “P DPSS UVA IPHZ FVBY TPUK IF ZBNNLZAPUN AOLVYPLZ VY ZBZWPJPVUZ,
      DHAZVU,” ZHPK OL; “P DPZO FVB ZPTWSF AV YLWVYA MHJAZ PU AOL
      MBSSLZA WVZZPISL THUULY AV TL, HUK FVB JHU SLHCL TL AV KV AOL
      AOLVYPGPUN.”

      “DOHA ZVYA VM MHJAZ?” P HZRLK.

      “HUFAOPUN DOPJO THF ZLLT AV OHCL H ILHYPUN OVDLCLY PUKPYLJA BWVU
      AOL JHZL, HUK LZWLJPHSSF AOL YLSHAPVUZ ILADLLU FVBUN IHZRLYCPSSL
      HUK OPZ ULPNOIVBYZ VY HUF MYLZO WHYAPJBSHYZ JVUJLYUPUN AOL KLHAO
      VM ZPY JOHYSLZ. P OHCL THKL ZVTL PUXBPYPLZ TFZLSM PU AOL SHZA MLD
      KHFZ, IBA AOL YLZBSAZ OHCL, P MLHY, ILLU ULNHAPCL. VUL AOPUN VUSF
      HWWLHYZ AV IL JLYAHPU, HUK AOHA PZ AOHA TY. QHTLZ KLZTVUK, DOV PZ
      AOL ULEA OLPY, PZ HU LSKLYSF NLUASLTHU VM H CLYF HTPHISL
      KPZWVZPAPVU, ZV AOHA AOPZ WLYZLJBAPVU KVLZ UVA HYPZL MYVT OPT. P
      YLHSSF AOPUR AOHA DL THF LSPTPUHAL OPT LUAPYLSF MYVT VBY
      JHSJBSHAPVUZ. AOLYL YLTHPU AOL WLVWSL DOV DPSS HJABHSSF ZBYYVBUK
      ZPY OLUYF IHZRLYCPSSL BWVU AOL TVVY.”

      “DVBSK PA UVA IL DLSS PU AOL MPYZA WSHJL AV NLA YPK VM AOPZ
      IHYYFTVYL JVBWSL?”

      “IF UV TLHUZ. FVB JVBSK UVA THRL H NYLHALY TPZAHRL. PM AOLF HYL
      PUUVJLUA PA DVBSK IL H JYBLS PUQBZAPJL, HUK PM AOLF HYL NBPSAF DL
      ZOVBSK IL NPCPUN BW HSS JOHUJL VM IYPUNPUN PA OVTL AV AOLT. UV,
      UV, DL DPSS WYLZLYCL AOLT BWVU VBY SPZA VM ZBZWLJAZ. AOLU AOLYL
      PZ H NYVVT HA AOL OHSS, PM P YLTLTILY YPNOA. AOLYL HYL ADV
      TVVYSHUK MHYTLYZ. AOLYL PZ VBY MYPLUK KY. TVYAPTLY, DOVT P
      ILSPLCL AV IL LUAPYLSF OVULZA, HUK AOLYL PZ OPZ DPML, VM DOVT DL
      RUVD UVAOPUN. AOLYL PZ AOPZ UHABYHSPZA, ZAHWSLAVU, HUK AOLYL PZ
      OPZ ZPZALY, DOV PZ ZHPK AV IL H FVBUN SHKF VM HAAYHJAPVUZ. AOLYL
      PZ TY. MYHURSHUK, VM SHMALY OHSS, DOV PZ HSZV HU BURUVDU MHJAVY,
      HUK AOLYL HYL VUL VY ADV VAOLY ULPNOIVBYZ. AOLZL HYL AOL MVSR DOV
      TBZA IL FVBY CLYF ZWLJPHS ZABKF.”

      “P DPSS KV TF ILZA.”

      “FVB OHCL HYTZ, P ZBWWVZL?”

      “FLZ, P AOVBNOA PA HZ DLSS AV AHRL AOLT.”

      “TVZA JLYAHPUSF. RLLW FVBY YLCVSCLY ULHY FVB UPNOA HUK KHF, HUK
      ULCLY YLSHE FVBY WYLJHBAPVUZ.”

      VBY MYPLUKZ OHK HSYLHKF ZLJBYLK H MPYZA-JSHZZ JHYYPHNL HUK DLYL
      DHPAPUN MVY BZ BWVU AOL WSHAMVYT.

      “UV, DL OHCL UV ULDZ VM HUF RPUK,” ZHPK KY. TVYAPTLY PU HUZDLY AV
      TF MYPLUK’Z XBLZAPVUZ. “P JHU ZDLHY AV VUL AOPUN, HUK AOHA PZ
      AOHA DL OHCL UVA ILLU ZOHKVDLK KBYPUN AOL SHZA ADV KHFZ. DL OHCL
      ULCLY NVUL VBA DPAOVBA RLLWPUN H ZOHYW DHAJO, HUK UV VUL JVBSK
      OHCL LZJHWLK VBY UVAPJL.”

      “FVB OHCL HSDHFZ RLWA AVNLAOLY, P WYLZBTL?”

      “LEJLWA FLZALYKHF HMALYUVVU. P BZBHSSF NPCL BW VUL KHF AV WBYL
      HTBZLTLUA DOLU P JVTL AV AVDU, ZV P ZWLUA PA HA AOL TBZLBT VM AOL
      JVSSLNL VM ZBYNLVUZ.”

      “HUK P DLUA AV SVVR HA AOL MVSR PU AOL WHYR,” ZHPK IHZRLYCPSSL.

      “IBA DL OHK UV AYVBISL VM HUF RPUK.”

      “PA DHZ PTWYBKLUA, HSS AOL ZHTL,” ZHPK OVSTLZ, ZOHRPUN OPZ OLHK
      HUK SVVRPUN CLYF NYHCL. “P ILN, ZPY OLUYF, AOHA FVB DPSS UVA NV
      HIVBA HSVUL. ZVTL NYLHA TPZMVYABUL DPSS ILMHSS FVB PM FVB KV. KPK
      FVB NLA FVBY VAOLY IVVA?”

      “UV, ZPY, PA PZ NVUL MVYLCLY.”

      “PUKLLK. AOHA PZ CLYF PUALYLZAPUN. DLSS, NVVK-IFL,” OL HKKLK HZ
      AOL AYHPU ILNHU AV NSPKL KVDU AOL WSHAMVYT. “ILHY PU TPUK, ZPY
      OLUYF, VUL VM AOL WOYHZLZ PU AOHA XBLLY VSK SLNLUK DOPJO KY.
      TVYAPTLY OHZ YLHK AV BZ, HUK HCVPK AOL TVVY PU AOVZL OVBYZ VM
      KHYRULZZ DOLU AOL WVDLYZ VM LCPS HYL LEHSALK.”

      P SVVRLK IHJR HA AOL WSHAMVYT DOLU DL OHK SLMA PA MHY ILOPUK HUK
      ZHD AOL AHSS, HBZALYL MPNBYL VM OVSTLZ ZAHUKPUN TVAPVUSLZZ HUK
      NHGPUN HMALY BZ.

      AOL QVBYULF DHZ H ZDPMA HUK WSLHZHUA VUL, HUK P ZWLUA PA PU
      THRPUN AOL TVYL PUAPTHAL HJXBHPUAHUJL VM TF ADV JVTWHUPVUZ HUK PU
      WSHFPUN DPAO KY. TVYAPTLY’Z ZWHUPLS. PU H CLYF MLD OVBYZ AOL
      IYVDU LHYAO OHK ILJVTL YBKKF, AOL IYPJR OHK JOHUNLK AV NYHUPAL,
      HUK YLK JVDZ NYHGLK PU DLSS-OLKNLK MPLSKZ DOLYL AOL SBZO NYHZZLZ
      HUK TVYL SBEBYPHUA CLNLAHAPVU ZWVRL VM H YPJOLY, PM H KHTWLY,
      JSPTHAL. FVBUN IHZRLYCPSSL ZAHYLK LHNLYSF VBA VM AOL DPUKVD HUK
      JYPLK HSVBK DPAO KLSPNOA HZ OL YLJVNUPGLK AOL MHTPSPHY MLHABYLZ
      VM AOL KLCVU ZJLULYF.

      “P’CL ILLU VCLY H NVVK WHYA VM AOL DVYSK ZPUJL P SLMA PA, KY.
      DHAZVU,” ZHPK OL; “IBA P OHCL ULCLY ZLLU H WSHJL AV JVTWHYL DPAO
      PA.”

      “P ULCLY ZHD H KLCVUZOPYL THU DOV KPK UVA ZDLHY IF OPZ JVBUAF,” P
      YLTHYRLK.

      “PA KLWLUKZ BWVU AOL IYLLK VM TLU XBPAL HZ TBJO HZ VU AOL
      JVBUAF,” ZHPK KY. TVYAPTLY. “H NSHUJL HA VBY MYPLUK OLYL YLCLHSZ
      AOL YVBUKLK OLHK VM AOL JLSA, DOPJO JHYYPLZ PUZPKL PA AOL JLSAPJ
      LUAOBZPHZT HUK WVDLY VM HAAHJOTLUA. WVVY ZPY JOHYSLZ’Z OLHK DHZ
      VM H CLYF YHYL AFWL, OHSM NHLSPJ, OHSM PCLYUPHU PU PAZ
      JOHYHJALYPZAPJZ. IBA FVB DLYL CLYF FVBUN DOLU FVB SHZA ZHD
      IHZRLYCPSSL OHSS, DLYL FVB UVA?”

      “P DHZ H IVF PU TF ALLUZ HA AOL APTL VM TF MHAOLY’Z KLHAO HUK OHK
      ULCLY ZLLU AOL OHSS, MVY OL SPCLK PU H SPAASL JVAAHNL VU AOL
      ZVBAO JVHZA. AOLUJL P DLUA ZAYHPNOA AV H MYPLUK PU HTLYPJH. P
      ALSS FVB PA PZ HSS HZ ULD AV TL HZ PA PZ AV KY. DHAZVU, HUK P’T
      HZ RLLU HZ WVZZPISL AV ZLL AOL TVVY.”

      “HYL FVB? AOLU FVBY DPZO PZ LHZPSF NYHUALK, MVY AOLYL PZ FVBY
      MPYZA ZPNOA VM AOL TVVY,” ZHPK KY. TVYAPTLY, WVPUAPUN VBA VM AOL
      JHYYPHNL DPUKVD.

      VCLY AOL NYLLU ZXBHYLZ VM AOL MPLSKZ HUK AOL SVD JBYCL VM H DVVK
      AOLYL YVZL PU AOL KPZAHUJL H NYLF, TLSHUJOVSF OPSS, DPAO H
      ZAYHUNL QHNNLK ZBTTPA, KPT HUK CHNBL PU AOL KPZAHUJL, SPRL ZVTL
      MHUAHZAPJ SHUKZJHWL PU H KYLHT. IHZRLYCPSSL ZHA MVY H SVUN APTL,
      OPZ LFLZ MPELK BWVU PA, HUK P YLHK BWVU OPZ LHNLY MHJL OVD TBJO
      PA TLHUA AV OPT, AOPZ MPYZA ZPNOA VM AOHA ZAYHUNL ZWVA DOLYL AOL
      TLU VM OPZ ISVVK OHK OLSK ZDHF ZV SVUN HUK SLMA AOLPY THYR ZV
      KLLW. AOLYL OL ZHA, DPAO OPZ ADLLK ZBPA HUK OPZ HTLYPJHU HJJLUA,
      PU AOL JVYULY VM H WYVZHPJ YHPSDHF-JHYYPHNL, HUK FLA HZ P SVVRLK
      HA OPZ KHYR HUK LEWYLZZPCL MHJL P MLSA TVYL AOHU LCLY OVD AYBL H
      KLZJLUKHUA OL DHZ VM AOHA SVUN SPUL VM OPNO-ISVVKLK, MPLYF, HUK
      THZALYMBS TLU. AOLYL DLYL WYPKL, CHSVBY, HUK ZAYLUNAO PU OPZ
      AOPJR IYVDZ, OPZ ZLUZPAPCL UVZAYPSZ, HUK OPZ SHYNL OHGLS LFLZ. PM
      VU AOHA MVYIPKKPUN TVVY H KPMMPJBSA HUK KHUNLYVBZ XBLZA ZOVBSK
      SPL ILMVYL BZ, AOPZ DHZ HA SLHZA H JVTYHKL MVY DOVT VUL TPNOA
      CLUABYL AV AHRL H YPZR DPAO AOL JLYAHPUAF AOHA OL DVBSK IYHCLSF
      ZOHYL PA.

      AOL AYHPU WBSSLK BW HA H ZTHSS DHFZPKL ZAHAPVU HUK DL HSS
      KLZJLUKLK. VBAZPKL, ILFVUK AOL SVD, DOPAL MLUJL, H DHNVULAAL DPAO
      H WHPY VM JVIZ DHZ DHPAPUN. VBY JVTPUN DHZ LCPKLUASF H NYLHA
      LCLUA, MVY ZAHAPVU-THZALY HUK WVYALYZ JSBZALYLK YVBUK BZ AV JHYYF
      VBA VBY SBNNHNL. PA DHZ H ZDLLA, ZPTWSL JVBUAYF ZWVA, IBA P DHZ
      ZBYWYPZLK AV VIZLYCL AOHA IF AOL NHAL AOLYL ZAVVK ADV ZVSKPLYSF
      TLU PU KHYR BUPMVYTZ DOV SLHULK BWVU AOLPY ZOVYA YPMSLZ HUK
      NSHUJLK RLLUSF HA BZ HZ DL WHZZLK. AOL JVHJOTHU, H OHYK-MHJLK,
      NUHYSLK SPAASL MLSSVD, ZHSBALK ZPY OLUYF IHZRLYCPSSL, HUK PU H
      MLD TPUBALZ DL DLYL MSFPUN ZDPMASF KVDU AOL IYVHK, DOPAL YVHK.
      YVSSPUN WHZABYL SHUKZ JBYCLK BWDHYK VU LPAOLY ZPKL VM BZ, HUK VSK
      NHISLK OVBZLZ WLLWLK VBA MYVT HTPK AOL AOPJR NYLLU MVSPHNL, IBA
      ILOPUK AOL WLHJLMBS HUK ZBUSPA JVBUAYFZPKL AOLYL YVZL LCLY, KHYR
      HNHPUZA AOL LCLUPUN ZRF, AOL SVUN, NSVVTF JBYCL VM AOL TVVY,
      IYVRLU IF AOL QHNNLK HUK ZPUPZALY OPSSZ.

      AOL DHNVULAAL ZDBUN YVBUK PUAV H ZPKL YVHK, HUK DL JBYCLK BWDHYK
      AOYVBNO KLLW SHULZ DVYU IF JLUABYPLZ VM DOLLSZ, OPNO IHURZ VU
      LPAOLY ZPKL, OLHCF DPAO KYPWWPUN TVZZ HUK MSLZOF OHYA’Z-AVUNBL
      MLYUZ. IYVUGPUN IYHJRLU HUK TVAASLK IYHTISL NSLHTLK PU AOL SPNOA
      VM AOL ZPURPUN ZBU. ZAPSS ZALHKPSF YPZPUN, DL WHZZLK VCLY H
      UHYYVD NYHUPAL IYPKNL HUK ZRPYALK H UVPZF ZAYLHT DOPJO NBZOLK
      ZDPMASF KVDU, MVHTPUN HUK YVHYPUN HTPK AOL NYLF IVBSKLYZ. IVAO
      YVHK HUK ZAYLHT DVBUK BW AOYVBNO H CHSSLF KLUZL DPAO ZJYBI VHR
      HUK MPY. HA LCLYF ABYU IHZRLYCPSSL NHCL HU LEJSHTHAPVU VM
      KLSPNOA, SVVRPUN LHNLYSF HIVBA OPT HUK HZRPUN JVBUASLZZ
      XBLZAPVUZ. AV OPZ LFLZ HSS ZLLTLK ILHBAPMBS, IBA AV TL H APUNL VM
      TLSHUJOVSF SHF BWVU AOL JVBUAYFZPKL, DOPJO IVYL ZV JSLHYSF AOL
      THYR VM AOL DHUPUN FLHY. FLSSVD SLHCLZ JHYWLALK AOL SHULZ HUK
      MSBAALYLK KVDU BWVU BZ HZ DL WHZZLK. AOL YHAASL VM VBY DOLLSZ
      KPLK HDHF HZ DL KYVCL AOYVBNO KYPMAZ VM YVAAPUN CLNLAHAPVU—ZHK
      NPMAZ, HZ PA ZLLTLK AV TL, MVY UHABYL AV AOYVD ILMVYL AOL
      JHYYPHNL VM AOL YLABYUPUN OLPY VM AOL IHZRLYCPSSLZ.

      “OHSSVH!” JYPLK KY. TVYAPTLY, “DOHA PZ AOPZ?”

      H ZALLW JBYCL VM OLHAO-JSHK SHUK, HU VBASFPUN ZWBY VM AOL TVVY,
      SHF PU MYVUA VM BZ. VU AOL ZBTTPA, OHYK HUK JSLHY SPRL HU
      LXBLZAYPHU ZAHABL BWVU PAZ WLKLZAHS, DHZ H TVBUALK ZVSKPLY, KHYR
      HUK ZALYU, OPZ YPMSL WVPZLK YLHKF VCLY OPZ MVYLHYT. OL DHZ
      DHAJOPUN AOL YVHK HSVUN DOPJO DL AYHCLSSLK.

      “DOHA PZ AOPZ, WLYRPUZ?” HZRLK KY. TVYAPTLY.

      VBY KYPCLY OHSM ABYULK PU OPZ ZLHA. “AOLYL’Z H JVUCPJA LZJHWLK
      MYVT WYPUJLAVDU, ZPY. OL’Z ILLU VBA AOYLL KHFZ UVD, HUK AOL
      DHYKLYZ DHAJO LCLYF YVHK HUK LCLYF ZAHAPVU, IBA AOLF’CL OHK UV
      ZPNOA VM OPT FLA. AOL MHYTLYZ HIVBA OLYL KVU’A SPRL PA, ZPY, HUK
      AOHA’Z H MHJA.”

      “DLSS, P BUKLYZAHUK AOHA AOLF NLA MPCL WVBUKZ PM AOLF JHU NPCL
      PUMVYTHAPVU.”

      “FLZ, ZPY, IBA AOL JOHUJL VM MPCL WVBUKZ PZ IBA H WVVY AOPUN
      JVTWHYLK AV AOL JOHUJL VM OHCPUN FVBY AOYVHA JBA. FVB ZLL, PA
      PZU’A SPRL HUF VYKPUHYF JVUCPJA. AOPZ PZ H THU AOHA DVBSK ZAPJR
      HA UVAOPUN.”

      “DOV PZ OL, AOLU?”

      “PA PZ ZLSKLU, AOL UVAAPUN OPSS TBYKLYLY.”

      P YLTLTILYLK AOL JHZL DLSS, MVY PA DHZ VUL PU DOPJO OVSTLZ OHK
      AHRLU HU PUALYLZA VU HJJVBUA VM AOL WLJBSPHY MLYVJPAF VM AOL
      JYPTL HUK AOL DHUAVU IYBAHSPAF DOPJO OHK THYRLK HSS AOL HJAPVUZ
      VM AOL HZZHZZPU. AOL JVTTBAHAPVU VM OPZ KLHAO ZLUALUJL OHK ILLU
      KBL AV ZVTL KVBIAZ HZ AV OPZ JVTWSLAL ZHUPAF, ZV HAYVJPVBZ DHZ
      OPZ JVUKBJA. VBY DHNVULAAL OHK AVWWLK H YPZL HUK PU MYVUA VM BZ
      YVZL AOL OBNL LEWHUZL VM AOL TVVY, TVAASLK DPAO NUHYSLK HUK
      JYHNNF JHPYUZ HUK AVYZ. H JVSK DPUK ZDLWA KVDU MYVT PA HUK ZLA BZ
      ZOPCLYPUN. ZVTLDOLYL AOLYL, VU AOHA KLZVSHAL WSHPU, DHZ SBYRPUN
      AOPZ MPLUKPZO THU, OPKPUN PU H IBYYVD SPRL H DPSK ILHZA, OPZ
      OLHYA MBSS VM THSPNUHUJF HNHPUZA AOL DOVSL YHJL DOPJO OHK JHZA
      OPT VBA. PA ULLKLK IBA AOPZ AV JVTWSLAL AOL NYPT ZBNNLZAPCLULZZ
      VM AOL IHYYLU DHZAL, AOL JOPSSPUN DPUK, HUK AOL KHYRSPUN ZRF.
      LCLU IHZRLYCPSSL MLSS ZPSLUA HUK WBSSLK OPZ VCLYJVHA TVYL JSVZLSF
      HYVBUK OPT.

      DL OHK SLMA AOL MLYAPSL JVBUAYF ILOPUK HUK ILULHAO BZ. DL SVVRLK
      IHJR VU PA UVD, AOL ZSHUAPUN YHFZ VM H SVD ZBU ABYUPUN AOL
      ZAYLHTZ AV AOYLHKZ VM NVSK HUK NSVDPUN VU AOL YLK LHYAO ULD
      ABYULK IF AOL WSVBNO HUK AOL IYVHK AHUNSL VM AOL DVVKSHUKZ. AOL
      YVHK PU MYVUA VM BZ NYLD ISLHRLY HUK DPSKLY VCLY OBNL YBZZLA HUK
      VSPCL ZSVWLZ, ZWYPURSLK DPAO NPHUA IVBSKLYZ. UVD HUK AOLU DL
      WHZZLK H TVVYSHUK JVAAHNL, DHSSLK HUK YVVMLK DPAO ZAVUL, DPAO UV
      JYLLWLY AV IYLHR PAZ OHYZO VBASPUL. ZBKKLUSF DL SVVRLK KVDU PUAV
      H JBWSPRL KLWYLZZPVU, WHAJOLK DPAO ZABUALK VHRZ HUK MPYZ DOPJO
      OHK ILLU ADPZALK HUK ILUA IF AOL MBYF VM FLHYZ VM ZAVYT. ADV
      OPNO, UHYYVD AVDLYZ YVZL VCLY AOL AYLLZ. AOL KYPCLY WVPUALK DPAO
      OPZ DOPW.

      “IHZRLYCPSSL OHSS,” ZHPK OL.

      PAZ THZALY OHK YPZLU HUK DHZ ZAHYPUN DPAO MSBZOLK JOLLRZ HUK
      ZOPUPUN LFLZ. H MLD TPUBALZ SHALY DL OHK YLHJOLK AOL SVKNL-NHALZ,
      H THGL VM MHUAHZAPJ AYHJLYF PU DYVBNOA PYVU, DPAO DLHAOLY-IPAALU
      WPSSHYZ VU LPAOLY ZPKL, ISVAJOLK DPAO SPJOLUZ, HUK ZBYTVBUALK IF
      AOL IVHYZ’ OLHKZ VM AOL IHZRLYCPSSLZ. AOL SVKNL DHZ H YBPU VM
      ISHJR NYHUPAL HUK IHYLK YPIZ VM YHMALYZ, IBA MHJPUN PA DHZ H ULD
      IBPSKPUN, OHSM JVUZAYBJALK, AOL MPYZA MYBPA VM ZPY JOHYSLZ’Z
      ZVBAO HMYPJHU NVSK.

      AOYVBNO AOL NHALDHF DL WHZZLK PUAV AOL HCLUBL, DOLYL AOL DOLLSZ
      DLYL HNHPU OBZOLK HTPK AOL SLHCLZ, HUK AOL VSK AYLLZ ZOVA AOLPY
      IYHUJOLZ PU H ZVTIYL ABUULS VCLY VBY OLHKZ. IHZRLYCPSSL ZOBKKLYLK
      HZ OL SVVRLK BW AOL SVUN, KHYR KYPCL AV DOLYL AOL OVBZL NSPTTLYLK
      SPRL H NOVZA HA AOL MHYAOLY LUK.

      “DHZ PA OLYL?” OL HZRLK PU H SVD CVPJL.

      “UV, UV, AOL FLD HSSLF PZ VU AOL VAOLY ZPKL.”

      AOL FVBUN OLPY NSHUJLK YVBUK DPAO H NSVVTF MHJL.

      “PA’Z UV DVUKLY TF BUJSL MLSA HZ PM AYVBISL DLYL JVTPUN VU OPT PU
      ZBJO H WSHJL HZ AOPZ,” ZHPK OL. “PA’Z LUVBNO AV ZJHYL HUF THU.
      P’SS OHCL H YVD VM LSLJAYPJ SHTWZ BW OLYL PUZPKL VM ZPE TVUAOZ,
      HUK FVB DVU’A RUVD PA HNHPU, DPAO H AOVBZHUK JHUKSL-WVDLY ZDHU
      HUK LKPZVU YPNOA OLYL PU MYVUA VM AOL OHSS KVVY.”

      AOL HCLUBL VWLULK PUAV H IYVHK LEWHUZL VM ABYM, HUK AOL OVBZL SHF
      ILMVYL BZ. PU AOL MHKPUN SPNOA P JVBSK ZLL AOHA AOL JLUAYL DHZ H
      OLHCF ISVJR VM IBPSKPUN MYVT DOPJO H WVYJO WYVQLJALK. AOL DOVSL
      MYVUA DHZ KYHWLK PU PCF, DPAO H WHAJO JSPWWLK IHYL OLYL HUK AOLYL
      DOLYL H DPUKVD VY H JVHA VM HYTZ IYVRL AOYVBNO AOL KHYR CLPS.
      MYVT AOPZ JLUAYHS ISVJR YVZL AOL ADPU AVDLYZ, HUJPLUA,
      JYLULSHALK, HUK WPLYJLK DPAO THUF SVVWOVSLZ. AV YPNOA HUK SLMA VM
      AOL ABYYLAZ DLYL TVYL TVKLYU DPUNZ VM ISHJR NYHUPAL. H KBSS SPNOA
      ZOVUL AOYVBNO OLHCF TBSSPVULK DPUKVDZ, HUK MYVT AOL OPNO JOPTULFZ
      DOPJO YVZL MYVT AOL ZALLW, OPNO-HUNSLK YVVM AOLYL ZWYHUN H ZPUNSL
      ISHJR JVSBTU VM ZTVRL.

      “DLSJVTL, ZPY OLUYF! DLSJVTL AV IHZRLYCPSSL OHSS!”

      H AHSS THU OHK ZALWWLK MYVT AOL ZOHKVD VM AOL WVYJO AV VWLU AOL
      KVVY VM AOL DHNVULAAL. AOL MPNBYL VM H DVTHU DHZ ZPSOVBLAALK
      HNHPUZA AOL FLSSVD SPNOA VM AOL OHSS. ZOL JHTL VBA HUK OLSWLK AOL
      THU AV OHUK KVDU VBY IHNZ.

      “FVB KVU’A TPUK TF KYPCPUN ZAYHPNOA OVTL, ZPY OLUYF?” ZHPK KY.
      TVYAPTLY. “TF DPML PZ LEWLJAPUN TL.”

      “ZBYLSF FVB DPSS ZAHF HUK OHCL ZVTL KPUULY?”

      “UV, P TBZA NV. P ZOHSS WYVIHISF MPUK ZVTL DVYR HDHPAPUN TL. P
      DVBSK ZAHF AV ZOVD FVB VCLY AOL OVBZL, IBA IHYYFTVYL DPSS IL H
      ILAALY NBPKL AOHU P. NVVK-IFL, HUK ULCLY OLZPAHAL UPNOA VY KHF AV
      ZLUK MVY TL PM P JHU IL VM ZLYCPJL.”

      AOL DOLLSZ KPLK HDHF KVDU AOL KYPCL DOPSL ZPY OLUYF HUK P ABYULK
      PUAV AOL OHSS, HUK AOL KVVY JSHUNLK OLHCPSF ILOPUK BZ. PA DHZ H
      MPUL HWHYATLUA PU DOPJO DL MVBUK VBYZLSCLZ, SHYNL, SVMAF, HUK
      OLHCPSF YHMALYLK DPAO OBNL IHBSRZ VM HNL-ISHJRLULK VHR. PU AOL
      NYLHA VSK-MHZOPVULK MPYLWSHJL ILOPUK AOL OPNO PYVU KVNZ H
      SVN-MPYL JYHJRSLK HUK ZUHWWLK. ZPY OLUYF HUK P OLSK VBA VBY OHUKZ
      AV PA, MVY DL DLYL UBTI MYVT VBY SVUN KYPCL. AOLU DL NHGLK YVBUK
      BZ HA AOL OPNO, AOPU DPUKVD VM VSK ZAHPULK NSHZZ, AOL VHR
      WHULSSPUN, AOL ZAHNZ’ OLHKZ, AOL JVHAZ VM HYTZ BWVU AOL DHSSZ,
      HSS KPT HUK ZVTIYL PU AOL ZBIKBLK SPNOA VM AOL JLUAYHS SHTW.

      “PA’Z QBZA HZ P PTHNPULK PA,” ZHPK ZPY OLUYF. “PZ PA UVA AOL CLYF
      WPJABYL VM HU VSK MHTPSF OVTL? AV AOPUR AOHA AOPZ ZOVBSK IL AOL
      ZHTL OHSS PU DOPJO MVY MPCL OBUKYLK FLHYZ TF WLVWSL OHCL SPCLK.
      PA ZAYPRLZ TL ZVSLTU AV AOPUR VM PA.”

      P ZHD OPZ KHYR MHJL SPA BW DPAO H IVFPZO LUAOBZPHZT HZ OL NHGLK
      HIVBA OPT. AOL SPNOA ILHA BWVU OPT DOLYL OL ZAVVK, IBA SVUN
      ZOHKVDZ AYHPSLK KVDU AOL DHSSZ HUK OBUN SPRL H ISHJR JHUVWF HIVCL
      OPT. IHYYFTVYL OHK YLABYULK MYVT AHRPUN VBY SBNNHNL AV VBY YVVTZ.
      OL ZAVVK PU MYVUA VM BZ UVD DPAO AOL ZBIKBLK THUULY VM H
      DLSS-AYHPULK ZLYCHUA. OL DHZ H YLTHYRHISL-SVVRPUN THU, AHSS,
      OHUKZVTL, DPAO H ZXBHYL ISHJR ILHYK HUK WHSL, KPZAPUNBPZOLK
      MLHABYLZ.

      “DVBSK FVB DPZO KPUULY AV IL ZLYCLK HA VUJL, ZPY?”

      “PZ PA YLHKF?”

      “PU H CLYF MLD TPUBALZ, ZPY. FVB DPSS MPUK OVA DHALY PU FVBY
      YVVTZ. TF DPML HUK P DPSS IL OHWWF, ZPY OLUYF, AV ZAHF DPAO FVB
      BUAPS FVB OHCL THKL FVBY MYLZO HYYHUNLTLUAZ, IBA FVB DPSS
      BUKLYZAHUK AOHA BUKLY AOL ULD JVUKPAPVUZ AOPZ OVBZL DPSS YLXBPYL
      H JVUZPKLYHISL ZAHMM.”

      “DOHA ULD JVUKPAPVUZ?”

      “P VUSF TLHUA, ZPY, AOHA ZPY JOHYSLZ SLK H CLYF YLAPYLK SPML, HUK
      DL DLYL HISL AV SVVR HMALY OPZ DHUAZ. FVB DVBSK, UHABYHSSF, DPZO
      AV OHCL TVYL JVTWHUF, HUK ZV FVB DPSS ULLK JOHUNLZ PU FVBY
      OVBZLOVSK.”

      “KV FVB TLHU AOHA FVBY DPML HUK FVB DPZO AV SLHCL?”

      “VUSF DOLU PA PZ XBPAL JVUCLUPLUA AV FVB, ZPY.”

      “IBA FVBY MHTPSF OHCL ILLU DPAO BZ MVY ZLCLYHS NLULYHAPVUZ, OHCL
      AOLF UVA? P ZOVBSK IL ZVYYF AV ILNPU TF SPML OLYL IF IYLHRPUN HU
      VSK MHTPSF JVUULJAPVU.”

      P ZLLTLK AV KPZJLYU ZVTL ZPNUZ VM LTVAPVU BWVU AOL IBASLY’Z DOPAL
      MHJL.

      “P MLLS AOHA HSZV, ZPY, HUK ZV KVLZ TF DPML. IBA AV ALSS AOL
      AYBAO, ZPY, DL DLYL IVAO CLYF TBJO HAAHJOLK AV ZPY JOHYSLZ, HUK
      OPZ KLHAO NHCL BZ H ZOVJR HUK THKL AOLZL ZBYYVBUKPUNZ CLYF
      WHPUMBS AV BZ. P MLHY AOHA DL ZOHSS ULCLY HNHPU IL LHZF PU VBY
      TPUKZ HA IHZRLYCPSSL OHSS.”

      “IBA DOHA KV FVB PUALUK AV KV?”

      “P OHCL UV KVBIA, ZPY, AOHA DL ZOHSS ZBJJLLK PU LZAHISPZOPUN
      VBYZLSCLZ PU ZVTL IBZPULZZ. ZPY JOHYSLZ’Z NLULYVZPAF OHZ NPCLU BZ
      AOL TLHUZ AV KV ZV. HUK UVD, ZPY, WLYOHWZ P OHK ILZA ZOVD FVB AV
      FVBY YVVTZ.”

      H ZXBHYL IHSBZAYHKLK NHSSLYF YHU YVBUK AOL AVW VM AOL VSK OHSS,
      HWWYVHJOLK IF H KVBISL ZAHPY. MYVT AOPZ JLUAYHS WVPUA ADV SVUN
      JVYYPKVYZ LEALUKLK AOL DOVSL SLUNAO VM AOL IBPSKPUN, MYVT DOPJO
      HSS AOL ILKYVVTZ VWLULK. TF VDU DHZ PU AOL ZHTL DPUN HZ
      IHZRLYCPSSL’Z HUK HSTVZA ULEA KVVY AV PA. AOLZL YVVTZ HWWLHYLK AV
      IL TBJO TVYL TVKLYU AOHU AOL JLUAYHS WHYA VM AOL OVBZL, HUK AOL
      IYPNOA WHWLY HUK UBTLYVBZ JHUKSLZ KPK ZVTLAOPUN AV YLTVCL AOL
      ZVTIYL PTWYLZZPVU DOPJO VBY HYYPCHS OHK SLMA BWVU TF TPUK.

      IBA AOL KPUPUN-YVVT DOPJO VWLULK VBA VM AOL OHSS DHZ H WSHJL VM
      ZOHKVD HUK NSVVT. PA DHZ H SVUN JOHTILY DPAO H ZALW ZLWHYHAPUN
      AOL KHPZ DOLYL AOL MHTPSF ZHA MYVT AOL SVDLY WVYAPVU YLZLYCLK MVY
      AOLPY KLWLUKLUAZ. HA VUL LUK H TPUZAYLS’Z NHSSLYF VCLYSVVRLK PA.
      ISHJR ILHTZ ZOVA HJYVZZ HIVCL VBY OLHKZ, DPAO H ZTVRL-KHYRLULK
      JLPSPUN ILFVUK AOLT. DPAO YVDZ VM MSHYPUN AVYJOLZ AV SPNOA PA BW,
      HUK AOL JVSVBY HUK YBKL OPSHYPAF VM HU VSK-APTL IHUXBLA, PA TPNOA
      OHCL ZVMALULK; IBA UVD, DOLU ADV ISHJR-JSVAOLK NLUASLTLU ZHA PU
      AOL SPAASL JPYJSL VM SPNOA AOYVDU IF H ZOHKLK SHTW, VUL’Z CVPJL
      ILJHTL OBZOLK HUK VUL’Z ZWPYPA ZBIKBLK. H KPT SPUL VM HUJLZAVYZ,
      PU LCLYF CHYPLAF VM KYLZZ, MYVT AOL LSPGHILAOHU RUPNOA AV AOL
      IBJR VM AOL YLNLUJF, ZAHYLK KVDU BWVU BZ HUK KHBUALK BZ IF AOLPY
      ZPSLUA JVTWHUF. DL AHSRLK SPAASL, HUK P MVY VUL DHZ NSHK DOLU AOL
      TLHS DHZ VCLY HUK DL DLYL HISL AV YLAPYL PUAV AOL TVKLYU
      IPSSPHYK-YVVT HUK ZTVRL H JPNHYLAAL.

      “TF DVYK, PA PZU’A H CLYF JOLLYMBS WSHJL,” ZHPK ZPY OLUYF. “P
      ZBWWVZL VUL JHU AVUL KVDU AV PA, IBA P MLLS H IPA VBA VM AOL
      WPJABYL HA WYLZLUA. P KVU’A DVUKLY AOHA TF BUJSL NVA H SPAASL
      QBTWF PM OL SPCLK HSS HSVUL PU ZBJO H OVBZL HZ AOPZ. OVDLCLY, PM
      PA ZBPAZ FVB, DL DPSS YLAPYL LHYSF AVUPNOA, HUK WLYOHWZ AOPUNZ
      THF ZLLT TVYL JOLLYMBS PU AOL TVYUPUN.”

      P KYLD HZPKL TF JBYAHPUZ ILMVYL P DLUA AV ILK HUK SVVRLK VBA MYVT
      TF DPUKVD. PA VWLULK BWVU AOL NYHZZF ZWHJL DOPJO SHF PU MYVUA VM
      AOL OHSS KVVY. ILFVUK, ADV JVWZLZ VM AYLLZ TVHULK HUK ZDBUN PU H
      YPZPUN DPUK. H OHSM TVVU IYVRL AOYVBNO AOL YPMAZ VM YHJPUN
      JSVBKZ. PU PAZ JVSK SPNOA P ZHD ILFVUK AOL AYLLZ H IYVRLU MYPUNL
      VM YVJRZ, HUK AOL SVUN, SVD JBYCL VM AOL TLSHUJOVSF TVVY. P
      JSVZLK AOL JBYAHPU, MLLSPUN AOHA TF SHZA PTWYLZZPVU DHZ PU
      RLLWPUN DPAO AOL YLZA.

      HUK FLA PA DHZ UVA XBPAL AOL SHZA. P MVBUK TFZLSM DLHYF HUK FLA
      DHRLMBS, AVZZPUN YLZASLZZSF MYVT ZPKL AV ZPKL, ZLLRPUN MVY AOL
      ZSLLW DOPJO DVBSK UVA JVTL. MHY HDHF H JOPTPUN JSVJR ZAYBJR VBA
      AOL XBHYALYZ VM AOL OVBYZ, IBA VAOLYDPZL H KLHAOSF ZPSLUJL SHF
      BWVU AOL VSK OVBZL. HUK AOLU ZBKKLUSF, PU AOL CLYF KLHK VM AOL
      UPNOA, AOLYL JHTL H ZVBUK AV TF LHYZ, JSLHY, YLZVUHUA, HUK
      BUTPZAHRHISL. PA DHZ AOL ZVI VM H DVTHU, AOL TBMMSLK, ZAYHUNSPUN
      NHZW VM VUL DOV PZ AVYU IF HU BUJVUAYVSSHISL ZVYYVD. P ZHA BW PU
      ILK HUK SPZALULK PUALUASF. AOL UVPZL JVBSK UVA OHCL ILLU MHY HDHF
      HUK DHZ JLYAHPUSF PU AOL OVBZL. MVY OHSM HU OVBY P DHPALK DPAO
      LCLYF ULYCL VU AOL HSLYA, IBA AOLYL JHTL UV VAOLY ZVBUK ZHCL AOL
      JOPTPUN JSVJR HUK AOL YBZASL VM AOL PCF VU AOL DHSS.

JOHWALY 7.
AOL ZAHWSLAVUZ VM TLYYPWPA OVBZL


      AOL MYLZO ILHBAF VM AOL MVSSVDPUN TVYUPUN KPK ZVTLAOPUN AV LMMHJL
      MYVT VBY TPUKZ AOL NYPT HUK NYLF PTWYLZZPVU DOPJO OHK ILLU SLMA
      BWVU IVAO VM BZ IF VBY MPYZA LEWLYPLUJL VM IHZRLYCPSSL OHSS. HZ
      ZPY OLUYF HUK P ZHA HA IYLHRMHZA AOL ZBUSPNOA MSVVKLK PU AOYVBNO
      AOL OPNO TBSSPVULK DPUKVDZ, AOYVDPUN DHALYF WHAJOLZ VM JVSVBY
      MYVT AOL JVHAZ VM HYTZ DOPJO JVCLYLK AOLT. AOL KHYR WHULSSPUN
      NSVDLK SPRL IYVUGL PU AOL NVSKLU YHFZ, HUK PA DHZ OHYK AV YLHSPZL
      AOHA AOPZ DHZ PUKLLK AOL JOHTILY DOPJO OHK ZAYBJR ZBJO H NSVVT
      PUAV VBY ZVBSZ BWVU AOL LCLUPUN ILMVYL.

      “P NBLZZ PA PZ VBYZLSCLZ HUK UVA AOL OVBZL AOHA DL OHCL AV
      ISHTL!” ZHPK AOL IHYVULA. “DL DLYL APYLK DPAO VBY QVBYULF HUK
      JOPSSLK IF VBY KYPCL, ZV DL AVVR H NYLF CPLD VM AOL WSHJL. UVD DL
      HYL MYLZO HUK DLSS, ZV PA PZ HSS JOLLYMBS VUJL TVYL.”

      “HUK FLA PA DHZ UVA LUAPYLSF H XBLZAPVU VM PTHNPUHAPVU,” P
      HUZDLYLK. “KPK FVB, MVY LEHTWSL, OHWWLU AV OLHY ZVTLVUL, H DVTHU
      P AOPUR, ZVIIPUN PU AOL UPNOA?”

      “AOHA PZ JBYPVBZ, MVY P KPK DOLU P DHZ OHSM HZSLLW MHUJF AOHA P
      OLHYK ZVTLAOPUN VM AOL ZVYA. P DHPALK XBPAL H APTL, IBA AOLYL DHZ
      UV TVYL VM PA, ZV P JVUJSBKLK AOHA PA DHZ HSS H KYLHT.”

      “P OLHYK PA KPZAPUJASF, HUK P HT ZBYL AOHA PA DHZ YLHSSF AOL ZVI
      VM H DVTHU.”

      “DL TBZA HZR HIVBA AOPZ YPNOA HDHF.” OL YHUN AOL ILSS HUK HZRLK
      IHYYFTVYL DOLAOLY OL JVBSK HJJVBUA MVY VBY LEWLYPLUJL. PA ZLLTLK
      AV TL AOHA AOL WHSSPK MLHABYLZ VM AOL IBASLY ABYULK H ZOHKL WHSLY
      ZAPSS HZ OL SPZALULK AV OPZ THZALY’Z XBLZAPVU.

      “AOLYL HYL VUSF ADV DVTLU PU AOL OVBZL, ZPY OLUYF,” OL HUZDLYLK.
      “VUL PZ AOL ZJBSSLYF-THPK, DOV ZSLLWZ PU AOL VAOLY DPUN. AOL
      VAOLY PZ TF DPML, HUK P JHU HUZDLY MVY PA AOHA AOL ZVBUK JVBSK
      UVA OHCL JVTL MYVT OLY.”

      HUK FLA OL SPLK HZ OL ZHPK PA, MVY PA JOHUJLK AOHA HMALY
      IYLHRMHZA P TLA TYZ. IHYYFTVYL PU AOL SVUN JVYYPKVY DPAO AOL ZBU
      MBSS BWVU OLY MHJL. ZOL DHZ H SHYNL, PTWHZZPCL, OLHCF-MLHABYLK
      DVTHU DPAO H ZALYU ZLA LEWYLZZPVU VM TVBAO. IBA OLY ALSSAHSL LFLZ
      DLYL YLK HUK NSHUJLK HA TL MYVT ILADLLU ZDVSSLU SPKZ. PA DHZ ZOL,
      AOLU, DOV DLWA PU AOL UPNOA, HUK PM ZOL KPK ZV OLY OBZIHUK TBZA
      RUVD PA. FLA OL OHK AHRLU AOL VICPVBZ YPZR VM KPZJVCLYF PU
      KLJSHYPUN AOHA PA DHZ UVA ZV. DOF OHK OL KVUL AOPZ? HUK DOF KPK
      ZOL DLLW ZV IPAALYSF? HSYLHKF YVBUK AOPZ WHSL-MHJLK, OHUKZVTL,
      ISHJR-ILHYKLK THU AOLYL DHZ NHAOLYPUN HU HATVZWOLYL VM TFZALYF
      HUK VM NSVVT. PA DHZ OL DOV OHK ILLU AOL MPYZA AV KPZJVCLY AOL
      IVKF VM ZPY JOHYSLZ, HUK DL OHK VUSF OPZ DVYK MVY HSS AOL
      JPYJBTZAHUJLZ DOPJO SLK BW AV AOL VSK THU’Z KLHAO. DHZ PA
      WVZZPISL AOHA PA DHZ IHYYFTVYL, HMALY HSS, DOVT DL OHK ZLLU PU
      AOL JHI PU YLNLUA ZAYLLA? AOL ILHYK TPNOA DLSS OHCL ILLU AOL
      ZHTL. AOL JHITHU OHK KLZJYPILK H ZVTLDOHA ZOVYALY THU, IBA ZBJO
      HU PTWYLZZPVU TPNOA LHZPSF OHCL ILLU LYYVULVBZ. OVD JVBSK P
      ZLAASL AOL WVPUA MVYLCLY? VICPVBZSF AOL MPYZA AOPUN AV KV DHZ AV
      ZLL AOL NYPTWLU WVZATHZALY HUK MPUK DOLAOLY AOL ALZA ALSLNYHT OHK
      YLHSSF ILLU WSHJLK PU IHYYFTVYL’Z VDU OHUKZ. IL AOL HUZDLY DOHA
      PA TPNOA, P ZOVBSK HA SLHZA OHCL ZVTLAOPUN AV YLWVYA AV ZOLYSVJR
      OVSTLZ.

      ZPY OLUYF OHK UBTLYVBZ WHWLYZ AV LEHTPUL HMALY IYLHRMHZA, ZV AOHA
      AOL APTL DHZ WYVWPAPVBZ MVY TF LEJBYZPVU. PA DHZ H WSLHZHUA DHSR
      VM MVBY TPSLZ HSVUN AOL LKNL VM AOL TVVY, SLHKPUN TL HA SHZA AV H
      ZTHSS NYLF OHTSLA, PU DOPJO ADV SHYNLY IBPSKPUNZ, DOPJO WYVCLK AV
      IL AOL PUU HUK AOL OVBZL VM KY. TVYAPTLY, ZAVVK OPNO HIVCL AOL
      YLZA. AOL WVZATHZALY, DOV DHZ HSZV AOL CPSSHNL NYVJLY, OHK H
      JSLHY YLJVSSLJAPVU VM AOL ALSLNYHT.

      “JLYAHPUSF, ZPY,” ZHPK OL, “P OHK AOL ALSLNYHT KLSPCLYLK AV TY.
      IHYYFTVYL LEHJASF HZ KPYLJALK.”

      “DOV KLSPCLYLK PA?”

      “TF IVF OLYL. QHTLZ, FVB KLSPCLYLK AOHA ALSLNYHT AV TY. IHYYFTVYL
      HA AOL OHSS SHZA DLLR, KPK FVB UVA?”

      “FLZ, MHAOLY, P KLSPCLYLK PA.”

      “PUAV OPZ VDU OHUKZ?” P HZRLK.

      “DLSS, OL DHZ BW PU AOL SVMA HA AOL APTL, ZV AOHA P JVBSK UVA WBA
      PA PUAV OPZ VDU OHUKZ, IBA P NHCL PA PUAV TYZ. IHYYFTVYL’Z OHUKZ,
      HUK ZOL WYVTPZLK AV KLSPCLY PA HA VUJL.”

      “KPK FVB ZLL TY. IHYYFTVYL?”

      “UV, ZPY; P ALSS FVB OL DHZ PU AOL SVMA.”

      “PM FVB KPKU’A ZLL OPT, OVD KV FVB RUVD OL DHZ PU AOL SVMA?”

      “DLSS, ZBYLSF OPZ VDU DPML VBNOA AV RUVD DOLYL OL PZ,” ZHPK AOL
      WVZATHZALY ALZAPSF. “KPKU’A OL NLA AOL ALSLNYHT? PM AOLYL PZ HUF
      TPZAHRL PA PZ MVY TY. IHYYFTVYL OPTZLSM AV JVTWSHPU.”

      PA ZLLTLK OVWLSLZZ AV WBYZBL AOL PUXBPYF HUF MHYAOLY, IBA PA DHZ
      JSLHY AOHA PU ZWPAL VM OVSTLZ’Z YBZL DL OHK UV WYVVM AOHA
      IHYYFTVYL OHK UVA ILLU PU SVUKVU HSS AOL APTL. ZBWWVZL AOHA PA
      DLYL ZV—ZBWWVZL AOHA AOL ZHTL THU OHK ILLU AOL SHZA DOV OHK ZLLU
      ZPY JOHYSLZ HSPCL, HUK AOL MPYZA AV KVN AOL ULD OLPY DOLU OL
      YLABYULK AV LUNSHUK. DOHA AOLU? DHZ OL AOL HNLUA VM VAOLYZ VY OHK
      OL ZVTL ZPUPZALY KLZPNU VM OPZ VDU? DOHA PUALYLZA JVBSK OL OHCL
      PU WLYZLJBAPUN AOL IHZRLYCPSSL MHTPSF? P AOVBNOA VM AOL ZAYHUNL
      DHYUPUN JSPWWLK VBA VM AOL SLHKPUN HYAPJSL VM AOL _APTLZ_. DHZ
      AOHA OPZ DVYR VY DHZ PA WVZZPISF AOL KVPUN VM ZVTLVUL DOV DHZ
      ILUA BWVU JVBUALYHJAPUN OPZ ZJOLTLZ? AOL VUSF JVUJLPCHISL TVAPCL
      DHZ AOHA DOPJO OHK ILLU ZBNNLZALK IF ZPY OLUYF, AOHA PM AOL
      MHTPSF JVBSK IL ZJHYLK HDHF H JVTMVYAHISL HUK WLYTHULUA OVTL
      DVBSK IL ZLJBYLK MVY AOL IHYYFTVYLZ. IBA ZBYLSF ZBJO HU
      LEWSHUHAPVU HZ AOHA DVBSK IL XBPAL PUHKLXBHAL AV HJJVBUA MVY AOL
      KLLW HUK ZBIASL ZJOLTPUN DOPJO ZLLTLK AV IL DLHCPUN HU PUCPZPISL
      ULA YVBUK AOL FVBUN IHYVULA. OVSTLZ OPTZLSM OHK ZHPK AOHA UV TVYL
      JVTWSLE JHZL OHK JVTL AV OPT PU HSS AOL SVUN ZLYPLZ VM OPZ
      ZLUZHAPVUHS PUCLZAPNHAPVUZ. P WYHFLK, HZ P DHSRLK IHJR HSVUN AOL
      NYLF, SVULSF YVHK, AOHA TF MYPLUK TPNOA ZVVU IL MYLLK MYVT OPZ
      WYLVJJBWHAPVUZ HUK HISL AV JVTL KVDU AV AHRL AOPZ OLHCF IBYKLU VM
      YLZWVUZPIPSPAF MYVT TF ZOVBSKLYZ.

      ZBKKLUSF TF AOVBNOAZ DLYL PUALYYBWALK IF AOL ZVBUK VM YBUUPUN
      MLLA ILOPUK TL HUK IF H CVPJL DOPJO JHSSLK TL IF UHTL. P ABYULK,
      LEWLJAPUN AV ZLL KY. TVYAPTLY, IBA AV TF ZBYWYPZL PA DHZ H
      ZAYHUNLY DOV DHZ WBYZBPUN TL. OL DHZ H ZTHSS, ZSPT, JSLHU-ZOHCLU,
      WYPT-MHJLK THU, MSHELU-OHPYLK HUK SLHU-QHDLK, ILADLLU AOPYAF HUK
      MVYAF FLHYZ VM HNL, KYLZZLK PU H NYLF ZBPA HUK DLHYPUN H ZAYHD
      OHA. H APU IVE MVY IVAHUPJHS ZWLJPTLUZ OBUN VCLY OPZ ZOVBSKLY HUK
      OL JHYYPLK H NYLLU IBAALYMSF-ULA PU VUL VM OPZ OHUKZ.

      “FVB DPSS, P HT ZBYL, LEJBZL TF WYLZBTWAPVU, KY. DHAZVU,” ZHPK OL
      HZ OL JHTL WHUAPUN BW AV DOLYL P ZAVVK. “OLYL VU AOL TVVY DL HYL
      OVTLSF MVSR HUK KV UVA DHPA MVY MVYTHS PUAYVKBJAPVUZ. FVB THF
      WVZZPISF OHCL OLHYK TF UHTL MYVT VBY TBABHS MYPLUK, TVYAPTLY. P
      HT ZAHWSLAVU, VM TLYYPWPA OVBZL.”

      “FVBY ULA HUK IVE DVBSK OHCL AVSK TL HZ TBJO,” ZHPK P, “MVY P
      RULD AOHA TY. ZAHWSLAVU DHZ H UHABYHSPZA. IBA OVD KPK FVB RUVD
      TL?”

      “P OHCL ILLU JHSSPUN VU TVYAPTLY, HUK OL WVPUALK FVB VBA AV TL
      MYVT AOL DPUKVD VM OPZ ZBYNLYF HZ FVB WHZZLK. HZ VBY YVHK SHF AOL
      ZHTL DHF P AOVBNOA AOHA P DVBSK VCLYAHRL FVB HUK PUAYVKBJL
      TFZLSM. P AYBZA AOHA ZPY OLUYF PZ UVUL AOL DVYZL MVY OPZ
      QVBYULF?”

      “OL PZ CLYF DLSS, AOHUR FVB.”

      “DL DLYL HSS YHAOLY HMYHPK AOHA HMALY AOL ZHK KLHAO VM ZPY
      JOHYSLZ AOL ULD IHYVULA TPNOA YLMBZL AV SPCL OLYL. PA PZ HZRPUN
      TBJO VM H DLHSAOF THU AV JVTL KVDU HUK IBYF OPTZLSM PU H WSHJL VM
      AOPZ RPUK, IBA P ULLK UVA ALSS FVB AOHA PA TLHUZ H CLYF NYLHA
      KLHS AV AOL JVBUAYFZPKL. ZPY OLUYF OHZ, P ZBWWVZL, UV
      ZBWLYZAPAPVBZ MLHYZ PU AOL THAALY?”

      “P KV UVA AOPUR AOHA PA PZ SPRLSF.”

      “VM JVBYZL FVB RUVD AOL SLNLUK VM AOL MPLUK KVN DOPJO OHBUAZ AOL
      MHTPSF?”

      “P OHCL OLHYK PA.”

      “PA PZ LEAYHVYKPUHYF OVD JYLKBSVBZ AOL WLHZHUAZ HYL HIVBA OLYL!
      HUF UBTILY VM AOLT HYL YLHKF AV ZDLHY AOHA AOLF OHCL ZLLU ZBJO H
      JYLHABYL BWVU AOL TVVY.” OL ZWVRL DPAO H ZTPSL, IBA P ZLLTLK AV
      YLHK PU OPZ LFLZ AOHA OL AVVR AOL THAALY TVYL ZLYPVBZSF. “AOL
      ZAVYF AVVR H NYLHA OVSK BWVU AOL PTHNPUHAPVU VM ZPY JOHYSLZ, HUK
      P OHCL UV KVBIA AOHA PA SLK AV OPZ AYHNPJ LUK.”

      “IBA OVD?”

      “OPZ ULYCLZ DLYL ZV DVYRLK BW AOHA AOL HWWLHYHUJL VM HUF KVN
      TPNOA OHCL OHK H MHAHS LMMLJA BWVU OPZ KPZLHZLK OLHYA. P MHUJF
      AOHA OL YLHSSF KPK ZLL ZVTLAOPUN VM AOL RPUK BWVU AOHA SHZA UPNOA
      PU AOL FLD HSSLF. P MLHYLK AOHA ZVTL KPZHZALY TPNOA VJJBY, MVY P
      DHZ CLYF MVUK VM AOL VSK THU, HUK P RULD AOHA OPZ OLHYA DHZ
      DLHR.”

      “OVD KPK FVB RUVD AOHA?”

      “TF MYPLUK TVYAPTLY AVSK TL.”

      “FVB AOPUR, AOLU, AOHA ZVTL KVN WBYZBLK ZPY JOHYSLZ, HUK AOHA OL
      KPLK VM MYPNOA PU JVUZLXBLUJL?”

      “OHCL FVB HUF ILAALY LEWSHUHAPVU?”

      “P OHCL UVA JVTL AV HUF JVUJSBZPVU.”

      “OHZ TY. ZOLYSVJR OVSTLZ?”

      AOL DVYKZ AVVR HDHF TF IYLHAO MVY HU PUZAHUA IBA H NSHUJL HA AOL
      WSHJPK MHJL HUK ZALHKMHZA LFLZ VM TF JVTWHUPVU ZOVDLK AOHA UV
      ZBYWYPZL DHZ PUALUKLK.

      “PA PZ BZLSLZZ MVY BZ AV WYLALUK AOHA DL KV UVA RUVD FVB, KY.
      DHAZVU,” ZHPK OL. “AOL YLJVYKZ VM FVBY KLALJAPCL OHCL YLHJOLK BZ
      OLYL, HUK FVB JVBSK UVA JLSLIYHAL OPT DPAOVBA ILPUN RUVDU
      FVBYZLSM. DOLU TVYAPTLY AVSK TL FVBY UHTL OL JVBSK UVA KLUF FVBY
      PKLUAPAF. PM FVB HYL OLYL, AOLU PA MVSSVDZ AOHA TY. ZOLYSVJR
      OVSTLZ PZ PUALYLZAPUN OPTZLSM PU AOL THAALY, HUK P HT UHABYHSSF
      JBYPVBZ AV RUVD DOHA CPLD OL THF AHRL.”

      “P HT HMYHPK AOHA P JHUUVA HUZDLY AOHA XBLZAPVU.”

      “THF P HZR PM OL PZ NVPUN AV OVUVBY BZ DPAO H CPZPA OPTZLSM?”

      “OL JHUUVA SLHCL AVDU HA WYLZLUA. OL OHZ VAOLY JHZLZ DOPJO LUNHNL
      OPZ HAALUAPVU.”

      “DOHA H WPAF! OL TPNOA AOYVD ZVTL SPNOA VU AOHA DOPJO PZ ZV KHYR
      AV BZ. IBA HZ AV FVBY VDU YLZLHYJOLZ, PM AOLYL PZ HUF WVZZPISL
      DHF PU DOPJO P JHU IL VM ZLYCPJL AV FVB P AYBZA AOHA FVB DPSS
      JVTTHUK TL. PM P OHK HUF PUKPJHAPVU VM AOL UHABYL VM FVBY
      ZBZWPJPVUZ VY OVD FVB WYVWVZL AV PUCLZAPNHAL AOL JHZL, P TPNOA
      WLYOHWZ LCLU UVD NPCL FVB ZVTL HPK VY HKCPJL.”

      “P HZZBYL FVB AOHA P HT ZPTWSF OLYL BWVU H CPZPA AV TF MYPLUK,
      ZPY OLUYF, HUK AOHA P ULLK UV OLSW VM HUF RPUK.”

      “LEJLSSLUA!” ZHPK ZAHWSLAVU. “FVB HYL WLYMLJASF YPNOA AV IL DHYF
      HUK KPZJYLLA. P HT QBZASF YLWYVCLK MVY DOHA P MLLS DHZ HU
      BUQBZAPMPHISL PUAYBZPVU, HUK P WYVTPZL FVB AOHA P DPSS UVA
      TLUAPVU AOL THAALY HNHPU.”

      DL OHK JVTL AV H WVPUA DOLYL H UHYYVD NYHZZF WHAO ZAYBJR VMM MYVT
      AOL YVHK HUK DVBUK HDHF HJYVZZ AOL TVVY. H ZALLW,
      IVBSKLY-ZWYPURSLK OPSS SHF BWVU AOL YPNOA DOPJO OHK PU IFNVUL
      KHFZ ILLU JBA PUAV H NYHUPAL XBHYYF. AOL MHJL DOPJO DHZ ABYULK
      AVDHYKZ BZ MVYTLK H KHYR JSPMM, DPAO MLYUZ HUK IYHTISLZ NYVDPUN
      PU PAZ UPJOLZ. MYVT VCLY H KPZAHUA YPZL AOLYL MSVHALK H NYLF
      WSBTL VM ZTVRL.

      “H TVKLYHAL DHSR HSVUN AOPZ TVVY-WHAO IYPUNZ BZ AV TLYYPWPA
      OVBZL,” ZHPK OL. “WLYOHWZ FVB DPSS ZWHYL HU OVBY AOHA P THF OHCL
      AOL WSLHZBYL VM PUAYVKBJPUN FVB AV TF ZPZALY.”

      TF MPYZA AOVBNOA DHZ AOHA P ZOVBSK IL IF ZPY OLUYF’Z ZPKL. IBA
      AOLU P YLTLTILYLK AOL WPSL VM WHWLYZ HUK IPSSZ DPAO DOPJO OPZ
      ZABKF AHISL DHZ SPAALYLK. PA DHZ JLYAHPU AOHA P JVBSK UVA OLSW
      DPAO AOVZL. HUK OVSTLZ OHK LEWYLZZSF ZHPK AOHA P ZOVBSK ZABKF AOL
      ULPNOIVBYZ BWVU AOL TVVY. P HJJLWALK ZAHWSLAVU’Z PUCPAHAPVU, HUK
      DL ABYULK AVNLAOLY KVDU AOL WHAO.

      “PA PZ H DVUKLYMBS WSHJL, AOL TVVY,” ZHPK OL, SVVRPUN YVBUK VCLY
      AOL BUKBSHAPUN KVDUZ, SVUN NYLLU YVSSLYZ, DPAO JYLZAZ VM QHNNLK
      NYHUPAL MVHTPUN BW PUAV MHUAHZAPJ ZBYNLZ. “FVB ULCLY APYL VM AOL
      TVVY. FVB JHUUVA AOPUR AOL DVUKLYMBS ZLJYLAZ DOPJO PA JVUAHPUZ.
      PA PZ ZV CHZA, HUK ZV IHYYLU, HUK ZV TFZALYPVBZ.”

      “FVB RUVD PA DLSS, AOLU?”

      “P OHCL VUSF ILLU OLYL ADV FLHYZ. AOL YLZPKLUAZ DVBSK JHSS TL H
      ULDJVTLY. DL JHTL ZOVYASF HMALY ZPY JOHYSLZ ZLAASLK. IBA TF
      AHZALZ SLK TL AV LEWSVYL LCLYF WHYA VM AOL JVBUAYF YVBUK, HUK P
      ZOVBSK AOPUR AOHA AOLYL HYL MLD TLU DOV RUVD PA ILAALY AOHU P
      KV.”

      “PZ PA OHYK AV RUVD?”

      “CLYF OHYK. FVB ZLL, MVY LEHTWSL, AOPZ NYLHA WSHPU AV AOL UVYAO
      OLYL DPAO AOL XBLLY OPSSZ IYLHRPUN VBA VM PA. KV FVB VIZLYCL
      HUFAOPUN YLTHYRHISL HIVBA AOHA?”

      “PA DVBSK IL H YHYL WSHJL MVY H NHSSVW.”

      “FVB DVBSK UHABYHSSF AOPUR ZV HUK AOL AOVBNOA OHZ JVZA ZLCLYHS
      AOLPY SPCLZ ILMVYL UVD. FVB UVAPJL AOVZL IYPNOA NYLLU ZWVAZ
      ZJHAALYLK AOPJRSF VCLY PA?”

      “FLZ, AOLF ZLLT TVYL MLYAPSL AOHU AOL YLZA.”

      ZAHWSLAVU SHBNOLK. “AOHA PZ AOL NYLHA NYPTWLU TPYL,” ZHPK OL. “H
      MHSZL ZALW FVUKLY TLHUZ KLHAO AV THU VY ILHZA. VUSF FLZALYKHF P
      ZHD VUL VM AOL TVVY WVUPLZ DHUKLY PUAV PA. OL ULCLY JHTL VBA. P
      ZHD OPZ OLHK MVY XBPAL H SVUN APTL JYHUPUN VBA VM AOL IVN-OVSL,
      IBA PA ZBJRLK OPT KVDU HA SHZA. LCLU PU KYF ZLHZVUZ PA PZ H
      KHUNLY AV JYVZZ PA, IBA HMALY AOLZL HBABTU YHPUZ PA PZ HU HDMBS
      WSHJL. HUK FLA P JHU MPUK TF DHF AV AOL CLYF OLHYA VM PA HUK
      YLABYU HSPCL. IF NLVYNL, AOLYL PZ HUVAOLY VM AOVZL TPZLYHISL
      WVUPLZ!”

      ZVTLAOPUN IYVDU DHZ YVSSPUN HUK AVZZPUN HTVUN AOL NYLLU ZLKNLZ.
      AOLU H SVUN, HNVUPZLK, DYPAOPUN ULJR ZOVA BWDHYK HUK H KYLHKMBS
      JYF LJOVLK VCLY AOL TVVY. PA ABYULK TL JVSK DPAO OVYYVY, IBA TF
      JVTWHUPVU’Z ULYCLZ ZLLTLK AV IL ZAYVUNLY AOHU TPUL.

      THUF TVYL, WLYOHWZ, MVY AOLF NLA PU AOL DHF VM NVPUN AOLYL PU AOL

      AHRL. P OHCL MVBUK AOLT VBA.”

      DOPJO OL, VY HUFVUL LSZL, JVBSK VIQLJA.”

      “TF IYVAOLY PZ CLYF HUEPVBZ AV OHCL AOL OHSS PUOHIPALK, MVY OL
      AOPURZ PA PZ MVY AOL NVVK VM AOL WVVY MVSR BWVU AOL TVVY. OL

      ZBZWLJA AOHA P OHCL ZLLU FVB. NVVK-IFL!” ZOL ABYULK HUK OHK
      KPZHWWLHYLK PU H MLD TPUBALZ HTVUN AOL ZJHAALYLK IVBSKLYZ, DOPSL

      IHZRLYCPSSL OHSS.

      PU AOL LCLUPUN OL YLJBYYLK AV AOL ZBIQLJA VM OPZ VDU HJJVYK.

      P OHCL AVSK FVB AOHA AOL JVYYPKVY PZ IYVRLU IF AOL IHSJVUF DOPJO

      ZPKL. P DHPALK BUAPS OL OHK WHZZLK VBA VM ZPNOA HUK AOLU P
      MVSSVDLK OPT. DOLU P JHTL YVBUK AOL IHSJVUF OL OHK YLHJOLK AOL
      LUK VM AOL MHYAOLY JVYYPKVY, HUK P JVBSK ZLL MYVT AOL NSPTTLY VM
      SPNOA AOYVBNO HU VWLU KVVY AOHA OL OHK LUALYLK VUL VM AOL YVVTZ.
      UVD, HSS AOLZL YVVTZ HYL BUMBYUPZOLK HUK BUVJJBWPLK ZV AOHA OPZ
      LEWLKPAPVU ILJHTL TVYL TFZALYPVBZ AOHU LCLY. AOL SPNOA ZOVUL
      ZALHKPSF HZ PM OL DLYL ZAHUKPUN TVAPVUSLZZ. P JYLWA KVDU AOL
      WHZZHNL HZ UVPZLSLZZSF HZ P JVBSK HUK WLLWLK YVBUK AOL JVYULY VM
      AOL KVVY.

      IHYYFTVYL DHZ JYVBJOPUN HA AOL DPUKVD DPAO AOL JHUKSL OLSK
      HNHPUZA AOL NSHZZ. OPZ WYVMPSL DHZ OHSM ABYULK AVDHYKZ TL, HUK
      OPZ MHJL ZLLTLK AV IL YPNPK DPAO LEWLJAHAPVU HZ OL ZAHYLK VBA
      PUAV AOL ISHJRULZZ VM AOL TVVY. MVY ZVTL TPUBALZ OL ZAVVK
      DHAJOPUN PUALUASF. AOLU OL NHCL H KLLW NYVHU HUK DPAO HU
      PTWHAPLUA NLZABYL OL WBA VBA AOL SPNOA. PUZAHUASF P THKL TF DHF
      IHJR AV TF YVVT, HUK CLYF ZOVYASF JHTL AOL ZALHSAOF ZALWZ WHZZPUN

      JHUUVA NBLZZ, IBA AOLYL PZ ZVTL ZLJYLA IBZPULZZ NVPUN VU PU AOPZ

      “P KVU’A RUVD. PA’Z H ZVBUK AOLF OHCL VU AOL TVVY. P OLHYK PA
      VUJL ILMVYL.”

      PA KPLK HDHF, HUK HU HIZVSBAL ZPSLUJL JSVZLK PU BWVU BZ. DL ZAVVK
      ZAYHPUPUN VBY LHYZ, IBA UVAOPUN JHTL.

      “DHAZVU,” ZHPK AOL IHYVULA, “PA DHZ AOL JYF VM H OVBUK.”

      TF ISVVK YHU JVSK PU TF CLPUZ, MVY AOLYL DHZ H IYLHR PU OPZ CVPJL
      DOPJO AVSK VM AOL ZBKKLU OVYYVY DOPJO OHK ZLPGLK OPT.

      “DOHA KV AOLF JHSS AOPZ ZVBUK?” OL HZRLK.

      “DOV?”

      “AOL MVSR VU AOL JVBUAYFZPKL.”

      “VO, AOLF HYL PNUVYHUA WLVWSL. DOF ZOVBSK FVB TPUK DOHA AOLF JHSS
      PA?”

      “ALSS TL, DHAZVU. DOHA KV AOLF ZHF VM PA?”

      P OLZPAHALK IBA JVBSK UVA LZJHWL AOL XBLZAPVU.

      “AOLF ZHF PA PZ AOL JYF VM AOL OVBUK VM AOL IHZRLYCPSSLZ.”

      OL NYVHULK HUK DHZ ZPSLUA MVY H MLD TVTLUAZ.

      TPSLZ HDHF, VCLY FVUKLY, P AOPUR.”

      “PA DHZ OHYK AV ZHF DOLUJL PA JHTL.”

      “PA YVZL HUK MLSS DPAO AOL DPUK. PZU’A AOHA AOL KPYLJAPVU VM AOL
      NYLHA NYPTWLU TPYL?”

      “FLZ, PA PZ.”

      “DLSS, PA DHZ BW AOLYL. JVTL UVD, DHAZVU, KPKU’A FVB AOPUR
      FVBYZLSM AOHA PA DHZ AOL JYF VM H OVBUK? P HT UVA H JOPSK. FVB
      ULLK UVA MLHY AV ZWLHR AOL AYBAO.”

      “ZAHWSLAVU DHZ DPAO TL DOLU P OLHYK PA SHZA. OL ZHPK AOHA PA
      TPNOA IL AOL JHSSPUN VM H ZAYHUNL IPYK.”

      “UV, UV, PA DHZ H OVBUK. TF NVK, JHU AOLYL IL ZVTL AYBAO PU HSS
      AOLZL ZAVYPLZ? PZ PA WVZZPISL AOHA P HT YLHSSF PU KHUNLY MYVT ZV
      KHYR H JHBZL? FVB KVU’A ILSPLCL PA, KV FVB, DHAZVU?”

      “UV, UV.”

      “HUK FLA PA DHZ VUL AOPUN AV SHBNO HIVBA PA PU SVUKVU, HUK PA PZ

      ZBJO H JYF HZ AOHA. HUK TF BUJSL! AOLYL DHZ AOL MVVAWYPUA VM AOL
      OVBUK ILZPKL OPT HZ OL SHF. PA HSS MPAZ AVNLAOLY. P KVU’A AOPUR
      AOHA P HT H JVDHYK, DHAZVU, IBA AOHA ZVBUK ZLLTLK AV MYLLGL TF
      CLYF ISVVK. MLLS TF OHUK!”

      PA DHZ HZ JVSK HZ H ISVJR VM THYISL.

      “FVB’SS IL HSS YPNOA AVTVYYVD.”

      “P KVU’A AOPUR P’SS NLA AOHA JYF VBA VM TF OLHK. DOHA KV FVB
      HKCPZL AOHA DL KV UVD?”

      “ZOHSS DL ABYU IHJR?”

      “UV, IF AOBUKLY; DL OHCL JVTL VBA AV NLA VBY THU, HUK DL DPSS KV
      PA. DL HMALY AOL JVUCPJA, HUK H OLSS-OVBUK, HZ SPRLSF HZ UVA,
      HMALY BZ. JVTL VU! DL’SS ZLL PA AOYVBNO PM HSS AOL MPLUKZ VM AOL
      WPA DLYL SVVZL BWVU AOL TVVY.”

      DL ZABTISLK ZSVDSF HSVUN PU AOL KHYRULZZ, DPAO AOL ISHJR SVVT VM
      AOL JYHNNF OPSSZ HYVBUK BZ, HUK AOL FLSSVD ZWLJR VM SPNOA IBYUPUN
      ZALHKPSF PU MYVUA. AOLYL PZ UVAOPUN ZV KLJLWAPCL HZ AOL KPZAHUJL

      DOLUJL PA JHTL, HUK AOLU DL RULD AOHA DL DLYL PUKLLK CLYF JSVZL.
      H NBAALYPUN JHUKSL DHZ ZABJR PU H JYLCPJL VM AOL YVJRZ DOPJO

      “DOHA ZOHSS DL KV UVD?” DOPZWLYLK ZPY OLUYF.

      “DHPA OLYL. OL TBZA IL ULHY OPZ SPNOA. SLA BZ ZLL PM DL JHU NLA H
      NSPTWZL VM OPT.”

      AOL DVYKZ DLYL OHYKSF VBA VM TF TVBAO DOLU DL IVAO ZHD OPT. VCLY

      IYPZASPUN ILHYK, HUK OBUN DPAO THAALK OHPY, PA TPNOA DLSS OHCL

      KHYRULZZ SPRL H JYHMAF HUK ZHCHNL HUPTHS DOV OHZ OLHYK AOL ZALWZ
      VM AOL OBUALYZ.

      ZVTLAOPUN OHK LCPKLUASF HYVBZLK OPZ ZBZWPJPVUZ. PA THF OHCL ILLU

      HA AOL ZHTL TVTLUA AOL JVUCPJA ZJYLHTLK VBA H JBYZL HA BZ HUK

      DL YBZOLK VCLY AOL IYVD VM AOL OPSS, HUK AOLYL DHZ VBY THU

      BUHYTLK THU DOV DHZ YBUUPUN HDHF.

      DL DLYL IVAO ZDPMA YBUULYZ HUK PU MHPYSF NVVK AYHPUPUN, IBA DL
      ZVVU MVBUK AOHA DL OHK UV JOHUJL VM VCLYAHRPUN OPT. DL ZHD OPT

      OPSS. DL YHU HUK YHU BUAPS DL DLYL JVTWSLALSF ISVDU, IBA AOL
      ZWHJL ILADLLU BZ NYLD LCLY DPKLY. MPUHSSF DL ZAVWWLK HUK ZHA

      KPZAHUJL.

      HUK PA DHZ HA AOPZ TVTLUA AOHA AOLYL VJJBYYLK H TVZA ZAYHUNL HUK
      BULEWLJALK AOPUN. DL OHK YPZLU MYVT VBY YVJRZ HUK DLYL ABYUPUN AV
      NV OVTL, OHCPUN HIHUKVULK AOL OVWLSLZZ JOHZL. AOL TVVU DHZ SVD
      BWVU AOL YPNOA, HUK AOL QHNNLK WPUUHJSL VM H NYHUPAL AVY ZAVVK BW

      ISHJR HZ HU LIVUF ZAHABL VU AOHA ZOPUPUN IHJRNYVBUK, P ZHD AOL
      MPNBYL VM H THU BWVU AOL AVY. KV UVA AOPUR AOHA PA DHZ H
      KLSBZPVU, OVSTLZ. P HZZBYL FVB AOHA P OHCL ULCLY PU TF SPML ZLLU
      HUFAOPUN TVYL JSLHYSF. HZ MHY HZ P JVBSK QBKNL, AOL MPNBYL DHZ
      AOHA VM H AHSS, AOPU THU. OL ZAVVK DPAO OPZ SLNZ H SPAASL
      ZLWHYHALK, OPZ HYTZ MVSKLK, OPZ OLHK IVDLK, HZ PM OL DLYL
      IYVVKPUN VCLY AOHA LUVYTVBZ DPSKLYULZZ VM WLHA HUK NYHUPAL DOPJO
      SHF ILMVYL OPT. OL TPNOA OHCL ILLU AOL CLYF ZWPYPA VM AOHA
      ALYYPISL WSHJL. PA DHZ UVA AOL JVUCPJA. AOPZ THU DHZ MHY MYVT AOL
      WSHJL DOLYL AOL SHAALY OHK KPZHWWLHYLK. ILZPKLZ, OL DHZ H TBJO
      AHSSLY THU. DPAO H JYF VM ZBYWYPZL P WVPUALK OPT VBA AV AOL

      OPZ HYT AOL THU DHZ NVUL. AOLYL DHZ AOL ZOHYW WPUUHJSL VM NYHUPAL
      ZAPSS JBAAPUN AOL SVDLY LKNL VM AOL TVVU, IBA PAZ WLHR IVYL UV
      AYHJL VM AOHA ZPSLUA HUK TVAPVUSLZZ MPNBYL.

      P DPZOLK AV NV PU AOHA KPYLJAPVU HUK AV ZLHYJO AOL AVY, IBA PA
      DHZ ZVTL KPZAHUJL HDHF. AOL IHYVULA’Z ULYCLZ DLYL ZAPSS XBPCLYPUN
      MYVT AOHA JYF, DOPJO YLJHSSLK AOL KHYR ZAVYF VM OPZ MHTPSF, HUK
      OL DHZ UVA PU AOL TVVK MVY MYLZO HKCLUABYLZ. OL OHK UVA ZLLU AOPZ
      SVULSF THU BWVU AOL AVY HUK JVBSK UVA MLLS AOL AOYPSS DOPJO OPZ
      ZAYHUNL WYLZLUJL HUK OPZ JVTTHUKPUN HAAPABKL OHK NPCLU AV TL. “H
      DHYKLY, UV KVBIA,” ZHPK OL. “AOL TVVY OHZ ILLU AOPJR DPAO AOLT
      ZPUJL AOPZ MLSSVD LZJHWLK.” DLSS, WLYOHWZ OPZ LEWSHUHAPVU THF IL
      AOL YPNOA VUL, IBA P ZOVBSK SPRL AV OHCL ZVTL MBYAOLY WYVVM VM
      PA. AVKHF DL TLHU AV JVTTBUPJHAL AV AOL WYPUJLAVDU WLVWSL DOLYL
      AOLF ZOVBSK SVVR MVY AOLPY TPZZPUN THU, IBA PA PZ OHYK SPULZ AOHA
      DL OHCL UVA HJABHSSF OHK AOL AYPBTWO VM IYPUNPUN OPT IHJR HZ VBY
      VDU WYPZVULY. ZBJO HYL AOL HKCLUABYLZ VM SHZA UPNOA, HUK FVB TBZA
      HJRUVDSLKNL, TF KLHY OVSTLZ, AOHA P OHCL KVUL FVB CLYF DLSS PU
      AOL THAALY VM H YLWVYA. TBJO VM DOHA P ALSS FVB PZ UV KVBIA XBPAL
      PYYLSLCHUA, IBA ZAPSS P MLLS AOHA PA PZ ILZA AOHA P ZOVBSK SLA
      FVB OHCL HSS AOL MHJAZ HUK SLHCL FVB AV ZLSLJA MVY FVBYZLSM AOVZL
      DOPJO DPSS IL VM TVZA ZLYCPJL AV FVB PU OLSWPUN FVB AV FVBY
      JVUJSBZPVUZ. DL HYL JLYAHPUSF THRPUN ZVTL WYVNYLZZ. ZV MHY HZ AOL
      IHYYFTVYLZ NV DL OHCL MVBUK AOL TVAPCL VM AOLPY HJAPVUZ, HUK AOHA
      OHZ JSLHYLK BW AOL ZPABHAPVU CLYF TBJO. IBA AOL TVVY DPAO PAZ
      TFZALYPLZ HUK PAZ ZAYHUNL PUOHIPAHUAZ YLTHPUZ HZ PUZJYBAHISL HZ
      LCLY. WLYOHWZ PU TF ULEA P THF IL HISL AV AOYVD ZVTL SPNOA BWVU
      AOPZ HSZV. ILZA VM HSS DVBSK PA IL PM FVB JVBSK JVTL KVDU AV BZ.
      PU HUF JHZL FVB DPSS OLHY MYVT TL HNHPU PU AOL JVBYZL VM AOL ULEA
      MLD KHFZ.

JOHWALY 10.
LEAYHJA MYVT AOL KPHYF VM KY. DHAZVU


      ZV MHY P OHCL ILLU HISL AV XBVAL MYVT AOL YLWVYAZ DOPJO P OHCL
      MVYDHYKLK KBYPUN AOLZL LHYSF KHFZ AV ZOLYSVJR OVSTLZ. UVD,
      OVDLCLY, P OHCL HYYPCLK HA H WVPUA PU TF UHYYHAPCL DOLYL P HT
      JVTWLSSLK AV HIHUKVU AOPZ TLAOVK HUK AV AYBZA VUJL TVYL AV TF
      YLJVSSLJAPVUZ, HPKLK IF AOL KPHYF DOPJO P RLWA HA AOL APTL. H MLD
      LEAYHJAZ MYVT AOL SHAALY DPSS JHYYF TL VU AV AOVZL ZJLULZ DOPJO
      HYL PUKLSPISF MPELK PU LCLYF KLAHPS BWVU TF TLTVYF. P WYVJLLK,
      AOLU, MYVT AOL TVYUPUN DOPJO MVSSVDLK VBY HIVYAPCL JOHZL VM AOL
      JVUCPJA HUK VBY VAOLY ZAYHUNL LEWLYPLUJLZ BWVU AOL TVVY.

      _VJAVILY_ 16_AO_.—H KBSS HUK MVNNF KHF DPAO H KYPGGSL VM YHPU.
      AOL OVBZL PZ IHURLK PU DPAO YVSSPUN JSVBKZ, DOPJO YPZL UVD HUK
      AOLU AV ZOVD AOL KYLHYF JBYCLZ VM AOL TVVY, DPAO AOPU, ZPSCLY
      CLPUZ BWVU AOL ZPKLZ VM AOL OPSSZ, HUK AOL KPZAHUA IVBSKLYZ
      NSLHTPUN DOLYL AOL SPNOA ZAYPRLZ BWVU AOLPY DLA MHJLZ. PA PZ
      TLSHUJOVSF VBAZPKL HUK PU. AOL IHYVULA PZ PU H ISHJR YLHJAPVU
      HMALY AOL LEJPALTLUAZ VM AOL UPNOA. P HT JVUZJPVBZ TFZLSM VM H
      DLPNOA HA TF OLHYA HUK H MLLSPUN VM PTWLUKPUN KHUNLY—LCLY WYLZLUA
      KHUNLY, DOPJO PZ AOL TVYL ALYYPISL ILJHBZL P HT BUHISL AV KLMPUL
      PA.

      HUK OHCL P UVA JHBZL MVY ZBJO H MLLSPUN? JVUZPKLY AOL SVUN
      ZLXBLUJL VM PUJPKLUAZ DOPJO OHCL HSS WVPUALK AV ZVTL ZPUPZALY
      PUMSBLUJL DOPJO PZ HA DVYR HYVBUK BZ. AOLYL PZ AOL KLHAO VM AOL
      SHZA VJJBWHUA VM AOL OHSS, MBSMPSSPUN ZV LEHJASF AOL JVUKPAPVUZ
      VM AOL MHTPSF SLNLUK, HUK AOLYL HYL AOL YLWLHALK YLWVYAZ MYVT
      WLHZHUAZ VM AOL HWWLHYHUJL VM H ZAYHUNL JYLHABYL BWVU AOL TVVY.
      ADPJL P OHCL DPAO TF VDU LHYZ OLHYK AOL ZVBUK DOPJO YLZLTISLK AOL
      KPZAHUA IHFPUN VM H OVBUK. PA PZ PUJYLKPISL, PTWVZZPISL, AOHA PA
      ZOVBSK YLHSSF IL VBAZPKL AOL VYKPUHYF SHDZ VM UHABYL. H ZWLJAYHS
      OVBUK DOPJO SLHCLZ THALYPHS MVVATHYRZ HUK MPSSZ AOL HPY DPAO PAZ
      OVDSPUN PZ ZBYLSF UVA AV IL AOVBNOA VM. ZAHWSLAVU THF MHSS PU
      DPAO ZBJO H ZBWLYZAPAPVU, HUK TVYAPTLY HSZV, IBA PM P OHCL VUL
      XBHSPAF BWVU LHYAO PA PZ JVTTVU ZLUZL, HUK UVAOPUN DPSS WLYZBHKL
      TL AV ILSPLCL PU ZBJO H AOPUN. AV KV ZV DVBSK IL AV KLZJLUK AV
      AOL SLCLS VM AOLZL WVVY WLHZHUAZ, DOV HYL UVA JVUALUA DPAO H TLYL
      MPLUK KVN IBA TBZA ULLKZ KLZJYPIL OPT DPAO OLSS-MPYL ZOVVAPUN
      MYVT OPZ TVBAO HUK LFLZ. OVSTLZ DVBSK UVA SPZALU AV ZBJO MHUJPLZ,
      HUK P HT OPZ HNLUA. IBA MHJAZ HYL MHJAZ, HUK P OHCL ADPJL OLHYK
      AOPZ JYFPUN BWVU AOL TVVY. ZBWWVZL AOHA AOLYL DLYL YLHSSF ZVTL
      OBNL OVBUK SVVZL BWVU PA; AOHA DVBSK NV MHY AV LEWSHPU
      LCLYFAOPUN. IBA DOLYL JVBSK ZBJO H OVBUK SPL JVUJLHSLK, DOLYL KPK
      PA NLA PAZ MVVK, DOLYL KPK PA JVTL MYVT, OVD DHZ PA AOHA UV VUL
      ZHD PA IF KHF? PA TBZA IL JVUMLZZLK AOHA AOL UHABYHS LEWSHUHAPVU
      VMMLYZ HSTVZA HZ THUF KPMMPJBSAPLZ HZ AOL VAOLY. HUK HSDHFZ,
      HWHYA MYVT AOL OVBUK, AOLYL PZ AOL MHJA VM AOL OBTHU HNLUJF PU
      SVUKVU, AOL THU PU AOL JHI, HUK AOL SLAALY DOPJO DHYULK ZPY OLUYF
      HNHPUZA AOL TVVY. AOPZ HA SLHZA DHZ YLHS, IBA PA TPNOA OHCL ILLU
      AOL DVYR VM H WYVALJAPUN MYPLUK HZ LHZPSF HZ VM HU LULTF. DOLYL
      PZ AOHA MYPLUK VY LULTF UVD? OHZ OL YLTHPULK PU SVUKVU, VY OHZ OL
      MVSSVDLK BZ KVDU OLYL? JVBSK OL—JVBSK OL IL AOL ZAYHUNLY DOVT P
      ZHD BWVU AOL AVY?

      PA PZ AYBL AOHA P OHCL OHK VUSF AOL VUL NSHUJL HA OPT, HUK FLA
      AOLYL HYL ZVTL AOPUNZ AV DOPJO P HT YLHKF AV ZDLHY. OL PZ UV VUL
      DOVT P OHCL ZLLU KVDU OLYL, HUK P OHCL UVD TLA HSS AOL
      ULPNOIVBYZ. AOL MPNBYL DHZ MHY AHSSLY AOHU AOHA VM ZAHWSLAVU, MHY
      AOPUULY AOHU AOHA VM MYHURSHUK. IHYYFTVYL PA TPNOA WVZZPISF OHCL
      ILLU, IBA DL OHK SLMA OPT ILOPUK BZ, HUK P HT JLYAHPU AOHA OL
      JVBSK UVA OHCL MVSSVDLK BZ. H ZAYHUNLY AOLU PZ ZAPSS KVNNPUN BZ,
      QBZA HZ H ZAYHUNLY KVNNLK BZ PU SVUKVU. DL OHCL ULCLY ZOHRLU OPT
      VMM. PM P JVBSK SHF TF OHUKZ BWVU AOHA THU, AOLU HA SHZA DL TPNOA
      MPUK VBYZLSCLZ HA AOL LUK VM HSS VBY KPMMPJBSAPLZ. AV AOPZ VUL
      WBYWVZL P TBZA UVD KLCVAL HSS TF LULYNPLZ.

      TF MPYZA PTWBSZL DHZ AV ALSS ZPY OLUYF HSS TF WSHUZ. TF ZLJVUK
      HUK DPZLZA VUL PZ AV WSHF TF VDU NHTL HUK ZWLHR HZ SPAASL HZ
      WVZZPISL AV HUFVUL. OL PZ ZPSLUA HUK KPZAYHPA. OPZ ULYCLZ OHCL
      ILLU ZAYHUNLSF ZOHRLU IF AOHA ZVBUK BWVU AOL TVVY. P DPSS ZHF
      UVAOPUN AV HKK AV OPZ HUEPLAPLZ, IBA P DPSS AHRL TF VDU ZALWZ AV
      HAAHPU TF VDU LUK.

      DL OHK H ZTHSS ZJLUL AOPZ TVYUPUN HMALY IYLHRMHZA. IHYYFTVYL
      HZRLK SLHCL AV ZWLHR DPAO ZPY OLUYF, HUK AOLF DLYL JSVZLALK PU
      OPZ ZABKF ZVTL SPAASL APTL. ZPAAPUN PU AOL IPSSPHYK-YVVT P TVYL
      AOHU VUJL OLHYK AOL ZVBUK VM CVPJLZ YHPZLK, HUK P OHK H WYLAAF
      NVVK PKLH DOHA AOL WVPUA DHZ DOPJO DHZ BUKLY KPZJBZZPVU. HMALY H
      APTL AOL IHYVULA VWLULK OPZ KVVY HUK JHSSLK MVY TL. “IHYYFTVYL
      JVUZPKLYZ AOHA OL OHZ H NYPLCHUJL,” OL ZHPK. “OL AOPURZ AOHA PA
      DHZ BUMHPY VU VBY WHYA AV OBUA OPZ IYVAOLY-PU-SHD KVDU DOLU OL,
      VM OPZ VDU MYLL DPSS, OHK AVSK BZ AOL ZLJYLA.”

      AOL IBASLY DHZ ZAHUKPUN CLYF WHSL IBA CLYF JVSSLJALK ILMVYL BZ.

      “P THF OHCL ZWVRLU AVV DHYTSF, ZPY,” ZHPK OL, “HUK PM P OHCL, P
      HT ZBYL AOHA P ILN FVBY WHYKVU. HA AOL ZHTL APTL, P DHZ CLYF TBJO
      ZBYWYPZLK DOLU P OLHYK FVB ADV NLUASLTLU JVTL IHJR AOPZ TVYUPUN
      HUK SLHYULK AOHA FVB OHK ILLU JOHZPUN ZLSKLU. AOL WVVY MLSSVD OHZ
      LUVBNO AV MPNOA HNHPUZA DPAOVBA TF WBAAPUN TVYL BWVU OPZ AYHJR.”

      “PM FVB OHK AVSK BZ VM FVBY VDU MYLL DPSS PA DVBSK OHCL ILLU H
      KPMMLYLUA AOPUN,” ZHPK AOL IHYVULA, “FVB VUSF AVSK BZ, VY YHAOLY
      FVBY DPML VUSF AVSK BZ, DOLU PA DHZ MVYJLK MYVT FVB HUK FVB JVBSK
      UVA OLSW FVBYZLSM.”

      “P KPKU’A AOPUR FVB DVBSK OHCL AHRLU HKCHUAHNL VM PA, ZPY
      OLUYF—PUKLLK P KPKU’A.”

      “AOL THU PZ H WBISPJ KHUNLY. AOLYL HYL SVULSF OVBZLZ ZJHAALYLK
      VCLY AOL TVVY, HUK OL PZ H MLSSVD DOV DVBSK ZAPJR HA UVAOPUN. FVB
      VUSF DHUA AV NLA H NSPTWZL VM OPZ MHJL AV ZLL AOHA. SVVR HA TY.
      ZAHWSLAVU’Z OVBZL, MVY LEHTWSL, DPAO UV VUL IBA OPTZLSM AV KLMLUK
      PA. AOLYL’Z UV ZHMLAF MVY HUFVUL BUAPS OL PZ BUKLY SVJR HUK RLF.”

      “OL’SS IYLHR PUAV UV OVBZL, ZPY. P NPCL FVB TF ZVSLTU DVYK BWVU
      AOHA. IBA OL DPSS ULCLY AYVBISL HUFVUL PU AOPZ JVBUAYF HNHPU. P
      HZZBYL FVB, ZPY OLUYF, AOHA PU H CLYF MLD KHFZ AOL ULJLZZHYF
      HYYHUNLTLUAZ DPSS OHCL ILLU THKL HUK OL DPSS IL VU OPZ DHF AV

      OPT. FVB JHU’A ALSS VU OPT DPAOVBA NLAAPUN TF DPML HUK TL PUAV

      P ZOYBNNLK TF ZOVBSKLYZ. “PM OL DLYL ZHMLSF VBA VM AOL JVBUAYF PA

      DVTHU.”

      “AV TLLA H DVTHU! OL?”

      “FLZ, ZPY.”

      “P JHU’A NPCL FVB AOL UHTL, ZPY, IBA P JHU NPCL FVB AOL PUPAPHSZ.

      “OVD KV FVB RUVD AOPZ, IHYYFTVYL?”

      “DLSS?”

      KLHAO.”

      P DLUA HA VUJL AV TF YVVT HUK KYLD BW TF YLWVYA VM AOL TVYUPUN’Z

      _VJAVILY_ 17_AO_.—HSS KHF AVKHF AOL YHPU WVBYLK KVDU, YBZASPUN VU
      AOL PCF HUK KYPWWPUN MYVT AOL LHCLZ. P AOVBNOA VM AOL JVUCPJA VBA
      BWVU AOL ISLHR, JVSK, ZOLSALYSLZZ TVVY. WVVY KLCPS! DOHALCLY OPZ
      JYPTLZ, OL OHZ ZBMMLYLK ZVTLAOPUN AV HAVUL MVY AOLT. HUK AOLU P
      AOVBNOA VM AOHA VAOLY VUL—AOL MHJL PU AOL JHI, AOL MPNBYL HNHPUZA
      AOL TVVU. DHZ OL HSZV VBA PU AOHA KLSBNLK—AOL BUZLLU DHAJOLY, AOL
      THU VM KHYRULZZ? PU AOL LCLUPUN P WBA VU TF DHALYWYVVM HUK P
      DHSRLK MHY BWVU AOL ZVKKLU TVVY, MBSS VM KHYR PTHNPUPUNZ, AOL
      YHPU ILHAPUN BWVU TF MHJL HUK AOL DPUK DOPZASPUN HIVBA TF LHYZ.
      NVK OLSW AOVZL DOV DHUKLY PUAV AOL NYLHA TPYL UVD, MVY LCLU AOL
      MPYT BWSHUKZ HYL ILJVTPUN H TVYHZZ. P MVBUK AOL ISHJR AVY BWVU
      DOPJO P OHK ZLLU AOL ZVSPAHYF DHAJOLY, HUK MYVT PAZ JYHNNF ZBTTPA
      P SVVRLK VBA TFZLSM HJYVZZ AOL TLSHUJOVSF KVDUZ. YHPU ZXBHSSZ
      KYPMALK HJYVZZ AOLPY YBZZLA MHJL, HUK AOL OLHCF, ZSHAL-JVSVBYLK
      JSVBKZ OBUN SVD VCLY AOL SHUKZJHWL, AYHPSPUN PU NYLF DYLHAOZ KVDU
      AOL ZPKLZ VM AOL MHUAHZAPJ OPSSZ. PU AOL KPZAHUA OVSSVD VU AOL
      SLMA, OHSM OPKKLU IF AOL TPZA, AOL ADV AOPU AVDLYZ VM IHZRLYCPSSL
      OHSS YVZL HIVCL AOL AYLLZ. AOLF DLYL AOL VUSF ZPNUZ VM OBTHU SPML
      DOPJO P JVBSK ZLL, ZHCL VUSF AOVZL WYLOPZAVYPJ OBAZ DOPJO SHF
      AOPJRSF BWVU AOL ZSVWLZ VM AOL OPSSZ. UVDOLYL DHZ AOLYL HUF AYHJL
      VM AOHA SVULSF THU DOVT P OHK ZLLU VU AOL ZHTL ZWVA ADV UPNOAZ
      ILMVYL.

      HZ P DHSRLK IHJR P DHZ VCLYAHRLU IF KY. TVYAPTLY KYPCPUN PU OPZ
      KVN-JHYA VCLY H YVBNO TVVYSHUK AYHJR DOPJO SLK MYVT AOL VBASFPUN
      MHYTOVBZL VM MVBSTPYL. OL OHZ ILLU CLYF HAALUAPCL AV BZ, HUK
      OHYKSF H KHF OHZ WHZZLK AOHA OL OHZ UVA JHSSLK HA AOL OHSS AV ZLL

      KVN-JHYA, HUK OL NHCL TL H SPMA OVTLDHYK. P MVBUK OPT TBJO
      AYVBISLK VCLY AOL KPZHWWLHYHUJL VM OPZ SPAASL ZWHUPLS. PA OHK
      DHUKLYLK VU AV AOL TVVY HUK OHK ULCLY JVTL IHJR. P NHCL OPT ZBJO
      JVUZVSHAPVU HZ P TPNOA, IBA P AOVBNOA VM AOL WVUF VU AOL NYPTWLU
      TPYL, HUK P KV UVA MHUJF AOHA OL DPSS ZLL OPZ SPAASL KVN HNHPU.

      “IF AOL DHF, TVYAPTLY,” ZHPK P HZ DL QVSALK HSVUN AOL YVBNO YVHK,
      “P ZBWWVZL AOLYL HYL MLD WLVWSL SPCPUN DPAOPU KYPCPUN KPZAHUJL VM
      AOPZ DOVT FVB KV UVA RUVD?”

      “OHYKSF HUF, P AOPUR.”

      “JHU FVB, AOLU, ALSS TL AOL UHTL VM HUF DVTHU DOVZL PUPAPHSZ HYL
      S. S.?”

      OL AOVBNOA MVY H MLD TPUBALZ.

      “UV,” ZHPK OL. “AOLYL HYL H MLD NPWZPLZ HUK SHIVBYPUN MVSR MVY
      DOVT P JHU’A HUZDLY, IBA HTVUN AOL MHYTLYZ VY NLUAYF AOLYL PZ UV

      SPCLZ PU JVVTIL AYHJLF.”

      “DOV PZ ZOL?” P HZRLK.

      “ZOL PZ MYHURSHUK’Z KHBNOALY.”

      “DOHA! VSK MYHURSHUK AOL JYHUR?”

      “LEHJASF. ZOL THYYPLK HU HYAPZA UHTLK SFVUZ, DOV JHTL ZRLAJOPUN

      NPYS OHZ OHK H WYLAAF IHK APTL.”

      “OVD KVLZ ZOL SPCL?”

      “P MHUJF VSK MYHURSHUK HSSVDZ OLY H WPAAHUJL, IBA PA JHUUVA IL

      MVY VUL, HUK ZPY JOHYSLZ MVY HUVAOLY. P NHCL H AYPMSL TFZLSM. PA
      DHZ AV ZLA OLY BW PU H AFWLDYPAPUN IBZPULZZ.”

      OL DHUALK AV RUVD AOL VIQLJA VM TF PUXBPYPLZ, IBA P THUHNLK AV
      ZHAPZMF OPZ JBYPVZPAF DPAOVBA ALSSPUN OPT AVV TBJO, MVY AOLYL PZ

      AOPZ TYZ. SHBYH SFVUZ, VM LXBPCVJHS YLWBAHAPVU, H SVUN ZALW DPSS
      OHCL ILLU THKL AVDHYKZ JSLHYPUN VUL PUJPKLUA PU AOPZ JOHPU VM
      TFZALYPLZ. P HT JLYAHPUSF KLCLSVWPUN AOL DPZKVT VM AOL ZLYWLUA,
      MVY DOLU TVYAPTLY WYLZZLK OPZ XBLZAPVUZ AV HU PUJVUCLUPLUA LEALUA

      ZV OLHYK UVAOPUN IBA JYHUPVSVNF MVY AOL YLZA VM VBY KYPCL. P OHCL
      UVA SPCLK MVY FLHYZ DPAO ZOLYSVJR OVSTLZ MVY UVAOPUN.

      P OHCL VUSF VUL VAOLY PUJPKLUA AV YLJVYK BWVU AOPZ ALTWLZABVBZ

      UVD, DOPJO NPCLZ TL VUL TVYL ZAYVUN JHYK DOPJO P JHU WSHF PU KBL
      APTL.

      TVYAPTLY OHK ZAHFLK AV KPUULY, HUK OL HUK AOL IHYVULA WSHFLK
      éJHYAé HMALYDHYKZ. AOL IBASLY IYVBNOA TL TF JVMMLL PUAV AOL

      “DLSS,” ZHPK P, “OHZ AOPZ WYLJPVBZ YLSHAPVU VM FVBYZ KLWHYALK, VY
      PZ OL ZAPSS SBYRPUN VBA FVUKLY?”

      “P KVU’A RUVD, ZPY. P OVWL AV OLHCLU AOHA OL OHZ NVUL, MVY OL OHZ

      SLMA VBA MVVK MVY OPT SHZA, HUK AOHA DHZ AOYLL KHFZ HNV.”

      “KPK FVB ZLL OPT AOLU?”

      “UV, ZPY, IBA AOL MVVK DHZ NVUL DOLU ULEA P DLUA AOHA DHF.”

      “AOLU OL DHZ JLYAHPUSF AOLYL?”

      “ZV FVB DVBSK AOPUR, ZPY, BUSLZZ PA DHZ AOL VAOLY THU DOV AVVR

      P ZHA DPAO TF JVMMLL-JBW OHSMDHF AV TF SPWZ HUK ZAHYLK HA
      IHYYFTVYL.

      “FVB RUVD AOHA AOLYL PZ HUVAOLY THU AOLU?”

      “FLZ, ZPY; AOLYL PZ HUVAOLY THU BWVU AOL TVVY.”

      “OHCL FVB ZLLU OPT?”

      “UV, ZPY.”

      “OVD KV FVB RUVD VM OPT AOLU?”

      “ZLSKLU AVSK TL VM OPT, ZPY, H DLLR HNV VY TVYL. OL’Z PU OPKPUN,

      IHYYFTVYL OLZPAHALK MVY H TVTLUA, HZ PM OL YLNYLAALK OPZ VBAIBYZA

      “SVVR HA ZPY JOHYSLZ’Z KLHAO! AOHA DHZ IHK LUVBNO, MVY HSS AOHA
      AOL JVYVULY ZHPK. SVVR HA AOL UVPZLZ VU AOL TVVY HA UPNOA.
      AOLYL’Z UVA H THU DVBSK JYVZZ PA HMALY ZBUKVDU PM OL DHZ WHPK MVY

      “IBA HIVBA AOPZ ZAYHUNLY,” ZHPK P. “JHU FVB ALSS TL HUFAOPUN

      THRL VBA.”

      VSK MVSR BZLK AV SPCL.”

      “IBA OVD HIVBA OPZ MVVK?”

      “ZLSKLU MVBUK VBA AOHA OL OHZ NVA H SHK DOV DVYRZ MVY OPT HUK
      IYPUNZ HSS OL ULLKZ. P KHYL ZHF OL NVLZ AV JVVTIL AYHJLF MVY DOHA

      “CLYF NVVK, IHYYFTVYL. DL THF AHSR MBYAOLY VM AOPZ ZVTL VAOLY
      APTL.” DOLU AOL IBASLY OHK NVUL P DHSRLK VCLY AV AOL ISHJR

      DOHA WHZZPVU VM OHAYLK JHU PA IL DOPJO SLHKZ H THU AV SBYR PU
      ZBJO H WSHJL HA ZBJO H APTL! HUK DOHA KLLW HUK LHYULZA WBYWVZL
      JHU OL OHCL DOPJO JHSSZ MVY ZBJO H AYPHS! AOLYL, PU AOHA OBA BWVU
      AOL TVVY, ZLLTZ AV SPL AOL CLYF JLUAYL VM AOHA WYVISLT DOPJO OHZ
      CLELK TL ZV ZVYLSF. P ZDLHY AOHA HUVAOLY KHF ZOHSS UVA OHCL
      WHZZLK ILMVYL P OHCL KVUL HSS AOHA THU JHU KV AV YLHJO AOL OLHYA
      VM AOL TFZALYF.

JOHWALY 11.
AOL THU VU AOL AVY


      AOL LEAYHJA MYVT TF WYPCHAL KPHYF DOPJO MVYTZ AOL SHZA JOHWALY
      OHZ IYVBNOA TF UHYYHAPCL BW AV AOL LPNOALLUAO VM VJAVILY, H APTL
      DOLU AOLZL ZAYHUNL LCLUAZ ILNHU AV TVCL ZDPMASF AVDHYKZ AOLPY
      ALYYPISL JVUJSBZPVU. AOL PUJPKLUAZ VM AOL ULEA MLD KHFZ HYL
      PUKLSPISF NYHCLU BWVU TF YLJVSSLJAPVU, HUK P JHU ALSS AOLT
      DPAOVBA YLMLYLUJL AV AOL UVALZ THKL HA AOL APTL. P ZAHYA AOLT
      MYVT AOL KHF DOPJO ZBJJLLKLK AOHA BWVU DOPJO P OHK LZAHISPZOLK
      ADV MHJAZ VM NYLHA PTWVYAHUJL, AOL VUL AOHA TYZ. SHBYH SFVUZ VM
      JVVTIL AYHJLF OHK DYPAALU AV ZPY JOHYSLZ IHZRLYCPSSL HUK THKL HU
      HWWVPUATLUA DPAO OPT HA AOL CLYF WSHJL HUK OVBY AOHA OL TLA OPZ
      KLHAO, AOL VAOLY AOHA AOL SBYRPUN THU BWVU AOL TVVY DHZ AV IL
      MVBUK HTVUN AOL ZAVUL OBAZ BWVU AOL OPSSZPKL. DPAO AOLZL ADV
      MHJAZ PU TF WVZZLZZPVU P MLSA AOHA LPAOLY TF PUALSSPNLUJL VY TF
      JVBYHNL TBZA IL KLMPJPLUA PM P JVBSK UVA AOYVD ZVTL MBYAOLY SPNOA
      BWVU AOLZL KHYR WSHJLZ.

      P OHK UV VWWVYABUPAF AV ALSS AOL IHYVULA DOHA P OHK SLHYULK HIVBA
      TYZ. SFVUZ BWVU AOL LCLUPUN ILMVYL, MVY KY. TVYAPTLY YLTHPULK
      DPAO OPT HA JHYKZ BUAPS PA DHZ CLYF SHAL. HA IYLHRMHZA, OVDLCLY,
      P PUMVYTLK OPT HIVBA TF KPZJVCLYF HUK HZRLK OPT DOLAOLY OL DVBSK
      JHYL AV HJJVTWHUF TL AV JVVTIL AYHJLF. HA MPYZA OL DHZ CLYF LHNLY
      AV JVTL, IBA VU ZLJVUK AOVBNOAZ PA ZLLTLK AV IVAO VM BZ AOHA PM P
      DLUA HSVUL AOL YLZBSAZ TPNOA IL ILAALY. AOL TVYL MVYTHS DL THKL
      AOL CPZPA AOL SLZZ PUMVYTHAPVU DL TPNOA VIAHPU. P SLMA ZPY OLUYF
      ILOPUK, AOLYLMVYL, UVA DPAOVBA ZVTL WYPJRPUNZ VM JVUZJPLUJL, HUK
      KYVCL VMM BWVU TF ULD XBLZA.

      DOLU P YLHJOLK JVVTIL AYHJLF P AVSK WLYRPUZ AV WBA BW AOL OVYZLZ,
      HUK P THKL PUXBPYPLZ MVY AOL SHKF DOVT P OHK JVTL AV PUALYYVNHAL.
      P OHK UV KPMMPJBSAF PU MPUKPUN OLY YVVTZ, DOPJO DLYL JLUAYHS HUK
      DLSS HWWVPUALK. H THPK ZOVDLK TL PU DPAOVBA JLYLTVUF, HUK HZ P
      LUALYLK AOL ZPAAPUN-YVVT H SHKF, DOV DHZ ZPAAPUN ILMVYL H
      YLTPUNAVU AFWLDYPALY, ZWYHUN BW DPAO H WSLHZHUA ZTPSL VM DLSJVTL.
      OLY MHJL MLSS, OVDLCLY, DOLU ZOL ZHD AOHA P DHZ H ZAYHUNLY, HUK
      ZOL ZHA KVDU HNHPU HUK HZRLK TL AOL VIQLJA VM TF CPZPA.

      AOL MPYZA PTWYLZZPVU SLMA IF TYZ. SFVUZ DHZ VUL VM LEAYLTL
      ILHBAF. OLY LFLZ HUK OHPY DLYL VM AOL ZHTL YPJO OHGLS JVSVBY, HUK
      OLY JOLLRZ, AOVBNO JVUZPKLYHISF MYLJRSLK, DLYL MSBZOLK DPAO AOL
      LEXBPZPAL ISVVT VM AOL IYBULAAL, AOL KHPUAF WPUR DOPJO SBYRZ HA
      AOL OLHYA VM AOL ZBSWOBY YVZL. HKTPYHAPVU DHZ, P YLWLHA, AOL
      MPYZA PTWYLZZPVU. IBA AOL ZLJVUK DHZ JYPAPJPZT. AOLYL DHZ
      ZVTLAOPUN ZBIASF DYVUN DPAO AOL MHJL, ZVTL JVHYZLULZZ VM
      LEWYLZZPVU, ZVTL OHYKULZZ, WLYOHWZ, VM LFL, ZVTL SVVZLULZZ VM SPW
      DOPJO THYYLK PAZ WLYMLJA ILHBAF. IBA AOLZL, VM JVBYZL, HYL
      HMALYAOVBNOAZ. HA AOL TVTLUA P DHZ ZPTWSF JVUZJPVBZ AOHA P DHZ PU
      AOL WYLZLUJL VM H CLYF OHUKZVTL DVTHU, HUK AOHA ZOL DHZ HZRPUN TL
      AOL YLHZVUZ MVY TF CPZPA. P OHK UVA XBPAL BUKLYZAVVK BUAPS AOHA
      PUZAHUA OVD KLSPJHAL TF TPZZPVU DHZ.

      “P OHCL AOL WSLHZBYL,” ZHPK P, “VM RUVDPUN FVBY MHAOLY.”

      AYBL.”

      “OVD ZV?” P HZRLK.

      AOL VSK THU WBA VU H CLYF RUVDPUN LEWYLZZPVU. “ILJHBZL P JVBSK
      ALSS AOLT DOHA AOLF HYL KFPUN AV RUVD; IBA UVAOPUN DVBSK PUKBJL

      P OHK ILLU JHZAPUN YVBUK MVY ZVTL LEJBZL IF DOPJO P JVBSK NLA

      “OH, OH, TF IVF, H CLYF TBJO TVYL PTWVYAHUA THAALY AOHU AOHA!

      TF OLHYA ZHUR MVY IHYYFTVYL. PA DHZ H ZLYPVBZ AOPUN AV IL PU AOL

      MVY H TPUBAL P ZAVVK AOLYL DPAO AOL WHWLY PU TF OHUKZ AOPURPUN

      PM AOLYL DHZ VUL YLWVYA AOLYL TPNOA IL VAOLYZ, ZV P SVVRLK YVBUK

      VBAZPKL AOL ZBU DHZ ZPURPUN SVD HUK AOL DLZA DHZ ISHGPUN DPAO
      ZJHYSLA HUK NVSK. PAZ YLMSLJAPVU DHZ ZOVA IHJR PU YBKKF WHAJOLZ

      HUK AOLU HA SHZA P OLHYK OPT. MHY HDHF JHTL AOL ZOHYW JSPUR VM H

JOHWALY 12.
KLHAO VU AOL TVVY


      MVY H TVTLUA VY ADV P ZHA IYLHAOSLZZ, OHYKSF HISL AV ILSPLCL TF
      LHYZ. AOLU TF ZLUZLZ HUK TF CVPJL JHTL IHJR AV TL, DOPSL H
      JYBZOPUN DLPNOA VM YLZWVUZPIPSPAF ZLLTLK PU HU PUZAHUA AV IL
      SPMALK MYVT TF ZVBS. AOHA JVSK, PUJPZPCL, PYVUPJHS CVPJL JVBSK
      ILSVUN AV IBA VUL THU PU HSS AOL DVYSK.

      “OVSTLZ!” P JYPLK—“OVSTLZ!”

      “JVTL VBA,” ZHPK OL, “HUK WSLHZL IL JHYLMBS DPAO AOL YLCVSCLY.”

      P ZAVVWLK BUKLY AOL YBKL SPUALS, HUK AOLYL OL ZHA BWVU H ZAVUL
      VBAZPKL, OPZ NYLF LFLZ KHUJPUN DPAO HTBZLTLUA HZ AOLF MLSS BWVU
      TF HZAVUPZOLK MLHABYLZ. OL DHZ AOPU HUK DVYU, IBA JSLHY HUK
      HSLYA, OPZ RLLU MHJL IYVUGLK IF AOL ZBU HUK YVBNOLULK IF AOL
      DPUK. PU OPZ ADLLK ZBPA HUK JSVAO JHW OL SVVRLK SPRL HUF VAOLY
      AVBYPZA BWVU AOL TVVY, HUK OL OHK JVUAYPCLK, DPAO AOHA JHASPRL
      SVCL VM WLYZVUHS JSLHUSPULZZ DOPJO DHZ VUL VM OPZ
      JOHYHJALYPZAPJZ, AOHA OPZ JOPU ZOVBSK IL HZ ZTVVAO HUK OPZ SPULU
      HZ WLYMLJA HZ PM OL DLYL PU IHRLY ZAYLLA.

      “P ULCLY DHZ TVYL NSHK AV ZLL HUFVUL PU TF SPML,” ZHPK P HZ P
      DYBUN OPT IF AOL OHUK.

      “VY TVYL HZAVUPZOLK, LO?”

      “DLSS, P TBZA JVUMLZZ AV PA.”

      “AOL ZBYWYPZL DHZ UVA HSS VU VUL ZPKL, P HZZBYL FVB. P OHK UV
      PKLH AOHA FVB OHK MVBUK TF VJJHZPVUHS YLAYLHA, ZAPSS SLZZ AOHA

      “TF MVVAWYPUA, P WYLZBTL?”

      “UV, DHAZVU, P MLHY AOHA P JVBSK UVA BUKLYAHRL AV YLJVNUPGL FVBY

      ZBWYLTL TVTLUA DOLU FVB JOHYNLK PUAV AOL LTWAF OBA.”

      “LEHJASF.”

      “P AOVBNOA HZ TBJO—HUK RUVDPUN FVBY HKTPYHISL ALUHJPAF P DHZ
      JVUCPUJLK AOHA FVB DLYL ZPAAPUN PU HTIBZO, H DLHWVU DPAOPU YLHJO,

      “LEJLSSLUA, DHAZVU! HUK OVD KPK FVB SVJHSPZL TL? FVB ZHD TL,

      “HUK OHCL UV KVBIA ZLHYJOLK HSS AOL OBAZ BUAPS FVB JHTL AV AOPZ

      “UV, FVBY IVF OHK ILLU VIZLYCLK, HUK AOHA NHCL TL H NBPKL DOLYL
      AV SVVR.”

      “AOL VSK NLUASLTHU DPAO AOL ALSLZJVWL, UV KVBIA. P JVBSK UVA THRL

      “FLZ.”

      “AV ZLL TYZ. SHBYH SFVUZ?”

      “LEHJASF.”

      “DLSS KVUL! VBY YLZLHYJOLZ OHCL LCPKLUASF ILLU YBUUPUN VU
      WHYHSSLS SPULZ, HUK DOLU DL BUPAL VBY YLZBSAZ P LEWLJA DL ZOHSS
      OHCL H MHPYSF MBSS RUVDSLKNL VM AOL JHZL.”

      “DLSS, P HT NSHK MYVT TF OLHYA AOHA FVB HYL OLYL, MVY PUKLLK AOL
      YLZWVUZPIPSPAF HUK AOL TFZALYF DLYL IVAO ILJVTPUN AVV TBJO MVY TF
      ULYCLZ. IBA OVD PU AOL UHTL VM DVUKLY KPK FVB JVTL OLYL, HUK DOHA

      DVYRPUN VBA AOHA JHZL VM ISHJRTHPSPUN.”

      “AOHA DHZ DOHA P DPZOLK FVB AV AOPUR.”

      “AOLU FVB BZL TL, HUK FLA KV UVA AYBZA TL!” P JYPLK DPAO ZVTL

      OVSTLZ.”

      “TF KLHY MLSSVD, FVB OHCL ILLU PUCHSBHISL AV TL PU AOPZ HZ PU
      THUF VAOLY JHZLZ, HUK P ILN AOHA FVB DPSS MVYNPCL TL PM P OHCL
      ZLLTLK AV WSHF H AYPJR BWVU FVB. PU AYBAO, PA DHZ WHYASF MVY FVBY

      DHZ ZAPSS ISHJR LUVBNO, IBA AOPZ THU OHK HA SLHZA KLZLYCLK KLHAO
      IF AOL SHDZ VM OPZ JVBUAYF. P AVSK OVSTLZ OVD AOL THAALY ZAVVK,
      TF OLHYA IBIISPUN VCLY DPAO AOHURMBSULZZ HUK QVF.

      “AOLU AOL JSVAOLZ OHCL ILLU AOL WVVY KLCPS’Z KLHAO,” ZHPK OL. “PA
      PZ JSLHY LUVBNO AOHA AOL OVBUK OHZ ILLU SHPK VU MYVT ZVTL HYAPJSL
      VM ZPY OLUYF’Z—AOL IVVA DOPJO DHZ HIZAYHJALK PU AOL OVALS, PU HSS
      WYVIHIPSPAF—HUK ZV YHU AOPZ THU KVDU. AOLYL PZ VUL CLYF ZPUNBSHY
      AOPUN, OVDLCLY: OVD JHTL ZLSKLU, PU AOL KHYRULZZ, AV RUVD AOHA
      AOL OVBUK DHZ VU OPZ AYHPS?”

      “OL OLHYK OPT.”

      “AV OLHY H OVBUK BWVU AOL TVVY DVBSK UVA DVYR H OHYK THU SPRL
      AOPZ JVUCPJA PUAV ZBJO H WHYVEFZT VM ALYYVY AOHA OL DVBSK YPZR
      YLJHWABYL IF ZJYLHTPUN DPSKSF MVY OLSW. IF OPZ JYPLZ OL TBZA OHCL
      YBU H SVUN DHF HMALY OL RULD AOL HUPTHS DHZ VU OPZ AYHJR. OVD KPK
      OL RUVD?”

      “H NYLHALY TFZALYF AV TL PZ DOF AOPZ OVBUK, WYLZBTPUN AOHA HSS
      VBY JVUQLJABYLZ HYL JVYYLJA—”

      “P WYLZBTL UVAOPUN.”

      “DLSS, AOLU, DOF AOPZ OVBUK ZOVBSK IL SVVZL AVUPNOA. P ZBWWVZL
      AOHA PA KVLZ UVA HSDHFZ YBU SVVZL BWVU AOL TVVY. ZAHWSLAVU DVBSK
      UVA SLA PA NV BUSLZZ OL OHK YLHZVU AV AOPUR AOHA ZPY OLUYF DVBSK
      IL AOLYL.”

      “TF KPMMPJBSAF PZ AOL TVYL MVYTPKHISL VM AOL ADV, MVY P AOPUR
      AOHA DL ZOHSS CLYF ZOVYASF NLA HU LEWSHUHAPVU VM FVBYZ, DOPSL
      TPUL THF YLTHPU MVYLCLY H TFZALYF. AOL XBLZAPVU UVD PZ, DOHA
      ZOHSS DL KV DPAO AOPZ WVVY DYLAJO’Z IVKF? DL JHUUVA SLHCL PA OLYL
      AV AOL MVELZ HUK AOL YHCLUZ.”

      “P ZBNNLZA AOHA DL WBA PA PU VUL VM AOL OBAZ BUAPS DL JHU
      JVTTBUPJHAL DPAO AOL WVSPJL.”

      “LEHJASF. P OHCL UV KVBIA AOHA FVB HUK P JVBSK JHYYF PA ZV MHY.
      OHSSVH, DHAZVU, DOHA’Z AOPZ? PA’Z AOL THU OPTZLSM, IF HSS AOHA’Z
      DVUKLYMBS HUK HBKHJPVBZ! UVA H DVYK AV ZOVD FVBY ZBZWPJPVUZ—UVA H
      DVYK, VY TF WSHUZ JYBTISL AV AOL NYVBUK.”

      H MPNBYL DHZ HWWYVHJOPUN BZ VCLY AOL TVVY, HUK P ZHD AOL KBSS YLK
      NSVD VM H JPNHY. AOL TVVU ZOVUL BWVU OPT, HUK P JVBSK KPZAPUNBPZO
      AOL KHWWLY ZOHWL HUK QHBUAF DHSR VM AOL UHABYHSPZA. OL ZAVWWLK
      DOLU OL ZHD BZ, HUK AOLU JHTL VU HNHPU.

      “DOF, KY. DHAZVU, AOHA’Z UVA FVB, PZ PA? FVB HYL AOL SHZA THU
      AOHA P ZOVBSK OHCL LEWLJALK AV ZLL VBA VU AOL TVVY HA AOPZ APTL
      VM UPNOA. IBA, KLHY TL, DOHA’Z AOPZ? ZVTLIVKF OBYA? UVA—KVU’A
      ALSS TL AOHA PA PZ VBY MYPLUK ZPY OLUYF!” OL OBYYPLK WHZA TL HUK
      ZAVVWLK VCLY AOL KLHK THU. P OLHYK H ZOHYW PUAHRL VM OPZ IYLHAO
      HUK AOL JPNHY MLSS MYVT OPZ MPUNLYZ.

      “DOV—DOV’Z AOPZ?” OL ZAHTTLYLK.

      “PA PZ ZLSKLU, AOL THU DOV LZJHWLK MYVT WYPUJLAVDU.”

      ZAHWSLAVU ABYULK H NOHZASF MHJL BWVU BZ, IBA IF H ZBWYLTL LMMVYA
      OL OHK VCLYJVTL OPZ HTHGLTLUA HUK OPZ KPZHWWVPUATLUA. OL SVVRLK
      ZOHYWSF MYVT OVSTLZ AV TL. “KLHY TL! DOHA H CLYF ZOVJRPUN HMMHPY!
      OVD KPK OL KPL?”

      “OL HWWLHYZ AV OHCL IYVRLU OPZ ULJR IF MHSSPUN VCLY AOLZL YVJRZ.
      TF MYPLUK HUK P DLYL ZAYVSSPUN VU AOL TVVY DOLU DL OLHYK H JYF.”

      “P OLHYK H JYF HSZV. AOHA DHZ DOHA IYVBNOA TL VBA. P DHZ BULHZF
      HIVBA ZPY OLUYF.”

      “DOF HIVBA ZPY OLUYF PU WHYAPJBSHY?” P JVBSK UVA OLSW HZRPUN.

      “ILJHBZL P OHK ZBNNLZALK AOHA OL ZOVBSK JVTL VCLY. DOLU OL KPK
      UVA JVTL P DHZ ZBYWYPZLK, HUK P UHABYHSSF ILJHTL HSHYTLK MVY OPZ
      ZHMLAF DOLU P OLHYK JYPLZ BWVU AOL TVVY. IF AOL DHF”—OPZ LFLZ
      KHYALK HNHPU MYVT TF MHJL AV OVSTLZ’Z—“KPK FVB OLHY HUFAOPUN LSZL
      ILZPKLZ H JYF?”

      “UV,” ZHPK OVSTLZ; “KPK FVB?”

      “UV.”

      “DOHA KV FVB TLHU, AOLU?”

      “VO, FVB RUVD AOL ZAVYPLZ AOHA AOL WLHZHUAZ ALSS HIVBA H WOHUAVT
      OVBUK, HUK ZV VU. PA PZ ZHPK AV IL OLHYK HA UPNOA BWVU AOL TVVY.
      P DHZ DVUKLYPUN PM AOLYL DLYL HUF LCPKLUJL VM ZBJO H ZVBUK
      AVUPNOA.”

      “DL OLHYK UVAOPUN VM AOL RPUK,” ZHPK P.

      “HUK DOHA PZ FVBY AOLVYF VM AOPZ WVVY MLSSVD’Z KLHAO?”

      “P OHCL UV KVBIA AOHA HUEPLAF HUK LEWVZBYL OHCL KYPCLU OPT VMM
      OPZ OLHK. OL OHZ YBZOLK HIVBA AOL TVVY PU H JYHGF ZAHAL HUK
      LCLUABHSSF MHSSLU VCLY OLYL HUK IYVRLU OPZ ULJR.”

      “AOHA ZLLTZ AOL TVZA YLHZVUHISL AOLVYF,” ZHPK ZAHWSLAVU, HUK OL
      NHCL H ZPNO DOPJO P AVVR AV PUKPJHAL OPZ YLSPLM. “DOHA KV FVB
      AOPUR HIVBA PA, TY. ZOLYSVJR OVSTLZ?”

      TF MYPLUK IVDLK OPZ JVTWSPTLUAZ. “FVB HYL XBPJR HA
      PKLUAPMPJHAPVU,” ZHPK OL.

      “DL OHCL ILLU LEWLJAPUN FVB PU AOLZL WHYAZ ZPUJL KY. DHAZVU JHTL
      KVDU. FVB HYL PU APTL AV ZLL H AYHNLKF.”

      “FLZ, PUKLLK. P OHCL UV KVBIA AOHA TF MYPLUK’Z LEWSHUHAPVU DPSS
      JVCLY AOL MHJAZ. P DPSS AHRL HU BUWSLHZHUA YLTLTIYHUJL IHJR AV
      SVUKVU DPAO TL AVTVYYVD.”

      “VO, FVB YLABYU AVTVYYVD?”

      “AOHA PZ TF PUALUAPVU.”

      “P OVWL FVBY CPZPA OHZ JHZA ZVTL SPNOA BWVU AOVZL VJJBYYLUJLZ
      DOPJO OHCL WBGGSLK BZ?”

      OVSTLZ ZOYBNNLK OPZ ZOVBSKLYZ.

      “VUL JHUUVA HSDHFZ OHCL AOL ZBJJLZZ MVY DOPJO VUL OVWLZ. HU
      PUCLZAPNHAVY ULLKZ MHJAZ HUK UVA SLNLUKZ VY YBTVBYZ. PA OHZ UVA
      ILLU H ZHAPZMHJAVYF JHZL.”

      TF MYPLUK ZWVRL PU OPZ MYHURLZA HUK TVZA BUJVUJLYULK THUULY.
      ZAHWSLAVU ZAPSS SVVRLK OHYK HA OPT. AOLU OL ABYULK AV TL.

      “P DVBSK ZBNNLZA JHYYFPUN AOPZ WVVY MLSSVD AV TF OVBZL, IBA PA
      DVBSK NPCL TF ZPZALY ZBJO H MYPNOA AOHA P KV UVA MLLS QBZAPMPLK
      PU KVPUN PA. P AOPUR AOHA PM DL WBA ZVTLAOPUN VCLY OPZ MHJL OL
      DPSS IL ZHML BUAPS TVYUPUN.”

      HUK ZV PA DHZ HYYHUNLK. YLZPZAPUN ZAHWSLAVU’Z VMMLY VM
      OVZWPAHSPAF, OVSTLZ HUK P ZLA VMM AV IHZRLYCPSSL OHSS, SLHCPUN
      AOL UHABYHSPZA AV YLABYU HSVUL. SVVRPUN IHJR DL ZHD AOL MPNBYL
      TVCPUN ZSVDSF HDHF VCLY AOL IYVHK TVVY, HUK ILOPUK OPT AOHA VUL
      ISHJR ZTBKNL VU AOL ZPSCLYLK ZSVWL DOPJO ZOVDLK DOLYL AOL THU DHZ
      SFPUN DOV OHK JVTL ZV OVYYPISF AV OPZ LUK.

      “DL’YL HA JSVZL NYPWZ HA SHZA,” ZHPK OVSTLZ HZ DL DHSRLK AVNLAOLY
      HJYVZZ AOL TVVY. “DOHA H ULYCL AOL MLSSVD OHZ! OVD OL WBSSLK
      OPTZLSM AVNLAOLY PU AOL MHJL VM DOHA TBZA OHCL ILLU H WHYHSFGPUN
      ZOVJR DOLU OL MVBUK AOHA AOL DYVUN THU OHK MHSSLU H CPJAPT AV OPZ
      WSVA. P AVSK FVB PU SVUKVU, DHAZVU, HUK P ALSS FVB UVD HNHPU,
      AOHA DL OHCL ULCLY OHK H MVLTHU TVYL DVYAOF VM VBY ZALLS.”

      “P HT ZVYYF AOHA OL OHZ ZLLU FVB.”

      “HUK ZV DHZ P HA MPYZA. IBA AOLYL DHZ UV NLAAPUN VBA VM PA.”

      “DOHA LMMLJA KV FVB AOPUR PA DPSS OHCL BWVU OPZ WSHUZ UVD AOHA OL
      RUVDZ FVB HYL OLYL?”

      “PA THF JHBZL OPT AV IL TVYL JHBAPVBZ, VY PA THF KYPCL OPT AV
      KLZWLYHAL TLHZBYLZ HA VUJL. SPRL TVZA JSLCLY JYPTPUHSZ, OL THF IL
      AVV JVUMPKLUA PU OPZ VDU JSLCLYULZZ HUK PTHNPUL AOHA OL OHZ
      JVTWSLALSF KLJLPCLK BZ.”

      “DOF ZOVBSK DL UVA HYYLZA OPT HA VUJL?”

      “TF KLHY DHAZVU, FVB DLYL IVYU AV IL H THU VM HJAPVU. FVBY
      PUZAPUJA PZ HSDHFZ AV KV ZVTLAOPUN LULYNLAPJ. IBA ZBWWVZPUN, MVY
      HYNBTLUA’Z ZHRL, AOHA DL OHK OPT HYYLZALK AVUPNOA, DOHA VU LHYAO
      AOL ILAALY VMM ZOVBSK DL IL MVY AOHA? DL JVBSK WYVCL UVAOPUN
      HNHPUZA OPT. AOLYL’Z AOL KLCPSPZO JBUUPUN VM PA! PM OL DLYL
      HJAPUN AOYVBNO H OBTHU HNLUA DL JVBSK NLA ZVTL LCPKLUJL, IBA PM
      DL DLYL AV KYHN AOPZ NYLHA KVN AV AOL SPNOA VM KHF PA DVBSK UVA
      OLSW BZ PU WBAAPUN H YVWL YVBUK AOL ULJR VM PAZ THZALY.”

      “ZBYLSF DL OHCL H JHZL.”

      “UVA H ZOHKVD VM VUL—VUSF ZBYTPZL HUK JVUQLJABYL. DL ZOVBSK IL
      SHBNOLK VBA VM JVBYA PM DL JHTL DPAO ZBJO H ZAVYF HUK ZBJO
      LCPKLUJL.”

      “AOLYL PZ ZPY JOHYSLZ’Z KLHAO.”

      “MVBUK KLHK DPAOVBA H THYR BWVU OPT. FVB HUK P RUVD AOHA OL KPLK
      VM ZOLLY MYPNOA, HUK DL RUVD HSZV DOHA MYPNOALULK OPT, IBA OVD
      HYL DL AV NLA ADLSCL ZAVSPK QBYFTLU AV RUVD PA? DOHA ZPNUZ HYL
      AOLYL VM H OVBUK? DOLYL HYL AOL THYRZ VM PAZ MHUNZ? VM JVBYZL DL
      RUVD AOHA H OVBUK KVLZ UVA IPAL H KLHK IVKF HUK AOHA ZPY JOHYSLZ
      DHZ KLHK ILMVYL LCLY AOL IYBAL VCLYAVVR OPT. IBA DL OHCL AV WYVCL
      HSS AOPZ, HUK DL HYL UVA PU H WVZPAPVU AV KV PA.”

      “DLSS, AOLU, AVUPNOA?”

      “DL HYL UVA TBJO ILAALY VMM AVUPNOA. HNHPU, AOLYL DHZ UV KPYLJA
      JVUULJAPVU ILADLLU AOL OVBUK HUK AOL THU’Z KLHAO. DL ULCLY ZHD
      AOL OVBUK. DL OLHYK PA, IBA DL JVBSK UVA WYVCL AOHA PA DHZ
      YBUUPUN BWVU AOPZ THU’Z AYHPS. AOLYL PZ H JVTWSLAL HIZLUJL VM
      TVAPCL. UV, TF KLHY MLSSVD; DL TBZA YLJVUJPSL VBYZLSCLZ AV AOL
      MHJA AOHA DL OHCL UV JHZL HA WYLZLUA, HUK AOHA PA PZ DVYAO VBY
      DOPSL AV YBU HUF YPZR PU VYKLY AV LZAHISPZO VUL.”

      “HUK OVD KV FVB WYVWVZL AV KV ZV?”

      “P OHCL NYLHA OVWLZ VM DOHA TYZ. SHBYH SFVUZ THF KV MVY BZ DOLU
      AOL WVZPAPVU VM HMMHPYZ PZ THKL JSLHY AV OLY. HUK P OHCL TF VDU
      WSHU HZ DLSS. ZBMMPJPLUA MVY AVTVYYVD PZ AOL LCPS AOLYLVM; IBA P
      OVWL ILMVYL AOL KHF PZ WHZA AV OHCL AOL BWWLY OHUK HA SHZA.”

      P JVBSK KYHD UVAOPUN MBYAOLY MYVT OPT, HUK OL DHSRLK, SVZA PU
      AOVBNOA, HZ MHY HZ AOL IHZRLYCPSSL NHALZ.

      “HYL FVB JVTPUN BW?”

      “FLZ; P ZLL UV YLHZVU MVY MBYAOLY JVUJLHSTLUA. IBA VUL SHZA DVYK,
      DHAZVU. ZHF UVAOPUN VM AOL OVBUK AV ZPY OLUYF. SLA OPT AOPUR AOHA
      ZLSKLU’Z KLHAO DHZ HZ ZAHWSLAVU DVBSK OHCL BZ ILSPLCL. OL DPSS
      OHCL H ILAALY ULYCL MVY AOL VYKLHS DOPJO OL DPSS OHCL AV BUKLYNV
      AVTVYYVD, DOLU OL PZ LUNHNLK, PM P YLTLTILY FVBY YLWVYA HYPNOA,
      AV KPUL DPAO AOLZL WLVWSL.”

      “HUK ZV HT P.”

      “AOLU FVB TBZA LEJBZL FVBYZLSM HUK OL TBZA NV HSVUL. AOHA DPSS IL
      LHZPSF HYYHUNLK. HUK UVD, PM DL HYL AVV SHAL MVY KPUULY, P AOPUR
      AOHA DL HYL IVAO YLHKF MVY VBY ZBWWLYZ.”

JOHWALY 13.
MPEPUN AOL ULAZ


      ZPY OLUYF DHZ TVYL WSLHZLK AOHU ZBYWYPZLK AV ZLL ZOLYSVJR OVSTLZ,
      MVY OL OHK MVY ZVTL KHFZ ILLU LEWLJAPUN AOHA YLJLUA LCLUAZ DVBSK
      IYPUN OPT KVDU MYVT SVUKVU. OL KPK YHPZL OPZ LFLIYVDZ, OVDLCLY,
      DOLU OL MVBUK AOHA TF MYPLUK OHK ULPAOLY HUF SBNNHNL UVY HUF
      LEWSHUHAPVUZ MVY PAZ HIZLUJL. ILADLLU BZ DL ZVVU ZBWWSPLK OPZ
      DHUAZ, HUK AOLU VCLY H ILSHALK ZBWWLY DL LEWSHPULK AV AOL IHYVULA
      HZ TBJO VM VBY LEWLYPLUJL HZ PA ZLLTLK KLZPYHISL AOHA OL ZOVBSK
      RUVD. IBA MPYZA P OHK AOL BUWSLHZHUA KBAF VM IYLHRPUN AOL ULDZ AV
      IHYYFTVYL HUK OPZ DPML. AV OPT PA THF OHCL ILLU HU BUTPAPNHALK
      YLSPLM, IBA ZOL DLWA IPAALYSF PU OLY HWYVU. AV HSS AOL DVYSK OL
      DHZ AOL THU VM CPVSLUJL, OHSM HUPTHS HUK OHSM KLTVU; IBA AV OLY
      OL HSDHFZ YLTHPULK AOL SPAASL DPSMBS IVF VM OLY VDU NPYSOVVK, AOL
      JOPSK DOV OHK JSBUN AV OLY OHUK. LCPS PUKLLK PZ AOL THU DOV OHZ
      UVA VUL DVTHU AV TVBYU OPT.

      “P’CL ILLU TVWPUN PU AOL OVBZL HSS KHF ZPUJL DHAZVU DLUA VMM PU
      AOL TVYUPUN,” ZHPK AOL IHYVULA. “P NBLZZ P ZOVBSK OHCL ZVTL
      JYLKPA, MVY P OHCL RLWA TF WYVTPZL. PM P OHKU’A ZDVYU UVA AV NV
      HIVBA HSVUL P TPNOA OHCL OHK H TVYL SPCLSF LCLUPUN, MVY P OHK H
      TLZZHNL MYVT ZAHWSLAVU HZRPUN TL VCLY AOLYL.”

      “P OHCL UV KVBIA AOHA FVB DVBSK OHCL OHK H TVYL SPCLSF LCLUPUN,”
      ZHPK OVSTLZ KYPSF. “IF AOL DHF, P KVU’A ZBWWVZL FVB HWWYLJPHAL
      AOHA DL OHCL ILLU TVBYUPUN VCLY FVB HZ OHCPUN IYVRLU FVBY ULJR?”

      ZPY OLUYF VWLULK OPZ LFLZ. “OVD DHZ AOHA?”

      “AOPZ WVVY DYLAJO DHZ KYLZZLK PU FVBY JSVAOLZ. P MLHY FVBY
      ZLYCHUA DOV NHCL AOLT AV OPT THF NLA PUAV AYVBISL DPAO AOL
      WVSPJL.”

      “AOHA PZ BUSPRLSF. AOLYL DHZ UV THYR VU HUF VM AOLT, HZ MHY HZ P
      RUVD.”

      “AOHA’Z SBJRF MVY OPT—PU MHJA, PA’Z SBJRF MVY HSS VM FVB, ZPUJL
      FVB HYL HSS VU AOL DYVUN ZPKL VM AOL SHD PU AOPZ THAALY. P HT UVA
      ZBYL AOHA HZ H JVUZJPLUAPVBZ KLALJAPCL TF MPYZA KBAF PZ UVA AV
      HYYLZA AOL DOVSL OVBZLOVSK. DHAZVU’Z YLWVYAZ HYL TVZA
      PUJYPTPUHAPUN KVJBTLUAZ.”

      “IBA OVD HIVBA AOL JHZL?” HZRLK AOL IHYVULA. “OHCL FVB THKL
      HUFAOPUN VBA VM AOL AHUNSL? P KVU’A RUVD AOHA DHAZVU HUK P HYL
      TBJO AOL DPZLY ZPUJL DL JHTL KVDU.”

      “P AOPUR AOHA P ZOHSS IL PU H WVZPAPVU AV THRL AOL ZPABHAPVU
      YHAOLY TVYL JSLHY AV FVB ILMVYL SVUN. PA OHZ ILLU HU LEJLLKPUNSF
      KPMMPJBSA HUK TVZA JVTWSPJHALK IBZPULZZ. AOLYL HYL ZLCLYHS WVPUAZ
      BWVU DOPJO DL ZAPSS DHUA SPNOA—IBA PA PZ JVTPUN HSS AOL ZHTL.”

      “DL’CL OHK VUL LEWLYPLUJL, HZ DHAZVU OHZ UV KVBIA AVSK FVB. DL
      OLHYK AOL OVBUK VU AOL TVVY, ZV P JHU ZDLHY AOHA PA PZ UVA HSS
      LTWAF ZBWLYZAPAPVU. P OHK ZVTLAOPUN AV KV DPAO KVNZ DOLU P DHZ
      VBA DLZA, HUK P RUVD VUL DOLU P OLHY VUL. PM FVB JHU TBGGSL AOHA
      VUL HUK WBA OPT VU H JOHPU P’SS IL YLHKF AV ZDLHY FVB HYL AOL
      NYLHALZA KLALJAPCL VM HSS APTL.”

      “P AOPUR P DPSS TBGGSL OPT HUK JOHPU OPT HSS YPNOA PM FVB DPSS
      NPCL TL FVBY OLSW.”

      “DOHALCLY FVB ALSS TL AV KV P DPSS KV.”

      “CLYF NVVK; HUK P DPSS HZR FVB HSZV AV KV PA ISPUKSF, DPAOVBA
      HSDHFZ HZRPUN AOL YLHZVU.”

      “QBZA HZ FVB SPRL.”

      “PM FVB DPSS KV AOPZ P AOPUR AOL JOHUJLZ HYL AOHA VBY SPAASL
      WYVISLT DPSS ZVVU IL ZVSCLK. P OHCL UV KVBIA—”

      OL ZAVWWLK ZBKKLUSF HUK ZAHYLK MPELKSF BW VCLY TF OLHK PUAV AOL
      HPY. AOL SHTW ILHA BWVU OPZ MHJL, HUK ZV PUALUA DHZ PA HUK ZV
      ZAPSS AOHA PA TPNOA OHCL ILLU AOHA VM H JSLHY-JBA JSHZZPJHS
      ZAHABL, H WLYZVUPMPJHAPVU VM HSLYAULZZ HUK LEWLJAHAPVU.

      “DOHA PZ PA?” DL IVAO JYPLK.

      P JVBSK ZLL HZ OL SVVRLK KVDU AOHA OL DHZ YLWYLZZPUN ZVTL
      PUALYUHS LTVAPVU. OPZ MLHABYLZ DLYL ZAPSS JVTWVZLK, IBA OPZ LFLZ
      ZOVUL DPAO HTBZLK LEBSAHAPVU.

      “LEJBZL AOL HKTPYHAPVU VM H JVUUVPZZLBY,” ZHPK OL HZ OL DHCLK OPZ
      OHUK AVDHYKZ AOL SPUL VM WVYAYHPAZ DOPJO JVCLYLK AOL VWWVZPAL
      DHSS. “DHAZVU DVU’A HSSVD AOHA P RUVD HUFAOPUN VM HYA IBA AOHA PZ
      TLYL QLHSVBZF ILJHBZL VBY CPLDZ BWVU AOL ZBIQLJA KPMMLY. UVD,
      AOLZL HYL H YLHSSF CLYF MPUL ZLYPLZ VM WVYAYHPAZ.”

      “DLSS, P’T NSHK AV OLHY FVB ZHF ZV,” ZHPK ZPY OLUYF, NSHUJPUN
      DPAO ZVTL ZBYWYPZL HA TF MYPLUK. “P KVU’A WYLALUK AV RUVD TBJO
      HIVBA AOLZL AOPUNZ, HUK P’K IL H ILAALY QBKNL VM H OVYZL VY H
      ZALLY AOHU VM H WPJABYL. P KPKU’A RUVD AOHA FVB MVBUK APTL MVY
      ZBJO AOPUNZ.”

      “P RUVD DOHA PZ NVVK DOLU P ZLL PA, HUK P ZLL PA UVD. AOHA’Z H
      RULSSLY, P’SS ZDLHY, AOHA SHKF PU AOL ISBL ZPSR VCLY FVUKLY, HUK
      AOL ZAVBA NLUASLTHU DPAO AOL DPN VBNOA AV IL H YLFUVSKZ. AOLF HYL
      HSS MHTPSF WVYAYHPAZ, P WYLZBTL?”

      “LCLYF VUL.”

      “KV FVB RUVD AOL UHTLZ?”

      “IHYYFTVYL OHZ ILLU JVHJOPUN TL PU AOLT, HUK P AOPUR P JHU ZHF TF
      SLZZVUZ MHPYSF DLSS.”

      “DOV PZ AOL NLUASLTHU DPAO AOL ALSLZJVWL?”

      “AOHA PZ YLHY-HKTPYHS IHZRLYCPSSL, DOV ZLYCLK BUKLY YVKULF PU AOL
      DLZA PUKPLZ. AOL THU DPAO AOL ISBL JVHA HUK AOL YVSS VM WHWLY PZ
      ZPY DPSSPHT IHZRLYCPSSL, DOV DHZ JOHPYTHU VM JVTTPAALLZ VM AOL
      OVBZL VM JVTTVUZ BUKLY WPAA.”

      “HUK AOPZ JHCHSPLY VWWVZPAL AV TL—AOL VUL DPAO AOL ISHJR CLSCLA
      HUK AOL SHJL?”

      “HO, FVB OHCL H YPNOA AV RUVD HIVBA OPT. AOHA PZ AOL JHBZL VM HSS
      AOL TPZJOPLM, AOL DPJRLK OBNV, DOV ZAHYALK AOL OVBUK VM AOL
      IHZRLYCPSSLZ. DL’YL UVA SPRLSF AV MVYNLA OPT.”

      P NHGLK DPAO PUALYLZA HUK ZVTL ZBYWYPZL BWVU AOL WVYAYHPA.

      “KLHY TL!” ZHPK OVSTLZ, “OL ZLLTZ H XBPLA, TLLR-THUULYLK THU
      LUVBNO, IBA P KHYL ZHF AOHA AOLYL DHZ H SBYRPUN KLCPS PU OPZ
      LFLZ. P OHK WPJABYLK OPT HZ H TVYL YVIBZA HUK YBMMPHUSF WLYZVU.”

      “AOLYL’Z UV KVBIA HIVBA AOL HBAOLUAPJPAF, MVY AOL UHTL HUK AOL
      KHAL, 1647, HYL VU AOL IHJR VM AOL JHUCHZ.”

JOHWALY 14.
AOL OVBUK VM AOL IHZRLYCPSSLZ


      VUL VM ZOLYSVJR OVSTLZ’Z KLMLJAZ—PM, PUKLLK, VUL THF JHSS PA H
      KLMLJA—DHZ AOHA OL DHZ LEJLLKPUNSF SVHAO AV JVTTBUPJHAL OPZ MBSS
      WSHUZ AV HUF VAOLY WLYZVU BUAPS AOL PUZAHUA VM AOLPY MBSMPSTLUA.
      WHYASF PA JHTL UV KVBIA MYVT OPZ VDU THZALYMBS UHABYL, DOPJO
      SVCLK AV KVTPUHAL HUK ZBYWYPZL AOVZL DOV DLYL HYVBUK OPT. WHYASF
      HSZV MYVT OPZ WYVMLZZPVUHS JHBAPVU, DOPJO BYNLK OPT ULCLY AV AHRL
      HUF JOHUJLZ. AOL YLZBSA, OVDLCLY, DHZ CLYF AYFPUN MVY AOVZL DOV

      ZBKKLUSF HNHPUZA OPT. ZOL OHK SLHYULK ZVTLAOPUN VM AOL KLHAO VM

      VBAOVBZL VU AOL LCLUPUN AOHA ZPY OLUYF DHZ JVTPUN AV KPUULY. ZOL
      AHELK OLY OBZIHUK DPAO OPZ PUALUKLK JYPTL, HUK H MBYPVBZ ZJLUL
      MVSSVDLK PU DOPJO OL ZOVDLK OLY MVY AOL MPYZA APTL AOHA ZOL OHK H
      YPCHS PU OPZ SVCL. OLY MPKLSPAF ABYULK PU HU PUZAHUA AV IPAALY
      OHAYLK, HUK OL ZHD AOHA ZOL DVBSK ILAYHF OPT. OL APLK OLY BW,
      AOLYLMVYL, AOHA ZOL TPNOA OHCL UV JOHUJL VM DHYUPUN ZPY OLUYF,
      HUK OL OVWLK, UV KVBIA, AOHA DOLU AOL DOVSL JVBUAYFZPKL WBA KVDU
      AOL IHYVULA’Z KLHAO AV AOL JBYZL VM OPZ MHTPSF, HZ AOLF JLYAHPUSF
      DVBSK KV, OL JVBSK DPU OPZ DPML IHJR AV HJJLWA HU HJJVTWSPZOLK
      MHJA HUK AV RLLW ZPSLUA BWVU DOHA ZOL RULD. PU AOPZ P MHUJF AOHA
      PU HUF JHZL OL THKL H TPZJHSJBSHAPVU, HUK AOHA, PM DL OHK UVA
      ILLU AOLYL, OPZ KVVT DVBSK UVUL AOL SLZZ OHCL ILLU ZLHSLK. H
      DVTHU VM ZWHUPZO ISVVK KVLZ UVA JVUKVUL ZBJO HU PUQBYF ZV
      SPNOASF. HUK UVD, TF KLHY DHAZVU, DPAOVBA YLMLYYPUN AV TF UVALZ,
      P JHUUVA NPCL FVB H TVYL KLAHPSLK HJJVBUA VM AOPZ JBYPVBZ JHZL. P
      KV UVA RUVD AOHA HUFAOPUN LZZLUAPHS OHZ ILLU SLMA BULEWSHPULK.”

      “OL JVBSK UVA OVWL AV MYPNOALU ZPY OLUYF AV KLHAO HZ OL OHK KVUL
      AOL VSK BUJSL DPAO OPZ IVNPL OVBUK.”

      “AOL ILHZA DHZ ZHCHNL HUK OHSM-ZAHYCLK. PM PAZ HWWLHYHUJL KPK UVA
      MYPNOALU PAZ CPJAPT AV KLHAO, HA SLHZA PA DVBSK WHYHSFGL AOL
      YLZPZAHUJL DOPJO TPNOA IL VMMLYLK.”

      “UV KVBIA. AOLYL VUSF YLTHPUZ VUL KPMMPJBSAF. PM ZAHWSLAVU JHTL
      PUAV AOL ZBJJLZZPVU, OVD JVBSK OL LEWSHPU AOL MHJA AOHA OL, AOL

      “PA PZ H MVYTPKHISL KPMMPJBSAF, HUK P MLHY AOHA FVB HZR AVV TBJO
